# astro-ph.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [The Amplitude-Growth Degeneracy and Implied $A_s$ Diagnostic for Background-Inert Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13914)
*Ameya Kolhatkar,P. K. Sahoo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明在共线 $f(Q)$ 引力中，背景惯性微扰耦合参数 $\lambda$ 与团簇振幅参数 $\sigma_{80}$ 存在简并（degeneracy），这一简归根源于原初振幅 $A_s$ 与当前增长因子 $D_0(\lambda)$ 之间的更深层简并。通过引入 Planck 的 $\ln(A_s)$ 先验可以修复 $\sigma_{80}$ 的人工膨胀，但 $A_s$ 与 Planck 值之间存在 $1.7\sigma-2.2\sigma$ 的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验 $f(Q)$ 引力框架中背景惯性微扰耦合参数与宇宙学观测之间的简并关系，并评估其是否会导致对宇宙学参数的错误估计。

Method: 利用压缩 CMB 距离先验（compressed CMB distance priors）分析 $f(Q)$ 引力中的耦合参数；提出一种一致性检验方案，通过计算重现采样器预测的 $\sigma_{80}$ 所需 $A_s$ 来诊断简并；使用两套基于耦合/解耦 $f\sigma_8(z)$ 数据的管道；模型涵盖 $\Lambda$CDM 和 $f(Q)$ 框架下的混合模型（Hybrid model）。

Result: 加入 $\lambda_0\sqrt{QQ_0}$ 修正项后，$\sigma_{80}$ 被膨胀至非物理值，$A_s$ 增加 $20\%-30\%$，与 Planck 值呈 $1.7\sigma-2.2\sigma$ 的张力；引入 $\ln(A_s)$ 先验后所有约束参数恢复基线值；每个额外参数带来约 2 单位的惩罚；$\Lambda$CDM$+\lambda_0+\ln(A_s)$ + SDSS DR16 组合对 vanilla $\Lambda$CDM 有微弱偏好。

Conclusion: $f(Q)$ 引力中的参数简并可能显著影响对 $\sigma_{80}$ 和 $A_s$ 的推断，但通过引入 Planck 先验可以缓解这一问题；所提出的一致性检验方案可推广至 $f(Q)$ 类以外的模型。

Abstract: We prove that any background-inert perturbative coupling $ λ$ in coincident $ f(Q) $ gravity exhibits a degeneracy with the clustering amplitude $ σ_{80} $, when using compressed CMB distance priors. This degeneracy is, in fact, a direct materialization of a more deeper $ A_s-D_0(λ) $ degeneracy between the primordial amplitude $ A_s $ and the present day growth factor $ D_0(λ) $. We outline a consistency check scheme, applicable to models even outside the $ f(Q) $ class, by computing $ A_s $ needed to reproduce the $ σ_{80} $ predicted by the sampler. We perform our analysis with two dataset pipelines, based on the coupled/decoupled $ fσ_8(z) $ data. To ensure theoretical diversity, we include $ Λ$CDM and the Hybrid model in the $ f(Q) $ framework. Our results illustrate that adding the $ λ_0\sqrt{QQ_0} $ correction to the models inflates $ σ_{80} $ to unphysical values, while showing moderate evidence in favor of the said models. However, this results in an increase of $ 20\%-30\% $ in $ A_s $ in $ 1.7σ-2.2σ$ tension with Planck values. We utilize the $ 1σ$ $ \ln(A_s) $ constraints from Planck as priors in order to fix the artificial increase in $ σ_{80} $ and find that all the constrained parameters return to their baseline values. Each model is penalized by around $ 2 $ units per extra parameter. Interestingly, the $ Λ$CDM$ +λ_0+\ln(A_s) $ + SDSS DR16 combination shows a weak preference over the vanilla $ Λ$CDM model, validated by the values of $ \log\mathcal{Z},\;AIC,\;DIC, $ and BIC.

</details>


### [2] [Isocurvature-Free QCD Axion Dark Matter from Inflaton-Driven Early QCD: the Necessity of Inflationary Plateaus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15192)
*Katherine Freese,Evangelos I. Sfakianakis,Barmak Shams Es Haghi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过暴胀子（inflaton）与标准模型胶子（gluons）的直接耦合来动态改变QCD禁闭标度（confinement scale）的机制，使轴子（axion）暂时变重以抑制等曲率扰动，并在暴胀结束后恢复轻质量状态，通过德西特（de Sitter）涨落产生暗物质丰度。通过参数化背景演化ε(N) ∝ 1/N^p，论文解析地证明了该机制天然选择缓坡（plateau-like）暴胀模型（p≥2），排斥单项式（monomial）模型（p=1），并通过同一耦合实现再加热（reheating），同时将标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）推向更蓝的值，为原本被宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据排除的模型开辟可行参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决轴子暗物质产生过程中等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）过大的问题，同时避免对暴胀势（inflationary potential）作出特定假设，探索一类通用的暴胀背景参数化如何约束该机制的可行性。

Method: 通过引入暴胀子与标准模型胶子的直接耦合，使QCD禁闭标度在暴胀期间动态增大，轴子因此变重并抑制其等曲率扰动。暴胀背景由参数ε(N) ∝ 1/N^p描述，其中N为暴胀结束前的e-折叠（e-folds）数，单参数p区分不同暴胀模型类别（p=1对应单项式模型，p=2对应标准缓坡模型，p≥3对应超平坦缓坡或山顶（hilltop）模型）。分析采用解析方法而非指定具体暴胀势。

Result: 解析结果表明该机制仅对缓坡类模型（p≥2）可行：单项式模型（p=1）会导致禁闭标度增长过快，使得QCD扇区失去微扰可控性（perturbative control）；而缓坡模型能保持QCD扇区可控。在最小场景下，通过同一暴胀子-胶子耦合实现再加热，并仅在退禁闭（deconfinement）发生于CMB窗口之后时才能获得可行的轴子暗物质产生。此外，早期禁闭扇区会将标量谱指数推向更大、更蓝的值，从而为原本被CMB数据排除的模型打开可行参数空间。

Conclusion: 该暴胀子-胶子耦合机制天然选择缓坡或超平坦缓坡类暴胀模型（p≥2），并提出一种无需额外耦合或精细调节的轴子暗物质产生路径，同时通过改变标量谱指数为暴胀模型提供新的CMB可检验性判据。

Abstract: A direct coupling between the inflaton and Standard Model gluons can dynamically raise the QCD confinement scale during inflation, making the axion temporarily heavy and suppressing axion isocurvature perturbations. As inflation proceeds, the confinement scale relaxes, the axion becomes light, and late-time de Sitter fluctuations can generate the observed dark matter abundance. We analyze this mechanism without specifying an inflationary potential, instead parametrizing the background by $ε(N) \propto 1/N^p$, where $N$ is the number of $e$-folds before the end of inflation. The single parameter $p$ distinguishes monomial models ($p=1$), standard plateau models ($p=2$), and ultra-flat plateau or hilltop-like models ($p\ge 3$). We (analytically) show that the mechanism selects plateau-like ($p\ge 2$) inflation: monomial models generically cause the confinement scale to grow too rapidly, while plateau models keep the QCD sector under perturbative control. In the minimal scenario, reheating occurs through the same inflaton-gluon coupling, and viable axion dark matter production is obtained when deconfinement occurs after the CMB window. The early-confinement sector also shifts the scalar spectral index to larger, bluer values, opening viable parameter space for models otherwise disfavored by CMB data.

</details>

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Integral representation of time-harmonic solutions to Maxwell's equations with fast numerical convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14183)
*Kalpesh Jaykar,Richard D. James*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文构建了一类无源区域中麦克斯韦方程组（Maxwell's equations）时间谐波解的积分表示，该表示包含可赋值的广义函数以适配特定边界或远场条件。在周期性与光滑性条件下，这些解可通过多维梯形法则（trapezoidal rules）以指数收敛速度近似，物理上对应有限平面波源对时间谐波解的逼近。该框架适用于二十面体对称（icosahedral symmetry）结构的相干辐射配置，并推广至亥姆霍兹型方程（Helmholtz-type equations）描述的多种物理现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有X射线衍射（XRD）方法已被推广至扭曲X射线下的螺旋原子结构研究，本文在此基础上进一步发展广义积分表示方法，旨在解决更广泛的时间谐波电磁场解的表达与近似问题，并探索其在具有二十面体对称性结构中的相干辐射应用。

Method: 基于已有文献中的积分形式，构建了真空或均匀无源介质中麦克斯韦方程组时间谐波解的积分表示，引入可赋值的广义函数以满足边界或远场条件。利用多维梯形法则实现指数收敛的数值近似，物理上解释为有限平面波源对解的逼近。

Result: 满足周期性与光滑性条件的解可通过多维梯形法则以指数收敛速度近似；有限平面波源逼近可在二十面体对称结构处实现相干干涉；该表示满足无源区域内任意多个指定位置上的狄利克雷条件（Dirichlet conditions），并扩展至声波与弹性波等亥姆霍兹型方程。

Conclusion: 所构建的积分表示为一大类时间谐波麦克斯韦方程组解提供了统一的表示与近似框架，物理上可利用有限平面波源实现，且适用于二十面体对称结构的辐射问题。该方法同时适用于其他亥姆霍兹型波动现象，具有较广的物理适用性。

Abstract: The robustness of XRD methods for the determination of the lattice parameters of crystals is well established. These methods have been extended to helical atomic structures using twisted x-rays \cite{friesecke_twisted_2016}. Building on an integral form
  used in \cite{friesecke_twisted_2016}, we construct integral representations of a broad class of time-harmonic solutions to Maxwell's equations in a vacuum or, more generally, in a homogeneous medium without source terms. The representation includes assignable generalized functions (distributions) that can be tailored to specific boundary or far-field conditions. When the assignable functions satisfy mild periodicity and smoothness conditions, the solutions can be approximated using multi-dimensional trapezoidal rules with exponentially fast convergence. This approximation can be physically interpreted as utilizing finite sources of plane waves to approximate the broad class of time-harmonic solutions to Maxwell's equations. Using these solutions, we show that radiation from suitably placed and oriented sources can serve as incoming radiation for structures with icosahedral symmetry to achieve constructive interference after interacting with the icosahedral structure. The finite source approximations are sufficiently general to satisfy the general Dirichlet conditions at an arbitrarily large number of assigned locations in a source-free domain. The integral representation also extends to a broad class of physical phenomena governed by Helmholtz-type equations. Examples include the scalar wave equation for acoustic waves and elastic wave propagation in linear isotropic solids, which involve both scalar and vector wave equations.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.soft'></div>

# cond-mat.soft [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Interference of dynamical arrest, thermodynamic instabilities and energy-scale competition in symmetric binary mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14064)
*Ricardo Peredo-Ortiz,Edilio Lázaro-Lázaro,Magdaleno Medina-Noyola,Luis Fernando Elizondo-Aguilera*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文扩展了二元混合物在热力学不稳定区域内的描述和分类，揭示了非平衡动力学阻滞（dynamical arrest）如何通过两种不稳定性与阻滞的相互作用产生不同机制驱动的非晶态，并引入结构序参量χ实现统一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统相图分类（Types I-IV）基于能量竞争，能够描述二元混合物的平衡行为，但在软物质混合物中，强竞争相互作用和动力学势垒常常导致动力学阻滞，破坏平衡态和亚稳态的形成，使传统相图描述不完整。因此需要一种能够涵盖非平衡阻滞态的扩展描述框架。

Method: 将二元混合物的描述和分类扩展到热力学不稳定区域内部，具体分析两种不稳定性（相分离不稳定性与凝聚不稳定性）与动力学阻滞之间的相互作用如何产生多种机制驱动的非晶态（amorphous states）。通过引入结构序参量χ来描述不同阻滞态之间的交叉区域。

Result: 在强交叉吸引（strong cross-attraction）下，动力学阻滞抑制了相分离（demixing）；而在竞争性区域中，混合物可能表现出凝聚驱动（condensation-driven）或相分离诱导（demixing-induced）的阻滞态。这些状态之间的交叉可以通过结构序参量χ统一描述。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个统一的非平衡描述框架，能够将理论预测与实验观察到的阻滞态进行协调，弥补了传统平衡相图在软物质混合物研究中的不足。

Abstract: The equilibrium behavior of binary mixtures can be understood through the competition of energy scales, which classifies their corresponding phase diagrams into distinct topological regimes (Types I-IV). However, in many soft-matter mixtures, strong competing interactions and kinetic barriers often promote dynamical arrest, disrupting the formation of equilibrium and metastable states, and thus rendering conventional phase diagrams incomplete. Here we extend the description and classification of binary systems inside regions of thermodynamical instability. Specifically, we discuss how the interplay between two kind of instabilities and kinetic arrest generates a variety of amorphous states driven by different underlying mechanisms. For strong cross-attraction, for example, dynamical arrest suppresses demixing, whereas in competitive regimes, a mixture may display either condensation-driven or demixing-induced arrested states. The crossover between these regimes can be described by a structural order parameter $χ$, providing a unified non-equilibrium description that reconciles theoretical predictions with experimentally observed arrested states.

</details>

# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Nonlinear Multiphysics Modeling of Batch Digester Discharge Dynamics with Rheology-Driven Hydraulic Transport and Drainability Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14155)
*José M. Campos-Salazar*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 针对间歇式蒸煮器（batch digester）排放过程中因浆料浓度演化与流变不确定性导致的强非线性水力传输动力学问题，本文提出了一种非线性动态模型与鲁棒滑模控制（Sliding Mode Control, SMC）策略，用于工业间歇式蒸煮器系统的排放流量调节。该框架整合了非牛顿流体流变学、浓度依赖的水力阻力、排水能力效应、沟流现象及非线性水力传输行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 间歇式蒸煮器的排放操作（blowdown operations）中存在高度非线性的水力传输动力学（nonlinear hydraulic transport dynamics），其根源在于浆料一致性（slurry consistency）的时变演化与流变参数的不确定性（rheological uncertainty），传统控制方法难以有效应对。

Method: 建立了一个非线性动态模型（nonlinear dynamic model），该模型将非牛顿流体流变学（non-Newtonian slurry rheology）、浓度依赖的水力阻力（consistency-dependent hydraulic resistance）、排水能力效应（drainability effects）、沟流现象（channeling phenomena）以及非线性水力传输行为纳入统一框架；在此基础上，设计了鲁棒滑模控制（Sliding Mode Control, SMC）策略以实现排放流量的调节。

Result: 摘要中未提供具体的数值或仿真结果。

Conclusion: 所提出的非线性动态模型与滑模控制策略能够有效应对间歇式蒸煮器排放过程中由浆料浓度演变与流变不确定性引起的非线性水力传输动力学问题，为实现工业蒸煮器系统的稳定排放流量调节提供了理论依据和控制框架。

Abstract: Batch digester blowdown operations exhibit highly nonlinear hydraulic transport dynamics due to evolving slurry consistency and rheological uncertainty. This work presents a nonlinear dynamic model and a robust Sliding Mode Control (SMC) strategy for discharge-flow regulation in industrial batch digester systems. The proposed framework incorporates non-Newtonian slurry rheology, consistency-dependent hydraulic resistance, drainability effects, channeling phenomena, and nonlinear hydraulic transport behavior.

</details>


### [6] [Weakly nonlinear analysis of Hopf bifurcations in the elastohydrodynamics of Cosserat rods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14702)
*Mohamed Warda*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过多尺度展开和可解性条件，推导了受末端追随力驱动的粘性流体中Cosserat杆颤振失稳弱非线性饱和的Stuart-Landau振幅方程，给出了超临界Hopf分岔的解析描述，并验证了与数值模拟的标度一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作已建立了粘性流体中Cosserat杆在末端追随力（follower force）作用下的颤振失稳（flutter instability）的线性理论，但该不稳定性在完全非线性过阻尼动力学中产生稳定极限环振荡（limit-cycle oscillations），其近阈值涌现机制尚缺乏解析描述。本文旨在给出该极限环的解析理论。

Method: 在临界追随力附近，对压缩直线基态进行多尺度展开（multiple-scale expansion）并逐阶消除久期增长项（secular growth）。在三次阶使用非厄米算子（non-Hermitian operator）的伴随本征模（adjoint eigenmode）施加可解性条件（solvability condition），导出临界振荡模式的Stuart-Landau振幅方程。

Result: Landau系数表示为涉及临界本征模、其伴随模及二次修正的内积（inner product）形式。约化理论预测了超临界Hopf分岔（supercritical Hopf bifurcation），稳态尖端振荡振幅按阈值距离的平方根标度增长。

Conclusion: 解析预测与非线性模拟中观察到的近阈值标度一致，为低雷诺数（low Reynolds number）压力驱动软体机械臂中自持拍击（self-sustained beating）的起始提供了解析规范形（normal form）。

Abstract: We study the weakly nonlinear saturation of the flutter instability of a planar Cosserat rod in a viscous fluid driven by a terminal follower force. This instability, established in our preceding work as a Hopf bifurcation of a non-self-adjoint linear operator, produces stable limit-cycle oscillations in the fully nonlinear overdamped dynamics. Here we derive an analytical description of the emergence of this limit cycle near threshold. Working close to the critical follower force, we perform a multiple-scale expansion about the compressed straight base state and systematically remove secular growth at higher orders. Solvability at cubic order, enforced using the adjoint eigenmode of the non-Hermitian operator, yields a Stuart-Landau amplitude equation for the critical oscillatory mode. The Landau coefficients are expressed as explicit inner products involving the critical eigenmode, its adjoint, and quadratic corrections. The resulting reduced theory predicts a supercritical Hopf bifurcation with a steady-state tip oscillation amplitude scaling as the square root of the distance from threshold. These predictions rationalize the near-threshold scaling observed in nonlinear simulations and provide an analytical normal form for the onset of self-sustained beating in pressure-driven soft robotic arms at low Reynolds number.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.stat-mech'></div>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [A microcanonical approach to criticality in the mean-field $φ^4$ model: evidence of intrinsic microcanonical structure before the thermodynamic limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14198)
*Loris Di Cairano,Roberto Franzosi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出微正则拐点分析（MIPA）方法，将有限尺寸临界性从热力学极限的模糊残余提升为一种结构性质，并通过平均场φ⁴模型验证了其有限尺寸临界标记向热力学临界点的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将集体临界行为（collective critical behavior）定义为仅在无穷大尺寸极限下才出现的热力学非解析性与发散性。本文旨在提出一种互补视角：临界性是系统组分间相互作用重排所导致的结构性质，在有限尺寸下已存在，仅渐近地变得奇异。

Method: 作者基于微正则熵（microcanonical entropy）的导数，在有限N体系中建立内在极值/拐点形态（intrinsic extremal/inflection morphologies）的表达；进而提出微正则拐点分析（Microcanonical Inflection-Point Analysis, MIPA），将这些形态转化为唯一的有限尺寸临界标记（finite-size critical marker）和明确的临界轨迹（critical trajectory）。以平均场φ⁴模型（mean-field φ⁴ model）作为严格基准，通过微正则模拟重构β_N(ε)和γ_N(ε)，并与解析结果进行对照验证。

Result: MIPA轨迹精确收敛于热力学临界点（thermodynamic critical point），同时协调其他可观测量向渐近行为（asymptotic behavior）的趋近过程。有限尺寸临界性由此被证明是可测量、可预测的对象。

Conclusion: 本工作将有限尺寸临界性从热力学极限的圆滑残余（rounded remnant）提升为一种本身具有可测量性和预测性的对象，对现代有限系统平台及数值研究具有直接意义。

Abstract: Collective critical behavior is often identified with thermodynamic nonanalyticities and divergences emerging only in the infinite-size limit. Here we adopt a complementary viewpoint: criticality is a structural property due to the rearrangement of the interactions among system's constituents that already exists at finite size and becomes singular only asymptotically. We show that the microcanonical entropy derivatives provide a natural finite-$N$ arena where such structure is encoded in intrinsic extremal/inflection morphologies, and that microcanonical inflection-point analysis (MIPA) turns these morphologies into a unique finite-size critical marker and a well-defined critical trajectory. Using the mean-field $φ^4$ model as a stringent benchmark, we reconstruct $β_N(\varepsilon)$ and $γ_N(\varepsilon)$ from microcanonical simulations, validate them against analytic results, and demonstrate that the MIPA trajectory converges to the exact thermodynamic critical point while simultaneously organizing the approach of other observables to their asymptotic behavior. Our results elevate finite-size criticality from a rounded remnant of the thermodynamic limit to a measurable and predictive object in its own right, with direct relevance to modern finite-system platforms and numerical studies.

</details>


### [8] [Matrix-Product Belief Propagation for continuous-state-space variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14522)
*Federico Florio,Alfredo Braunstein*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将矩阵乘积置信传播（Matrix-Product Belief Propagation）方法推广到连续或混合连续/离散自由度随机动力学模型上的方案，通过希尔伯特函数基的可调展开实现了线性计算复杂度，并在动力学伊辛模型（Kinetic Ising dynamics）上验证了其精度与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模稀疏网络上计算离散随机动力学的可观测量是许多应用的基础。已有的矩阵乘积置信传播方法虽能以受控误差半解析地估计可观测量，但仅适用于离散自由度模型。为将这一高效框架扩展到连续或混合连续/离散自由度系统，需要发展新的推广技术。

Method: 方法的核心是利用希尔伯特函数基（Hilbert function basis）进行可调展开，将连续或混合自由度嵌入函数空间表示。在该框架下，矩阵乘积置信传播方法中的矩阵大小（即键尺寸，bond size）与基尺寸共同决定了计算复杂度，且整体复杂度在时间跨度和网络规模上保持线性。

Result: 采用傅里叶基（Fourier basis）对动力学伊辛模型（Kinetic Ising dynamics）进行混合连续/离散表示，其中中间“局部场”（local fields）被处理为连续变量。通过与蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte-Carlo simulations）的对比验证了方法的准确性，并计算了时间自相关（time auto-correlations）、能量与磁化的时间演化，以及给定未来时间磁化的大偏差函数（large deviation function）。

Conclusion: 该方法成功将矩阵乘积置信传播的适用范围从离散自由度拓展至连续及混合自由度系统，且在保证线性计算复杂度的前提下实现了可控精度，为大规模稀疏网络上复杂随机动力学系统的半解析分析提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Computation of observables in discrete stochastic, possibly conditioned, dynamics over large sparse networks is at the basis of a myriad of applications. The Matrix-Product Belief Propagation method allows a semi-analytical estimation of such observables with a controlled error that depends on the size of the employed matrices, called bond size. Its computational cost is linear in the time horizon and the network size for a large family of models with discrete degrees of freedom. Here, a generalization of this method to models with continuous or mixed continuous/discrete degrees of freedom is presented, using a tunable expansion in a Hilbert function basis. The computational cost of the method is linear in the network size with a prefactor that depends on the basis size and the bond size. The method's efficacy is demonstrated by employing a Fourier basis for a mixed continuous/discrete representation of the Kinetic Ising dynamics with real-valued random couplings, where intermediate ``local fields'' are treated as continuous. The accuracy of the method is verified via comparison with Monte-Carlo simulations. For this model, we calculate time auto-correlations, time evolution of energy and magnetization, and finally we estimate the large deviation function of the magnetization at a given future time.

</details>

### [9] [Fast contracted Clebsch--Gordan tensor products for equivariant graph neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15073)
*Anton Bochkarev,Yury Lysogorskiy,Ralf Drautz*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于O(3)等变机器学习势函数中收缩Clebsch–Gordan张量积的O(L³)算法。通过将角度积分映射到结构化Gauss–Legendre和Fourier张量积网格，径向通道收缩与角度变换得以解耦。利用球面泊松括号恢复奇宇称Clebsch–Gordan通道，该方法扩展到原子团簇展开风格的等变消息传递，并通过数值求积验证。基准测试表明墙钟时间在实用l_max范围内呈L²缩放，在大l_max下过渡为L³。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有O(3)等变机器学习势函数中，收缩Clebsch–Gordan张量积的计算复杂度较高，且奇宇称通道（antisymmetric parity-odd Clebsch–Gordan channels）无法通过标量S²网格上的对称点积（symmetric pointwise product）直接实现，需要更高效的算法来降低计算开销。

Method: 将角度积分映射到Gauss–Legendre与Fourier张量积网格上，使径向通道收缩与角度变换解耦；利用表面旋量配对（surface-curl pairing）即球面泊松括号（spherical Poisson bracket）从网格上恢复L=1角动量，从而获得奇宇称Clebsch–Gordan通道，同时保持旋转等变性（rotational equivariance）。

Result: 在固定规范多项式秩（Canonical Polyadic rank, CP rank）下，收缩Clebsch–Gordan张量积的计算复杂度为O(L³)；完整未收缩张量积仍受O(L⁴)输出规模下界约束。基准测试显示墙钟时间在实用l_max范围内经验性地呈L²缩放，在线性项收缩（on-site contraction）中这是预渐近行为，在大l_max下转为L³；在消息传递（message passing）中这是结构性行为，运行时间受内存带宽限制于L²规模的网格张量上。

Conclusion: 该O(L³)算法有效降低了O(3)等变机器学习势函数中收缩Clebsch–Gordan张量积的计算代价，并成功处理了此前难以在网格上实现的奇宇称通道。该方法可扩展到宇称感知等变消息传递（parity-aware equivariant message passing）架构，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: We present an $\mathcal{O}(L^3)$ algorithm for evaluating contracted Clebsch--Gordan tensor products in $\mathrm{O}(3)$-equivariant machine learning potentials at fixed Canonical Polyadic (CP) rank. Mapping the angular integral to a structured Gauss--Legendre and Fourier tensor-product grid decouples the radial channel contractions from the angular transforms. The antisymmetric parity-odd Clebsch--Gordan channels, unreachable by the symmetric pointwise product on a scalar $S^2$ grid, are recovered through the surface-curl pairing $\hat r \cdot [\nabla_{S^2} A \times \nabla_{S^2} B]$, the spherical Poisson bracket, which supplies the $L=1$ angular momentum on the grid while preserving rotational equivariance. The construction extends to parity-aware equivariant message passing in atomic-cluster-expansion-style architectures and is verified by direct numerical quadrature. The full uncontracted Clebsch--Gordan tensor product remains subject to the $\mathcal{O}(L^4)$ output-size lower bound. A benchmark shows wall-clock scaling empirically as $L^2$ across the practical $l_{\max}$ range. For the on-site contraction this is pre-asymptotic, giving way to $L^3$ at large $l_{\max}$. For message passing it is structural and the runtime is memory-bandwidth bound on $L^2$-sized grid tensors.

### [10] [Dual Shapiro steps and fundamental transconductance in dc driven Bloch transistor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14080)
*A. B. Zorin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出基于布洛赫晶体管（Bloch transistor）的超导电路方案，利用约瑟夫森振荡（Josephson oscillations）与布洛赫振荡（Bloch oscillations）的相互锁相（phase lock）效应，在电流-电压曲线上形成类似双Shapiro台阶的电流台阶，并实现跨导等于量子电导倒数（1/R_Q），为无需强磁场的替代量子电阻标准（quantum standard of resistance）提供新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子电阻标准通常依赖强磁场下的量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect），实验条件苛刻。本文旨在探索一种基于超导电路、无需强磁场的替代方案，利用布洛赫晶体管中两种振荡的锁相机制实现量子化电阻。

Method: 采用由两个小电容约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）串联、中间形成小岛（island）的布洛赫晶体管结构，通过两个直流电源分别控制约瑟夫森振荡（频率f_J = 2e\overline{V_J}/h）和布洛赫振荡（频率f_B = \overline{I_B}/2e），利用二者之间的相互锁相条件f_J = f_B，在电流-电压曲线上获得电流台阶。

Result: 在布洛赫晶体管中，约瑟夫森振荡与布洛赫振荡实现锁相时，电流-电压曲线上出现电流台阶\overline{I}_B = 2ef_J，行为类似于微波辐照下的双Shapiro台阶（dual Shapiro steps）。同时，跨导\overline{I_B}/\overline{V_J}等于1/R_Q，其中R_Q = h/4e^2为电阻量子（resistance quantum）。

Conclusion: 上述结果表明，基于布洛赫晶体管的超导电路有望构建一种无需强磁场的替代量子电阻标准，为新型量子计量（quantum metrology）方案提供理论依据和实验方向。

Abstract: We propose a superconducting circuit based on the Bloch transistor, a quantum device consisting of two small-capacitance Josephson junctions connected in series and having a small island in between. This device is driven by two dc electrical sources controlling Josephson oscillations of frequency $f_J = 2e\overline{V_J}/h$, related to the average voltage $\overline{V_J}$ on the transistor, and Bloch oscillations of frequency $f_B = \overline{I_B}/2e$, related to the average current $\overline{I_B}$ injected into the transistor island. Due to the Bloch transistor properties, these two types of oscillations can mutually phase lock, i.e., $f_J = f_B$. This leads to formation of current steps on the current-voltage curve at $\overline{I}_B = 2ef_J$, which are similar to the dual Shapiro steps appearing at current $\overline{I}=2ef$ under microwave irradiation of frequency $f$. Moreover, transconductance $\overline{I_B}/\overline{V_J}$ takes the fundamental value of $1/R_Q$, where $R_Q = h/4e^2$ is the resistance quantum. The obtained results pave the way to the alternative quantum standard of resistance, based on the superconducting circuit and operating without applying strong magnetic field.

</details>


### [11] [Shear-stress-constrained superconductivity in Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14265)
*Liling Sun,Shu Cai,Jinyu Zhao,Qi Wu,Yang Ding,Tao Xiang,Ho-kwang Mao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究提出，Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）镍氧化物仅在 Ni-O 框架的局部受限变形处于一个有界的剪切应变窗口（bounded shear-strain window）时才会表现出超导电性，这种剪切应力约束超导电性（shear-stress-constrained superconductivity）统一解释了压力阈值、可逆性、空间不均匀性、压力介质依赖性、薄膜-基底敏感性和可重复性等多种实验现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper镍氧化物在块材加压和薄膜外延约束下均能表现超导电性，但其对样品质量、氧含量、缺陷和应力条件高度敏感，缺乏一个统一的物理机制来解释这些复杂的实验现象。

Method: 提出一个理论框架：超导电性仅在Ni-O框架的局部受限变形落在一个有界剪切应变窗口内时才会出现；该变形控制了八面体旋转（octahedral rotations）、层间Ni-O-Ni键角以及Ni dz2和dx2-y2轨道之间的耦合。

Result: 该剪切应力约束超导电性机制能够统一解释RP镍氧化物的压力阈值、可逆性、空间不均匀性、压力介质依赖性、薄膜-基底敏感性和可重复性等关键实验特征。

Conclusion: RP镍氧化物的超导电性受到剪切应变的严格约束，这一物理图像为理解该体系不同实验条件下的超导行为提供了统一的框架。

Abstract: Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates exhibit superconductivity under pressure in bulk crystals and under epitaxial constraint in thin films, while remaining highly sensitive to sample quality, oxygen content, defects, and stress conditions. We propose that the metastable RP lattice becomes superconducting only when the local constrained deformation of the Ni-O framework falls within a bounded shear-strain window. This deformation controls octahedral rotations, the interlayer Ni-O-Ni bond angle, and coupling between Ni dz2 and dx2-y2 orbitals. This shear-stress-constrained superconductivity scenario unifies the understanding of the pressure threshold, reversibility, spatial inhomogeneity, pressure-medium dependence, film-substrate sensitivity, and reproducibility.

</details>


### [12] [Atomically resolved intrinsic superconducting gap in (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14806)
*Xinxin Wang,Yaqi Chen,Cui Ding,Lizhi Xu,Jian-Jian Miao,Guangdi Zhou,Zhuoyu Chen,Yu-Jie Sun,Jin-Feng Jia,Qi-Kun Xue*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper双层镍酸盐（bilayer nickelates）是研究高温超导的新平台，但其超导配对对称性（superconducting pairing symmetry）尚存争议。本文旨在通过原子尺度实验观测明确该体系的超导能隙结构。

Method: 使用原子级分辨率的扫描隧道显微镜和谱学（scanning tunnelling microscopy and spectroscopy, STM/STS），在低温超高真空（UHV）条件下研究生长于SrLaAlO4衬底上的1.5个单胞（unit-cell）厚（La,Pr）3Ni2O7薄膜，并通过不同UHV暴露时间对比样品表面状态。

Result: 低温UHV转移样品呈现有序的sqrt(2) × sqrt(2)表面重构，并产生可重复的U形谱（U-shaped spectra），具有~14 meV和~20 meV两个能隙尺度（gap scales）以及展平的零电导底部；而UHV中长时间暴露且转移过程中未冷却的样品虽保留表面重构且超导转变起始温度（onset）高于40 K，却呈现V形谱（V-shaped spectra）。宽能谱范围测量表明氧流失（oxygen loss）可混入密度波相关谱重（density-wave-related spectral weight）。

Conclusion: 测量结果提供了双层镍酸盐超薄膜中本征无节点超导能隙（intrinsic nodeless superconducting gap）的原子尺度观测证据，支持无节点配对对称性。

Abstract: Ruddlesden-Popper bilayer nickelates provide an emerging platform for studying high-temperature superconductivity, yet the superconducting pairing symmetry remains under debate. Here, we use atomic-resolution scanning tunnelling microscopy and spectroscopy to investigate superconducting 1.5-unit-cell (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 films grown on SrLaAlO4. A cryogenic ultrahigh-vacuum (UHV) sample transfer preserves an ordered sqrt(2) * sqrt(2) surface and yields reproducible U-shaped spectra with two gap scales of ~14 and ~20 meV and extended flat zero-conductance bottoms. By contrast, samples exposed for a longer time in UHV without cooling during transfer show V-shaped spectra despite retaining the surface reconstruction and a transport superconducting transition onset above 40 K. Wide-energy-range spectra indicate that oxygen loss can mix density-wave-related spectral weight. Our measurements provide an atomic-scale observation of the intrinsic nodeless superconducting gap in bilayer nickelate ultrathin films.

### [13] [T-E formulation-based modeling of thin HTS shell magnetization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14818)
*Leonid Prigozhin,Vladimir Sokolovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文扩展了基于T-E公式（T-E formulation）的混合有限元方法（mixed finite element method），从平直超导薄膜推广到非平坦超导壳层（含金属基底），并通过球体磁化及圆柱形磁动力泵等算例验证了该方法能同时准确计算电流密度与电场分布，且无需对周围空间进行网格剖分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的薄膜磁化数值方法主要聚焦于计算电流密度分布，而第二类超导体（type-II superconductor）的高度非线性电流-电压特性使得电场的精确计算极其困难。先前针对平直超导薄膜的T-E公式混合有限元方法虽然能同时求解两个变量，但尚不能处理非平坦的曲面超导壳层结构。 

Method: 该方法基于T-E公式的混合有限元框架，将计算域限制在超导薄膜/壳层本身，无需对周围空间进行网格剖分（no meshing of the surrounding space）。通过薄壳近似（thin-shell approximation）将问题降维至二维，并将其从平直薄膜扩展到非平坦超导壳层，同时考虑金属基底的存在。

Result: 通过多个测试算例（包括球体磁化模型）验证了方法的有效性，并将其应用于圆柱形磁动力泵（cylindrical magnetic dynamo pump）的实际模型，成功计算了产生的开路电压（open-circuit voltage）。

Conclusion: 扩展后的T-E公式混合有限元方法能够在非平坦超导壳层结构中同时精确计算电流密度与电场，为复杂几何构型的超导磁化建模提供了有效的数值工具。

Abstract: Numerical methods for modeling thin-film magnetization are primarily focused on computing the current density distribution. The highly nonlinear current-voltage characteristic of type-II superconductors significantly complicates the accurate computation of the electric field. The T-E formulation-based mixed finite element method, previously derived for flat superconducting films, enables the simultaneous, accurate determination of both variables. Another advantage of this method is that the computational domain is limited to the film itself: no meshing of the surrounding space is required. The thin-shell approximation reduces the problem to a two-dimensional one.
  This work extends the T-E formulation and numerical method to non-flat superconducting shells with a metal substrate. We validate the method with several test examples, including modeling the magnetization of a sphere. The method is then applied to a realistic model of a cylindrical magnetic dynamo pump, and the generated open-circuit voltage is computed.

### [14] [Perfect transmission and parallel composition for quantum walks on graphs with two leads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14640)
*Allan John Gerrard,Ryo Asaka,Kazumitsu Sakai*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对连接两个引线（leads）的有限图上的连续时间量子游走（continuous-time quantum walk），推导出双端散射矩阵（two-terminal scattering matrix）的特征多项式显式公式，并引入三个可加性实数参量（μ₁、μ₂、ν）来刻画平行图组合下的完美透射条件，将设计特定透射性质的图问题转化为几何向量求和问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在有限图两端连接引线情况下的连续时间量子游走的散射问题，旨在系统刻画图结构与其透射特性之间的数学关系，并降低对具有指定透射性质的图进行设计的复杂度。

Method: 利用有限图及其删点子图（vertex-deleted subgraphs）的特征多项式，推导双端散射矩阵的显式公式。对于实权重双端图，引入三个满足平行组合（parallel composition）可加性的实数量（μ₁、μ₂、ν），利用它们描述完美透射条件。

Result: 完美透射（perfect transmission）在固定动量下的充要条件为 μ₁ = μ₂，且其对应点位于 (μ,ν) 平面上的双曲线（hyperbola）上；双曲线上的不同点决定了透射相位（transmission phase）。这使得寻找具有预设透射特性的图可以转化为对更小构建模块进行几何向量求和的问题。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一套代数‑几何框架，将量子游走中图的透射性质分析简化为有限个可加参量的几何运算，为模块化设计具有特定透射谱的量子图网络提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We study scattering for continuous-time quantum walks on finite graphs with two attached leads. We derive explicit formulae for the two-terminal scattering matrix in terms of characteristic polynomials of the finite graph and its vertex-deleted subgraphs. For real-weighted two-terminal graphs, we then introduce three real quantities, $μ_1$, $μ_2$, and $ν$, which are each additive under parallel composition of graphs. In these variables, perfect transmission at fixed momentum is characterized by the condition $μ_1=μ_2$ together with a hyperbola in the corresponding $(μ,ν)$-plane, whose points determine the transmission phase. This turns the search for graphs with prescribed transmission properties into a geometric vector-sum problem for smaller building blocks.

</details>


### [15] [Evolution of Gaussian mixed states under the Markovian master equation for a driven quantum oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14756)
*B. A. Tay*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究线性位移或驱动的量子马尔可夫主方程，证明快速旋转模式不影响线性驱动力下的位移动力学，得到位移高斯混合态的解析解，并揭示了非驱动与驱动刘维尔算符在能量算符位移变换下的例外点结构共享性，以及临界阻尼振荡器在例外点处的多项式-指数衰减行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有结果表明高斯混合态的位移动力学依赖于刘维尔算符（Liouvillian）的幺正部分和系统衰减率，但与浴温度无关。本文进一步探究线性驱动力下快速旋转模式对位移动力学是否产生影响，并希望建立非驱动与驱动系统的例外点（exceptional points）结构之间的关联。

Method: 研究采用量子马尔可夫主方程（quantum Markovian master equation）的解析求解方法，通过能量算符位移算符（unitary displacement operator）建立非驱动与驱动刘维尔算符之间的联系。分别以脉冲力（impulsive force）和谐振力（harmonic force）为例分析含时外力的影响。

Result: 快速旋转模式在存在线性驱动力时不影响系统的位移动力学。获得了位移高斯混合态（displaced Gaussian mixed states）的解析解。验证了非驱动与驱动系统共享相同的例外点结构。在例外点处，临界阻尼振荡器的位移呈现出特征性的时间多项式因子乘以指数衰减（polynomial-in-time prefactor multiplied by exponential decay）的形式。恒定驱动下的结果在含时驱动下仍然有效。

Conclusion: 线性驱动下快速旋转模式对位移动力学无影响这一结论拓宽了对量子主方程动力学行为的理解。非驱动与驱动系统之间通过幺正变换共享例外点结构，为分析临界阻尼行为提供了统一框架。含时外力下的结果保持与恒定驱动一致，表明该分析具有良好的普适性。

Abstract: We study a generic quantum Markovian master equation for a linearly displaced or driven harmonic oscillator. It was known that the displacement dynamics of Gaussian mixed states depends on the unitary part of the Liouvillian, the decay rate of the system but not on the bath temperature. Here we further show that the fast-rotating modes do not affect the system's displacement dynamics under linear driving forces. Analytical solutions of the quantum master equation are obtained for displaced Gaussian mixed states. Because the non-driven and driven Liouvillians are related by a unitary displacement operator, they are expected to share the same exceptional points structure. At the exceptional points, the displacement of critically damped oscillator displays a characteristics polynomial-in-time prefactor multiplied by an exponential decay. We discuss how external time-dependent forces affect the displacement dynamics using impulsive force and harmonic force as examples. The results obtained for constant driving remain valid in the presence of time-dependent driving.

### [16] [New approaches to almost i.i.d. information theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15114)
*Filippo Girardi,Giacomo De Palma,Ludovico Lami*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文针对量子信息论中“独立同分布（i.i.d.）”假设过于严格的问题，基于归一化量子Wasserstein距离和平均k体边际（average k-body marginal）两种思路，提出了两种“几乎独立同分布（almost i.i.d.）”量子态的新定义，并建立了三者之间的严格层级关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际量子信息处理场景中，独立同分布（i.i.d.）假设过于苛刻且不现实；为描述物理上更合理的“几乎i.i.d.”量子源，需要更灵活的定义和分类框架。

Method: 基于归一化量子Wasserstein距离（normalised quantum Wasserstein distance）和平均k体边际（average k-body marginal）两种途径，分别给出两种新的几乎i.i.d.量子态定义，并通过显式反例（explicit examples）证明三者之间的严格层级关系。

Result: 建立了三种几乎i.i.d.定义的严格层级关系：Mazzola等人的定义最为严格，基于量子Wasserstein距离的定义居中，基于k体边际的定义最为宽松，且三者之间存在严格分离。

Conclusion: 新的定义扩展了几乎i.i.d.量子态的分类体系，为进一步研究实际量子信息源的行为提供了更灵活的理论工具。

Abstract: Independent and identically distributed (i.i.d.) states are ubiquitous in quantum information theory. However, in a practical setting, the i.i.d. assumption is too stringent, and possibly not realistic. A physically more compelling class of 'almost i.i.d.' sources was recently proposed by [Mazzola/Sutter/Renner, arXiv:2603.15792]. In this paper, we introduce two alternative definitions of almost i.i.d. states, based on the normalised quantum Wasserstein distance and on the idea of looking at the average $k$-body marginal. We explore some basic properties of these notions and prove a strict hierarchical relation among them, with Mazzola et al.'s notion being the strictest, the one based on $k$-body marginals the loosest, and the one based on the quantum Wasserstein distance in between. Strict separation is established by means of explicit examples.

### [17] [Universal quantum resource distillation via composite generalised quantum Stein's lemma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15174)
*Ludovico Lami,Bartosz Regula,Ryuji Takagi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在资源非生成操作框架下，量子资源蒸馏（包括量子纠缠纯化）可以实现通用最优速率，无需任何关于输入态的先验知识，从而验证了量子资源蒸馏的鲁棒性。该结果依赖于广义量子Stein引理在复合假设检验中的扩展，以及单次量子信息学（one-shot quantum information）和模糊化技术（blurring technique）的新进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子资源操控协议（如纠缠蒸馏）的性能由从给定噪声态中产生目标态的速率衡量。但现有协议为达到最优速率，需要精确适配量子态，即要求对输入态的完美知识且不允许制备误差。本文旨在解决这一局限，探索能否在无需输入态知识的条件下实现通用最优蒸馏。

Method: 本文在资源非生成操作（resource non-generating operations）框架下进行研究，扩展了量子假设检验（quantum hypothesis testing）中的广义量子Stein引理（generalised quantum Stein's lemma），将其应用于复合假设检验场景——其中零假设不再是固定量子态，而是由未知态的独立同分布（i.i.d.）副本组成。该渐近问题的解决依赖于单次量子信息学（one-shot quantum information）的新发展以及对Lami（arXiv:2408.06410）模糊化技术（blurring technique）的改进。

Result: 研究发现，量子资源蒸馏可以通用地（universally）实现：无需任何关于输入态的知识即可达到最优蒸馏速率。该结果特别适用于非纠缠映射（non-entangling maps）下的量子纠缠纯化（purification of quantum entanglement），其中最优速率由正则化相对纠缠熵（regularised relative entropy of entanglement）决定。

Conclusion: 本文证明了量子资源蒸馏在资源非生成操作框架下具有通用性和鲁棒性，即输入态知识并非达到最优速率的前提条件。这一结论从理论上确保了量子资源操控协议的实用性，消除了对精确输入态知识的依赖。

Abstract: The performance of quantum resource manipulation protocols, including key examples such as distillation of quantum entanglement, is measured in terms of the rate at which desired target states can be produced from a given noisy state. However, to achieve optimal rates, known protocols require precise tailoring to the quantum state in question, demanding a perfect knowledge of the input and allowing no errors in its preparation. Here we show that distillation of quantum resources in the framework of resource non-generating operations can be performed universally: optimal rates of distillation can be achieved with no knowledge of the input state whatsoever, certifying the robustness of quantum resource distillation. The findings apply in particular to the purification of quantum entanglement under non-entangling maps, where the optimal rates are governed by the regularised relative entropy of entanglement. Our result relies on an extension of the generalised quantum Stein's lemma in quantum hypothesis testing to a composite setting where the null hypothesis is no longer a fixed quantum state, but is rather composed of i.i.d. copies of an unknown state. The solution of this asymptotic problem is made possible through new developments in one-shot quantum information and a refinement of the blurring technique from [Lami, arXiv:2408.06410].

### [18] [Translation symmetry-enforced long-range entanglement in mixed states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15200)
*Ryan Thorngren,Lei Gioia,Carolyn Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 通过计数论证表明，即使在平移对称性允许存在对称短程纠缠本征态的情况下，零动量扇区也无法被这些态完全张成；平移对称性从强到弱自发对称性破缺的固定点混合态必然具有长程纠缠（long-range entanglement），且这种纠缠无法通过长程连通关联函数检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示混合态（mixed states）中一种微妙的、被传统关联函数所忽略的长程纠缠形式，具体针对平移对称性（translation symmetry）下从强到弱自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking）的固定点态。

Method: 采用计数论证（counting argument），通过比较对称短程纠缠本征态的数量与零动量扇区（zero momentum sector）维度的关系，证明前者不足以张成后者。

Result: 零动量扇区不能被对称短程纠缠本征态张成，因此平移对称性从强到弱自发对称性破缺的固定点态是长程纠缠的，不能写成短程纠缠态的混合。

Conclusion: 存在一种混合态中的微妙长程纠缠，它无法通过长程连通关联函数（long-range connected correlation functions）被检测到，表明需要新的诊断工具来刻画此类纠缠。

Abstract: We show by a counting argument that even though translation symmetry admits symmetric short-range entangled (SRE) eigenstates, there are not enough such SRE eigenstates to span the zero momentum sector. This means that the fixed point strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking state of translation symmetry is long-range entangled: it cannot be written as a mixture of SRE states. This is a subtle form of long-range entanglement in mixed states that cannot be detected by long-range connected correlation functions.

### [19] [Extensive long-range magic in non-Abelian topological orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15150)
*Yuzhen Zhang,Isaac H. Kim,Yimu Bao,Sagar Vijay*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明非阿贝尔拓扑序的低能态具有无法通过常数深度局域幺正电路消除的长程魔力（magic），从而建立拓扑序的一种新资源理论刻画，并推导了稳定子态（stabilizer states）无法近似满足纠缠自举公理的非阿贝尔弦网模型低能态，以及高维系统中具有非平凡融合空间激发的态必然具有长程魔力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对拓扑序的复杂性刻画主要依赖于制备所需线性电路深度这一传统度量，但缺乏对拓扑序中量子资源（如魔力）精细结构的理解。本文旨在揭示非阿贝尔拓扑序的低能态是否具有超越电路深度的、不可消除的长程复杂性，并为拓扑序提供一种新的资源理论表征。

Method: 通过证明一个no-go定理，指出稳定子态即使在常数深度局域幺正电路作用下也无法近似满足纠缠自举（entanglement bootstrap）公理的非阿贝尔弦网模型（string-net model）的低能态。此外，分析阿贝尔弦网态中互易编织相位（mutual braiding phases）的量子化条件，并论证其违例必然导致长程魔力。对于高维系统，基于纠缠面积律（entanglement area law）及具有非平凡融合空间（fusion space）的激发，进行一般性论证。

Result: （1）非阿贝尔拓扑序的低能态具有长程且无法由常数深度局域幺正电路消除的魔力；（2）稳定子态（即使允许常数深度局域幺正操作）无法近似满足纠缠自举公理的非阿贝尔弦网模型低能态；（3）稳定子可实现的阿贝尔弦网相中，互易编织相位由on-site qudit维数量子化，违反该条件必然导致长程魔力；（4）高维空间中，满足纠缠面积律且拥有非平凡融合空间的任意态均具有长程魔力，适用于量子双模型（quantum double models）的基态和低能态。

Conclusion: 非阿贝尔拓扑序的低能态蕴含一种内在且长程的魔法资源，这一发现细化了传统对拓扑序复杂性的理解，并为拓扑序提供了一种基于资源理论（resource theory）的新刻画。该结论对高维系统中的拓扑相也普遍适用。

Abstract: We show that the low-energy states of non-Abelian topological orders possess extensive magic which is long-ranged, and cannot be eliminated by a constant-depth local unitary circuit. This refines conventional notions of complexity beyond the linear circuit depth which is required to prepare any topological phase, and provides a new resource-theoretic characterization of topological orders. A central technical result is a no-go theorem establishing that stabilizer states--even up to constant-depth local unitarie--cannot approximate low-energy states of non-Abelian string-net models which satisfy the entanglement bootstrap axioms. Moreover, we show that stabilizer-realizable Abelian string-net phases have mutual braiding phases quantized by the on-site qudit dimension, and that any violation of this condition necessarily implies extensive long-range magic. Extending to higher spatial dimensions, we argue that any state obeying an entanglement area law and hosting excitations with nontrivial fusion spaces must exhibit extensive long-range magic. This applies, in particular, to ground-states and low-energy states of higher-dimensional quantum double models.

Method: 采用全电控协议，通过调节电场强度来识别离散的自旋-轨道相位匹配条件（spin-orbit phase-matching conditions），从而恢复近完美的态传输；同时，控制电场方向可对齐自旋-轨道轴，抑制非激发守恒过程。

Abstract: Semiconductor hole-spin qubits offer a promising route to quantum computation due to their weak hyperfine interaction, and strong intrinsic spin-orbit coupling enabling electric control of qubits. Scalable architectures, however, require coherent long-distance quantum state transfer, which is hindered in these systems by spin-orbit induced anisotropic exchange. Here we show that this limitation can be overcome by using an all-electric control protocol. By tuning the electric field strength, we identify discrete spin-orbit phase-matching conditions that restore near-perfect state transfer, independent of the rotation axis. Complementarily, controlling the electric field direction aligns the spin-orbit axis, suppressing excitation non-conserving processes and enabling robust transfer without fine tuning. Our results establish that electrical control of spin-orbit phases through either magnitude tuning or axis alignment as a practical route for robust quantum information transport in hole-spin quantum dot arrays.

### [21] [Power sensitivity of broadband radiofrequency detectors based on quantum diamond spins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14244)
*Nicholas Gillespie,Christopher T. -K. Lew,Ryan Kinsella,Andy Sayers,Brant Gibson,David A. Broadway,Jean-Philippe Tetienne*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从理论上分析了基于金刚石氮-空位（NV）中心的射频（RF）探测器在输入RF功率下的灵敏度，推导了功率灵敏度与RF-自旋界面几何尺寸的标度律，发现功率灵敏度与特征物理尺寸成反比，并数值估计了可达的灵敏度极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注NV基RF探测器的磁场灵敏度，这适用于近场源RF信号。然而，对于外部输入RF功率的应用场景，需要以输入RF功率为基准的灵敏度分析，目前尚缺乏相关理论框架。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究功率灵敏度作为RF-自旋界面几何（radiofrequency-spin interface geometry）的函数；推导了斜率检测（slope-detection）和方差检测（variance-detection）两种RF传感协议下的功率灵敏度标度律，并考虑了多种噪声机制（noise regimes）。

Result: 在大多数场景下，功率灵敏度与RF-自旋界面的特征物理尺寸成反比（例如共面波导的宽度或环形天线的直径），即结构越小、探测的NV体积越小，功率灵敏度越高——这与磁场灵敏度的趋势相反。数值估计显示，光子散粒噪声极限下可达灵敏度为10^{-20} W Hz^{-1}（斜率检测）和10^{-12} W Hz^{-1/2}（方差检测）。

Conclusion: 该工作为NV基RF探测器的进一步优化奠定了理论基础，明确揭示了功率灵敏度与小尺寸结构之间的关联，为实际器件设计提供了指导方向。

Abstract: Nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centres in diamond can be used to detect radiofrequency (RF) signals through coupling of the RF magnetic field with the NV spins, combined with optical readout of the spin state. The sensitivity of such RF detectors has so far been mainly studied in terms of magnetic field sensitivity, which is relevant when the RF signal is generated by a near-field source. However, for applications where the RF input is delivered externally, a more relevant quantity is the sensitivity in terms of the input RF power. Here we theoretically analyse the power sensitivity of NV-based RF detectors as a function of the RF-spin interface geometry. We derive scaling laws of the power sensitivity for both slope-detection and variance-detection RF sensing protocols, and for various noise regimes. We find that, in most scenarios, the power sensitivity scales inversely with the characteristic physical dimension of the RF-spin interface, for instance the width of a coplanar waveguide or the diameter of a loop antenna. In other words, the smaller the structure and the probed NV volume, the better the power sensitivity, which is contrary to the case of magnetic field sensitivity. Lastly, we numerically estimate that photon shot noise limited sensitivities of 10^{-20} W Hz^{-1} (slope) and 10^{-12} W Hz^{-1/2} (variance) are achievable. This work lays the groundwork for further optimisation of NV-based RF detectors.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超导量子比特（qubit）系统在高维量子计算（qudit-based quantum computing）中面临泄漏误差（leakage errors）的挑战，缺乏天然保护机制。本文旨在设计一种可直接实现受保护的高维多能级系统（qudit），以突破量子比特范式的限制。

Method: 系统推广了通量量子比特（fluxonium）的设计，通过多谐波约瑟夫森结块（multi-harmonic Josephson building block elements）实现傅里叶工程（Fourier engineering），从而定制约瑟夫森势（Josephson potential）的形状，在其极小值处产生分数通量态（fraxons）作为低能态（low-lying states）。采用了非阿贝尔受激拉曼绝热通道（non-Abelian stimulated Raman adiabatic passage, STIRAP）协议实现单qutrit门操作。

Result: 展示了 $d=4$ 和 $d=5$ 的qudit系统能谱（spectrum），并详细分析了qutrit（$d=3$）情形。分析了与辐射耦合的偶极矩阵元（dipole matrix elements）。

Conclusion: 该平台为电路工程（circuit engineering）和超越量子比特（beyond the qubit）范式的量子计算（quantum computing）开辟了新前景。

Abstract: We propose a superconducting circuit hosting $d$ low-lying states, well separated from the rest of the spectrum, that naturally realizes a qudit system protected from leakage errors. The system represents a generalization of the fluxonium and the low-energy states are constituted by fractional fluxon states, that we call {\it fraxons}, localized in the minima of a suitably designed Josephson potential. The latter is tailored through a Fourier engineering approach, that employs multi-harmonic Josephson building block elements composed by a Josephson junction and an inductance connected in series. We present the spectrum of a $d=4$ and a $d=5$ qudit system and study in detail the qutrit case. We analyze the dipole matrix elements for coupling to radiation and propose a non-Abelian, stimulated Raman adiabatic passage (STIRAP) protocol for single-qutrit gates, that is particularly suited for the present system. The proposed platform opens novel perspectives in circuit engineering and quantum computing beyond the qubit paradigm.

</details>


### [23] [Mixed-State Long-Range Entanglement from Dimensional Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15201)
*Leonardo A. Lessa,Tsung-Cheng Lu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种强对称多体混合态中长程纠缠（LRE）的新机制，该机制不依赖于对称性反常或长程关联。以一维环上平移不变子空间中的最大混合态为例，指出平移对称短程纠缠态所张子空间维度仅随系统尺寸多项式增长，而整个平移不变子空间维度呈指数增长，从而证明该态为LRE。此外，该态具有对数增长的条件互信息、强到弱自发对称性破缺以及依赖于Rényi指数的算符空间纠缠等非传统性质。作者还构造了一个几何非局域的Lindbladian，使该态作为稳态得以稳定。研究结果指出“维度失配（dimensional mismatch）”是内在存在于多体混合态中的一条通向LRE的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索强对称多体混合态中一种不依赖于对称性反常或长程关联的长程纠缠（LRE）新机制，以拓展对混合态拓扑相和纠缠结构的理解。

Method: 以一维环上平移不变子空间最大混合态为主要例子，通过比较平移对称短程纠缠态子空间与全平移不变子空间的维度规模（多项式 vs 指数增长），证明LRE存在；并分析条件互信息、对称性破缺类型和Rényi熵等纠缠量度。

Result: 该最大混合态具有对数增长的条件互信息、强到弱自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry-breaking）以及依赖Rényi指数的算符空间纠缠（Rényi-index-dependent operator-space entanglement）。构造的几何非局域Lindbladian可稳定该态作为稳态。

Conclusion: 维度失配（dimensional mismatch）是一种内在于多体混合态的、通向长程纠缠（LRE）的新途径，不依赖于对称性反常或长程关联。

Abstract: We present a new mechanism for long-range entanglement (LRE) in strongly symmetric many-body mixed states that does not rely on symmetry anomalies or long-range correlations. Our primary example is the maximally mixed state in the translation-invariant subspace on a one-dimensional ring. This state is LRE because translationally symmetric short-range entangled states span a subspace whose dimension grows only polynomially with system size, whereas the full translation-invariant subspace grows exponentially. We further discuss certain unconventional properties of this state, including logarithmically growing conditional mutual information, strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry-breaking, and Rényi-index-dependent operator-space entanglement. We also construct a geometrically non-local Lindbladian to stabilize this state as the steady state. Our results identify dimensional mismatch as a novel route to LRE that is intrinsic to many-body mixed states.

</details>

### [24] [Analytic thin disks and rings in a class of nonasymptotically flat static spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13890)
*Shokoufe Faraji,Ruijing Tang*

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有外部四极畸变的轴对称时空中薄盘吸积的动力学与辐射特征，发现外部物质分布的畸变效应会显著影响轨道运动与吸积结构，并表明畸变时空的局域几何具有可观测的吸积形态与辐射特征后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统理想化孤立模型忽视了外部物质分布对致密天体强场环境的改变，该研究旨在检验带有外部四极畸变的局域几何能否产生独特的吸积信号，并确定该局域解保持自洽的物理径向范围。

Method: 研究采用真空爱因斯坦场方程的精确解，构建一个略微变形的致密天体沉浸于外部四极场中的静态轴对称时空，并在此背景下分析几何薄、光学厚的相对论吸积（relativistic accretion）。

Result: 外部四极畸变在轨道动力学和吸积结构上留下了清晰印记；辐射区外缘与辐射压—气体压主导的转变密切相关，表明畸变几何与流动热力学性质之间存在联系。

Conclusion: 畸变时空的局域性不仅是形式上的几何特征，更对吸积流的形态与辐射性质具有可观测后果。

Abstract: External matter distributions can substantially reshape the strong field environment of compact objects, yet this effect is usually neglected in idealized isolated models. In this work, we investigate geometrically thin, optically thick relativistic accretion onto a static axisymmetric space-time that describes a slightly deformed compact object immersed in an external quadrupolar field as an exact solution of vacuum Einstein field equations. Our aim is to determine whether such locally geometries can produce distinctive accretion signatures and, more broadly, to identify the physically meaningful radial domain over which the local solution remains self-consistent. We show that the external quadrupolar distortion leaves a clear imprint on both orbital dynamics and accretion structure. We further find that the outer edge of the radiating region is closely tied to the transition between radiation pressure and gas pressure dominance, which may link the geometry to the thermodynamic properties of the flow. Therefore, the local nature of the distorted spacetime is not merely a formal geometric feature, but has observable consequences for the morphology and emission properties of accretion flows.

### [25] [On the impossibility of observational confirmation of black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13901)
*Thiago T. Bergamaschi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文指出，广义相对论虽取得了显著的实验与观测成功，但近期LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA、事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）和GRAVITY合作组的数据仅提供了黑洞候选体（black hole candidates）的证据，而非黑洞存在的确凿证明；根本上，广义相对论本身对观测可证实性施加了限制，任何观测数据都不足以确认黑洞的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清一个广泛存在的误解：公众和部分学界常将LIGO、事件视界望远镜等数据视为黑洞存在的直接证明（demonstration），但实际上这些数据仅排除了特定的致密天体替代模型，无法提供黑洞存在的决定性证据。

Method: 通过对当前引力波与电磁观测数据的理论分析，结合广义相对论（general relativity）的基本原理，论证观测数据在逻辑上无法证实黑洞的存在。

Result: 当前数据与克尔黑洞（Kerr black holes）的预言高度吻合，但仅能排除部分替代模型；广义相对论本身在原理上限制了任何观测数据对黑洞存在的确认能力。

Conclusion: 无论黑洞是否存在，广义相对论决定了没有任何观测数据可以充分（sufficiently）确认黑洞的存在；因此，当前所谓的“黑洞证据”在严格意义上仅对应黑洞候选体。

Abstract: General relativity has achieved remarkable experimental and observational success. Critically, recent data from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA, Event Horizon Telescope, and GRAVITY collaborations are often credited with \textit{demonstrating} the existence of black holes, but in fact they only provide evidence for objects that should be regarded as black hole candidates. While current data are in striking agreement with the predictions for Kerr black holes, they can only rule out specific alternative models of compact objects rather than provide conclusive proof of black holes. More fundamentally, and independent of whether or not black holes exist, general relativity itself imposes limits on what can be observationally established. Essentially, no observational data is sufficient to confirm the existence of black holes.

</details>


### [26] [Thermodynamics and optical aspects of ModMax black holes in higher order curvature gravity with quintessence dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13908)
*Ahmad Al-Badawi,Usman Zafar,Abdul Jawad,Kazuharu Bamba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在高阶曲率引力（higher-order curvature gravity）中，通过将 ModMax 框架下的电磁场与暗能量（quintessence）耦合，导出了一个精确的黑洞解，并分析了其热力学（thermodynamics）、几何热力学（geothermodynamics）及光学性质（包括光子球和阴影半径），发现高阶曲率修正和暗能量显著增大了阴影尺寸，而电荷的作用相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高阶曲率引力框架下，结合非线性电磁理论（如 ModMax）和暗能量组分，构造并研究新的精确黑洞解，以探索其热力学稳定性、相结构以及可观测光学特征（如黑洞阴影）。

Method: 将 ModMax 非线性电磁理论与 quintessence 暗能量组分耦合到高阶曲率引力中，求解得到纯电黑洞解；利用热力学几何（thermodynamic geometry）分析微观相互作用和相变；通过零测地线（null geodesics）推导光子球半径及阴影半径的精确解析表达式。

Result: ModMax 理论在此纯电情形下等价于对麦克斯韦电动力学（Maxwell electrodynamics）中电荷的重新标度；热力学曲率（thermodynamic curvature）的发散点与热容（heat capacity）的零点一致，验证了相结构的一致性；高阶曲率修正和 quintessence 显著增大黑洞阴影尺寸，而电荷则减小阴影，且 quintessence 的影响比电荷更显著。

Conclusion: 暗能量和更高阶曲率修正能够在黑洞阴影中产生可观测的特征信号，为通过天文观测区分不同引力理论和暗能量模型提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: In this work, we derive an exact black hole solution in higher-order curvature gravity by coupling an electromagnetic sector formulated within the ModMax framework to a quintessence dark energy component. Focusing on purely electrically charged configurations, we analyze the thermodynamic and geothermodynamic properties of the solution to investigate its stability and phase structure. Within this sector, the ModMax theory effectively reduces Maxwell electrodynamics up to a rescaling of the electric charge, and thus the obtained solution corresponds to a consistent subset of the broader nonlinear theory. Using thermodynamic geometry, we examine microscopic interactions and phase transitions, showing that divergences in the thermodynamic curvature coincide with the vanishing of the heat capacity, confirming the consistency of the phase structure. We further explore the optical properties of the black hole by studying null geodesics and determining the photon sphere and the corresponding shadow radius for different values of the quintessence state parameter $ω$. Exact analytical expressions for the photon-sphere radius are derived, revealing that higher-order curvature corrections and quintessence significantly enhance the shadow size, whereas the electric charge has the opposite effect. Notably, quintessence is found to have a more pronounced impact on the shadow than the charge. These results highlight that dark energy and higher-order curvature corrections can yield potentially observable signatures in black hole shadows.

### [27] [No-go theorem for spontaneous vectorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13920)
*Hsu-Wen Chiang,Sebastian Garcia-Saenz,Aofei Sang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在广义矢量-张量引力理论中，初始无毛的黑洞无法通过自发的矢量化机制（spontaneous vectorization）生长出矢量毛发；若矢量场出现负有效质量平方，必然会伴随鬼（ghost）或不稳定性（gradient-type instabilities），从而对耦合常数施加约束，并发现 Kerr 黑洞在自转超过临界值时可能失稳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义矢量-张量引力理论（generalized vector-tensor theories of gravity）因允许有毛黑洞解而引起关注，从而规避了标准的无毛定理（no-hair theorems）。然而，这类黑洞如何从合理的初始条件形成仍是一个悬而未决的问题。

Method: 通过理论分析，考察了矢量场自发矢量化的可能性，即场因获得负有效质量平方（negative effective mass squared）而生长。利用稳定性分析，证明这种负有效质量平方的出现必然伴随鬼或梯度不稳定性。

Result: 如果初始态是无毛黑洞，则不可能实现矢量化。要求避免不稳定性可导出对耦合常数的有趣约束。特别地，Kerr 黑洞在自转超过某一临界值时可能变得不稳定。

Conclusion: 禁止鬼和梯度不稳定性为理论耦合常数给出了依赖于黑洞参数的界限；该结论适用于广义相对论中几乎所有稳态轴对称解。

Abstract: Generalized vector-tensor theories of gravity have drawn attention for admitting hairy black hole solutions, thereby circumventing the standard no-hair theorems. It remains an open question, however, how such black holes may form starting from reasonable initial conditions. It has been suggested that vector hair may grow spontaneously as a result of the field developing a negative effective mass squared $-$ the so-called spontaneous vectorization mechanism. We demonstrate that this is not possible if the initial state is a hairless black hole, a result that applies to essentially all stationary and axisymmetric solutions of interest in general relativity. More precisely, we prove that the appearance of a negative effective mass squared for the vector field must necessarily be accompanied by ghost- or gradient-type instabilities. Demanding the absence of such instabilities translates into interesting bounds on the coupling constants of the theory as functions of the black hole parameters. In particular, we discover that a Kerr black hole may become unstable when the spin increases above a certain critical value.

</details>

Method: 通过对近期报道的Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR)解实施退磁（demagnetizing）操作，构造得到一种新的Ricci平坦度规。

Result: 新度规是Kerr度规的形变，由参数B刻画；渐近区域变为纺锤形规则穹顶，而非渐近平坦；但仍可建立黑洞热力学第一定律，部分热力学关系与Kerr黑洞一致，仿佛B不存在。

Abstract: We construct a new Ricci-flat metric by demagnetizing the recently reported Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) solution. The metric is a deformation of the Kerr metric characterized by a parameter $B$, so that the asymptotic Kerr becomes a regular dome of spindle shape with north and south poles. Despite lacking an asymptotically-flat region, we find that the first law of black hole thermodynamics can be established. Some thermodynamic relations are identical to those of the Kerr black hole, as if the constant $B$ is absent. Our Ricci-flat rotating metric serves a neutral seed for a variety of inequivalent schemes of magnetizing the Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes.

### [29] [When Bumblebee Meets NLED: Lorentz-Violating Black Holes and Regular Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13963)
*Zhi-Chao Li,H. Lu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在熊蜂引力（bumblebee gravity）与非线性电动力学（NLED）耦合的框架下，利用辅助Maxwell-标量形式构造了带电黑洞解，并通过精细调节质量-电荷关系消除了中心奇点，得到了从AdS或dS核心插值到洛伦兹破缺真空的规则无视界时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在熊蜂引力与非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics, NLED）的耦合体系中构造带电黑洞解，并探索消除中心奇点的可能性。

Method: 采用辅助Maxwell-标量（auxiliary Maxwell-scalar）形式，对熊蜂矢量场施加径向构型模长固定条件，并引入严格的非最小熊蜂-NLED耦合。

Result: 得到了包含独立质量和电荷参数的一般黑洞解；中心奇异性有两个来源：Schwarzschild型极点与洛伦兹破缺真空的残余锥形奇点。通过精细调节质量-电荷关系可移除极点奇异性，得到边缘规则黑洞（marginally regular black holes）；在Born-Infeld理论等合适的NLED框架下，可同时移除两类奇点，代价是质量和电荷均需精细调节为耦合常数的特定函数。

Conclusion: 所得到的解描述了从反德西特（AdS）或德西特（dS）核心插值到洛伦兹破缺真空的规则无视界时空（regular horizonless spacetimes）。

Abstract: We construct charged black hole solutions in bumblebee gravity coupled to a general class of nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED) using an auxiliary Maxwell-scalar formalism. The norm-fixed radial configuration of the bumblebee vector makes the solutions asymptotic to a conical Lorentz-violating vacuum and requires stringent nonminimal bumblebee-NLED couplings. The general black hole solutions contain independent mass and charge parameters. There are two sources of singular behavior at the center: one is due to the Schwarzschild-type pole and the other is the residual conical singularity of the Lorentz-violating vacuum. By fine-tuning the mass-charge relation, one can generally remove the pole singularity, giving rise to marginally regular black holes. For a suitable NLED theory such as Born-Infeld theory, both singularity sources can be removed at the cost of requiring both the mass and the charge to be fine-tuned to specific functions of the coupling constants. The resulting solutions describe regular horizonless spacetimes interpolating from AdS or dS cores to Lorentz-violating vacua.

### [30] [Multipolar Proca stars: electric, magnetic and hybrid solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13965)
*Carlos Herdeiro,Eugen Radu,Etevaldo dos Santos Costa Filho,Nicolas Sanchis-Gual*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-普罗卡模型中构造了全新的、处处正则且渐近平坦的孤立子解（solitons），包括静态电型与磁型多极解以及两者的非线性混合解，并发现磁型和混合解在动力学演化中不稳定，会衰变至电型解或坍缩为黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索爱因斯坦-普罗卡（Einstein–Proca）模型中超越已知球形普罗卡星（Proca stars）的更多孤立子解，并研究其稳定性，从而理解该模型中自引力束缚态的结构多样性。

Method: 将平直时空中的奇异普罗卡多极子（Proca multipoles）以自引力（self-gravitating）方式延续至弯曲时空，构造静态轴对称解，并进一步通过电型与磁型多极子的非线性叠加构造混合解，随后对部分解进行动力学演化。

Result: 成功构造了电型（electric-type，含球形势垒星ℓ=0）和磁型（magnetic-type，起于ℓ=1，无球面对应物）两类静态轴对称解，以及具有非零局域角动量密度但总角动量为零的混合解（hybrid solutions）。动力学演化表明磁型和混合解不稳定，会衰变至电型中的长椭球式（prolate）或旋转式（spinning）普罗卡星，或坍缩为黑洞。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦-普罗卡模型中不仅存在球形和旋转的电型结构，还存在磁型及混合型孤立子解，但后两者在动力学上不稳定，最终倾向于演化为已知的、动力学稳健的电型解或黑洞。

Abstract: We construct new families of everywhere regular, asymptotically flat solitons in the Einstein--Proca model, obtained as self-gravitating continuations of flat-spacetime (singular) Proca multipoles. First we consider static and axially symmetric solutions, organized by a multipole number $\ell$. Two distinct classes arise: electric-type configurations, which include the spherical Proca stars as the $\ell=0$ case, and magnetic-type configurations, which have no spherical counterpart and start at $\ell=1$. Then we construct hybrid solutions as nonlinear superpositions of electric and magnetic multipoles. These have non-vanishing local angular momentum density but vanishing total angular momentum, and in some cases have no north-south $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetry. By performing dynamical evolutions of Proca stars in the new magnetic and hybrid sectors, we show they are unstable, decaying to the (static) prolate Proca stars or the (stationary) spinning Proca stars, previously identified as dynamically robust, electric sector configurations. In some cases, they can also collapse into a black hole.

</details>


### [31] [A No-Go Theorem for Topological Bridges with Matter-Vacuum Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14027)
*Rodrigo Maier*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，物质-真空耦合无法规避经典能量条件（如零能量条件NEC）对可穿越拓扑桥（虫洞）的限制；静态零潮汐力解必须违反NEC，真空不能“屏蔽”喉部几何，反而会因相互作用梯度阻碍所需几何。研究强化了经典能量条件的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可穿越拓扑桥（traversable topological bridges）传统上需要奇异物质（exotic matter）以违反零能量条件（Null Energy Condition, NEC）。本文旨在考察物质-真空耦合（matter-vacuum coupling）是否能绕过这一限制，从而无需引入奇异物质。

Method: 聚焦于零潮汐力（zero-tidal-force）解，针对静态构型（static configurations）建立一个严格的不可行定理（no-go theorem）。通过分析几何耀斑条件（geometric flare-out condition）与NEC合规源（NEC-compliant sources）之间的相容性，检验耦合参数Q和状态方程（equation of state）的影响。

Result: 物质-真空耦合无法绕过NEC违反的要求；几何耀斑条件与NEC合规源本质不相容，该结论与耦合参数Q或状态方程无关。真空不能屏蔽虫洞喉部（throat），相互作用梯度（interaction gradients）反而在数学上阻碍了所需几何的实现。

Conclusion: 因果保护（causality protection）内嵌于场方程（field equations）之中；真空的演化充当调节器（regulator）而非拓扑捷径（topological shortcuts）的促进者，从而强化了经典能量条件（classical energy conditions）的稳健性。

Abstract: Traversable topological bridges traditionally require exotic matter, violating the Null Energy Condition (NEC). This essay investigates whether matter-vacuum coupling can circumvent this necessity. Focusing on zero-tidal-force solutions, we establish a rigorous no-go theorem for static configurations, proving that such coupling cannot bypass the requirement for NEC violation. We demonstrate that the geometric flare-out condition is incompatible with NEC-compliant sources, regardless of the coupling $Q$ or equation of state. Crucially, the vacuum fails to shield the throat; instead, interaction gradients mathematically obstruct the required geometry. This result suggests that causality protection is inherent in the field equations, rendering the vacuum's evolution a regulator rather than a facilitator of topological shortcuts, thereby reinforcing the robustness of classical energy conditions.

</details>


### [32] [Reflecting Gravitons: The Graviton Laser and the Gertsenshtein effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14050)
*Thomas Forget,M. B. Paranjape,Urjit Yajnik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在实验室构建引力子激光器（graviton laser）的可行性。由于引力子无法被直接反射，过去仅在天体物理场景中被考虑。作者提出利用Gertsenshtein效应（引力子-光子转换），通过将引力子转换为光子、反射光子、再转换回引力子的方式，实现引力子在增益介质中的多次往返，从而在实验室中实现任意长的有效光程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去提出的引力子激光器方案因缺乏反射引力子的机制，在地球实验室环境中被认为不可行，仅在天体物理场景（如黑洞周围的引力子轨道）中仍存可能性。本文旨在探索一种可在实验室环境中实现的引力子激光器方案。

Method: 利用Gertsenshtein效应（Gertsenshtein effect），即引力子在外部磁场中转换为光子的过程。先通过该效应将引力子转化为光子，反射光子后再通过同一效应将光子重新转换为引力子，使其多次通过以超轻暗物质（ultra-light dark matter）为候选的引力子增益介质（lasing medium）。文中给出了三种可能的引力子增益系统示例。

Result: 通过设置对称的转换-反射装置，可以在增益介质两侧实现引力子的多次往返，从而将引力子通过增益介质的有效路径长度延长至任意长，为实验室构建引力子激光器提供了理论可能性。

Conclusion: 实验室构建引力子激光器在理论上并非不可行，Gertsenshtein效应提供了一种间接反射引力子的可行途径，使得引力子激光器在实验室场景中成为一个值得进一步研究的候选方案。

Abstract: Graviton lasers have been considered in the past, \cite{gl}, but practical terrestrial implementations appear infeasible. The absence of any known mechanism to reflect gravitons means that it remains unclear how a graviton beam could be directed repeatedly through a putative lasing medium. Astrophysical graviton lasing is still a possibilty as circular graviton orbits around blackholes afford the possibility of an arbitrarily long path length through the lasing medium of ultra-light dark matter \cite{bhgl,nhaxs}. In this essay, we consider the possibility of a graviton laser that could be constructed in a laboratory setting. The graviton lasing medium could be one of many possible gravitating systems, of which we give three possible examples. We calculate the possibility of reflecting the gravitons by using the conversion of gravitons into photons in an external magnetic field, the Gertsenshtein effect, \cite{Gertsenshtein1962}. We may convert the gravitons to photons, then reflect the photons, then reconvert the photons into gravitons via the same effect, and then pass them through the graviton lasing medium. With an identical apparatus on the other side, we can essentially extend the path length of the gravitons through the lasing medium as arbitrarily long as desired.

</details>


### [33] [Properties of natural polynomials for Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14078)
*Michelle Foucoin,Lionel London*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文综述了一类“自然”适用于黑洞拟正规模（quasi-normal modes）的多项式，这些多项式由拟正规模边界条件约束，能精确三对角化（tridiagonalize）Teukolsky径向方程。研究展示了其解析性质，包括三项递推关系、阶梯算子和微分方程，并证明Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞对应的多项式是带复参数的Pollaczek-Jacobi多项式。特别发现Schwarzschild情形中，三项递推关系在物理泛音指标（overtone index）处达到峰值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞拟正规模在引力波理论（gravitational wave theory）、信号建模和数据分析中具有重要作用，但其正交性与完备性等数学性质仍存在未解决的问题。经典多项式理论被提出作为研究框架，因此需要系统分析自然适用于拟正规模的多项式的解析性质，以更好地理解Teukolsky方程解的向量空间性质。

Method: 基于一类由拟正规模边界条件约束的多项式，将其应用于Teukolsky径向方程以实现精确三对角化。通过分析多项式的三项递推关系（3-term recurrence relation）、阶梯算子（ladder operators）和支配微分方程（governing differential equation），系统研究其解析性质，并识别Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞情形下的多项式类别。

Result: 证明了Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞的自然多项式属于带复参数（complex valued parameters）的Pollaczek-Jacobi多项式。在Schwarzschild情形中观察到一项新性质：多项式的三项递推关系总是在物理泛音指标处达到峰值。

Conclusion: 该工作支持了这些多项式在更广泛场景中的应用，并为其向Schwarzschild和Kerr之外的黑洞时空（black hole spacetimes）扩展奠定了基础。

Abstract: The quasi-normal modes of black holes play various important roles in gravitational wave theory, signal modeling, and data analysis; however, there remain open questions about their mathematical properties. Aspects of classical polynomial theory have been proposed as a framework to investigate quasinormal mode orthogonality and completeness. We have recently presented a class of polynomials that are "natural" to quasi-normal modes in that they are restricted by the quasi-normal mode boundary conditions, and exactly tridiagonalize Teukolsky's radial equation. In turn, these polynomials may be useful for better understanding the vector space properties of quasi-normal mode solutions to that equation. Here, we provide an overview of these polynomials' analytic properties: their 3-term recurrence relation, ladder operators and governing differential equation. We demonstrate that the natural polynomials for Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes are Pollaczek-Jacobi polynomials with complex valued parameters. Along the way, we observe a novel property that is particular to Schwarzschild: the polynomials' 3-term recurrence relation always peaks at the physical overtone index. This work supports the broader application of these polynomials, as well as their extension to black hole spacetimes beyond Schwarzschild and Kerr.

### [34] [On cosmological properties of black-hole hair in linearly coupled scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14132)
*Dražen Glavan,Darío Jaramillo-Garrido*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文研究了德西特时空中标量-高斯-博内引力理论的黑洞标量毛的超视界行为，发现毛既在时间上也在空间上增长，这种增长源于德西特时空中无质量标量场的动力学而非黑洞本身，且伴随稳态向外能流，说明测试场近似是瞬态的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在德西特（de Sitter）时空中，标量-高斯-博内（scalar-Gauss-Bonnet）理论的黑洞可以产生标量毛（scalar hair），但此前对其在超视界（superhorizon）尺度上的行为理解有限，尤其是这种毛是否稳定、是否与黑洞本身有关尚不清楚。

Method: 在线性耦合的平移对称标量-高斯-博内理论中，在测试场（test-field）近似下，解析研究了黑洞标量毛的超视界行为，并与德西特时空中无质量标量场的动力学进行对比；同时考察了点标量荷（point scalar charge）情形以及反作用（backreaction）的影响。

Result: 标量毛在超视界尺度上同时表现出时间增长和空间增长；这种增长并非黑洞特有，而是德西特时空中最小耦合无质量标量场的普遍动力学结果；点标量荷也呈现出类似行为；反作用首先出现在亚视界（subhorizon）尺度，且不能消除超视界轮廓；标量毛携带稳态向外能流，使测试场近似成为瞬态过程。

Conclusion: 德西特时空中黑洞标量毛的超视界增长来源于德西特时空的膨胀动力学，而非黑洞本身；标量化黑洞可被视为局域的亚视界标量扰动源；稳态能流的存在解释了为何自洽静态解的构造面临困难。

Abstract: We investigate the superhorizon behavior of scalar hair sourced by black holes in de Sitter spacetime in the linearly coupled shift-symmetric scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory. Working in the test-field regime, we show that this hair exhibits both temporal and spatial growth on superhorizon scales. This growth is not a special consequence of the black hole, but instead follows from the dynamics of a minimally coupled massless scalar field in expanding de Sitter spacetime. Moreover, it is not even specific to black holes, but also arises for a point scalar charge in de Sitter, indicating that a scalarized black hole acts effectively as a localized subhorizon source of scalar perturbations. Backreaction, when important, first arises on subhorizon scales and does not by itself eliminate the superhorizon profile. The time-dependent scalar hair also carries a steady outward energy flux, which frames the test-field regime as a transient, and helps explain the difficulties encountered in attempts to construct self-consistent static solutions.

Method: 采用f(R, G_{μν}T^{μν})引力模型（其中R为Ricci标量，G_{μν}为爱因斯坦张量，T^{μν}为能量-动量张量），在该形式下计算重子-熵比（baryon-to-entropy ratio, BnER）；随后将结果推广至广义GB情形。通过卡方（χ²）分析评估哈勃参数H(z)和距离模量μ(z)，并与ΛCDM范式进行比较。

Result: f(R, G_{μν}T^{μν})模型计算的BnER与观测限及估计的物质不平衡（matter imbalance）兼容；广义GB情形下的结果也与经验边界（empirical bounds）紧密吻合。χ²分析表明模型与CC及Pantheon+SH0ES数据集的当前宇宙学观测一致，且与ΛCDM范式具有令人满意的一致性。

Abstract: This work investigates the mechanism of gravitational baryogenesis (GB) under the formalism of f(R, G_{μν}T^{μν}) gravity, where R denotes the Ricci scalar, G_{μν} is the Einstein tensor and T^{μν} represents the energy--momentum tensor. f(R, G_{μν}T^{μν}) model is considered to evaluate the baryon-to-entropy ratio (BnER), which is subsequently compared against the observational limits. The results obtained exhibit compatibility with the estimated matter imbalance. Moreover, the analysis is extended to generalized GB case, resulting in outcomes that closely match empirical bounds. The findings reveal that the f(R, G_{μν}T^{μν}) formulation yields a viable theoretical setting for explaining the detected matter-antimatter disparity of the universe, highlighting its relevance in early cosmic evolution. To further validate the models, a chi-square (χ^2) analysis of the Hubble parameter, H(z), and distance modulus, μ(z), is performed, confirming their consistency with current cosmological observations. A comparative assessment simultaneously with the ΛCDM paradigm demonstrates a satisfactory level of agreement between the proposed model and cosmological observations from CC and Pantheon+SH0ES datasets.

### [36] [On the catastrophe time of fluids under the action of a gravitational field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14870)
*D. Astesiano,G. Ortenzi,M. L. Ruggiero*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文受Zel'dovich近似在天体结构形成中的核心作用启发，研究了球对称引力场中的Burgers型动力学。在牛顿框架下，通过拉格朗日映射（Lagrangian map）不可逆性条件，微扰推导了径向运动的灾变时间（catastrophe time），并发现微扰展开由无量纲参数α控制，而非局部引力加速度，因此即使在强引力下仍有效。随后将分析扩展到Schwarzschild时空中的径向测地线运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zel'dovich近似在描述引力塌缩导致的宇宙结构形成中扮演核心角色，这促使作者研究球对称引力场中的Burgers型动力学，以更好地理解灾变条件。

Method: 在牛顿引力框架下，通过拉格朗日映射（Lagrangian map）失去可逆性的条件，对径向运动进行微扰推导，得到灾变时间（catastrophe time）。分析表明微扰展开受控于无量纲参数α，而非局部引力加速度。随后将方法推广至Schwarzschild时空中的径向测地线运动。

Result: 微扰展开的控制参数是无量纲参数 α = μ / (r₀³ v₀(r₀)'²)，而非局部引力加速度，因此微扰展开即使在强引力条件下仍然有效。

Conclusion: 该研究为球对称引力场中Burgers型动力学的灾变描述提供了微扰框架，且发现该框架在强引力下依然适用，并可推广至广义相对论（general relativity）的Schwarzschild时空。

Abstract: Motivated by the central role of the Zel'dovich approximation in the description of cosmic structure formation through gravitational collapse, we investigate Burgers-type dynamics in a spherically symmetric gravitational field. In the Newtonian setting, we derive perturbatively the catastrophe time for radial motion by imposing the loss of invertibility of the Lagrangian map. We show that the perturbative expansion is controlled by the dimensionless parameter $
α=μ/{r_0^3 v_0(r_0)'^2}, $
rather than by the local gravitational acceleration alone. Hence, the expansion remain valid even when gravity is strong. We then extend the analysis to radial geodesic motion in Schwarzschild spacetime.

### [37] [Dyonic black holes supporting nearly-black self-gravitating thin shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14410)

Abstract: It has recently been revealed that dyonic black-hole spacetimes of a quasitopological non-linear electrodynamic field theory may be characterized by discrete radial regions with the property $dg_{tt}(r)/dr=0$ in which spherically symmetric massive {\it test} shells (Dyson shells with negligible self-gravity) can be supported in static equilibrium states. In the present paper we prove that the dyonic spacetimes of the non-linear electrodynamic field theory may also be characterized by the presence of radial regions with the dimensionless property $d[r\cdot g_{tt}(r)]/dr\to0^+$ in which massive {\it self-gravitating} thin shells that are on the verge of becoming black holes can be supported in static equilibrium states. Intriguingly, it is proved that the discrete radii of these self-gravitating nearly-black Dyson shells are universal in the sense that they are independent of the masses of the central supporting dyonic compact objects.
