### [38] [Energy conditions in consistent perfect fluid cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14479)
*Davide Batic,Christian G. Boehmer,Denys Dutykh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Brown变分原理，在$f(R,T)=R+\sigma R T$引力模型中研究平FLRW宇宙的宇宙学，将场方程改写为类爱因斯坦形式，导出有效能量密度、压强和状态方程参数，并通过能量条件分析揭示：辐射情形还原标准相对论宇宙学，而尘埃情形（$\sigma>0$）可产生负压驱动加速膨胀；同时给出了能量条件成立的多项式不等式和参数约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受$f(R,T)$引力中一致流体耦合的最新工作启发，旨在利用Brown变分原理系统地研究非平凡模型$f(R,T)=R+\sigma R T$的宇宙学行为，并借助能量条件（energy conditions）分析该模型的物理可行性。

Method: 采用Brown变分原理处理正压理想流体（barotropic perfect fluid）；在平FLRW度规下将场方程改写为类爱因斯坦（Einstein-like）形式，导出有效能量密度、有效压强和状态方程（equation of state, EOS）参数；将零、弱、强、主能量条件转化为简单多项式不等式进行定性分析。

Result: 辐射情形完全还原标准相对论宇宙学；尘埃情形且$\sigma>0$时有效流体获得负压，可驱动加速膨胀。在尘埃情形下，存在一个有限的哈勃参数窗口，其中强能量条件（strong energy condition）被违反，而零、弱、主能量条件仍然满足；反之，若强能量条件成立，其余条件自动满足。额外可行性条件$1+\sigma T>0$进一步限制哈勃范围并对$\sigma$给出上界，但依然保留非空的加速区域。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种基于定性技术的透明能量条件分析，系统地刻画了$f(R,T)$宇宙学中一致$R\,T$耦合的物理约束与加速膨胀条件。

Abstract: Motivated by recent work on consistent fluid couplings in $f(R, T)$ gravity, we study cosmology in the nontrivial model $f(R, T) = R + σR T$ using the Brown variational principle for a barotropic perfect fluid. For a flat FLRW universe, we cast the field equations into Einstein-like form and obtain explicit expressions for the effective energy density, pressure and equation of state (EOS) parameter. This allows us to rewrite the null, weak, strong and dominant energy conditions as simple polynomial inequalities. We show that radiation reproduces standard relativistic cosmology, whereas for dust and $σ>0$ the effective fluid acquires negative pressure and can drive accelerated expansion. In this dust case, there exists a finite window in the Hubble parameter during which the strong energy condition is violated, but the null, weak, and dominant energy conditions remain satisfied. Conversely, whenever the strong energy condition is imposed, the other conditions are automatically fulfilled. The additional viability requirement $1 + σT > 0$ further restricts the allowed Hubble range and yields an upper bound on $σ$ that still leaves a non-empty accelerating regime. Our analysis provides a transparent energy-condition study of a consistent $R\, T$ coupling in $f(R, T)$ cosmology, based on qualitative techniques.

</details>


### [39] [Quasinormal modes of massless scalar and electromagnetic perturbations for Euler Heisenberg black holes surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14528)
*Chengfu Feng,Sheng-Yuan Li,Xufen Zhang,Ming Zhang,De-Cheng Zou,Rui-Hong Yue*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了带电欧拉-海森伯格黑洞在完美流体暗物质环境中的标量和电磁扰动的拟正规模（quasinormal modes），采用渐近迭代法和六阶WKB近似计算拟正规频率，并分析了灰体因子（greybody factors）。发现黑洞电荷、非线性电动力学参数、暗物质参数和角量子数显著改变有效势垒结构，从而影响振荡频率、衰减率以及波的传输与反射特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解非线性电动力学效应和暗物质共同作用下黑洞扰动动力学行为，填补带电欧拉-海森伯格黑洞在暗物质背景中拟正规模和灰体因子研究的空白。

Method: 采用渐近迭代法（asymptotic iteration method）和六阶WKB近似（sixth-order WKB approximation）计算拟正规频率，并通过两种方法的相对偏差（relative deviation）定量验证结果可靠性；灰体因子在六阶WKB框架内评估。

Result: 黑洞电荷 $Q$、非线性电动力学参数 $a$、暗物质参数 $\lambda$ 和角量子数 $l$ 均显著改变有效势垒（effective potential barrier）结构，进而影响振荡频率、阻尼率以及波的传输与反射特性。

Conclusion: 验证了两种计算方法的一致性，揭示了多个参数对拟正规模和灰体因子的调控机制，为非线性电动力学与暗物质环境下的黑洞扰动研究提供了定量依据。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes of massless scalar and electromagnetic perturbations in charged Euler--Heisenberg black holes surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter. The quasinormal frequencies are calculated using the asymptotic iteration method and the sixth-order WKB approximation, and the relative deviation between the two methods is quantitatively analyzed to verify the reliability of results. The greybody factors for both perturbations are also evaluated within the sixth-order WKB framework. We systematically examine the effects of the black hole charge $Q$, nonlinear electrodynamic parameter $a$, dark matter parameter $λ$, and angular quantum number $l$ on the quasinormal frequencies and greybody factors. We find that these parameters significantly modify the structure of the effective potential barriers, and thus affect the oscillation frequencies, damping rates, and wave transmission and reflection properties of the perturbed fields.

</details>


### [40] [Consistency in the Quantum-Improved Charged Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14532)
*Chiang-Mei Chen,Akihiro Ishibashi,Nobuyoshi Ohta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有尺度依赖耦合（scale-dependent couplings）的量子改良带电黑洞在热力学与方程/作用量层面的一致性，发现牛顿耦合与电磁耦合可任意依赖于径向坐标，揭示了化学势中的微妙问题，并指出量子改良需要在爱因斯坦方程中引入额外的量子能量-动量张量（quantum energy-momentum tensor）。研究还表明，方程与作用量层面的一致性要求牛顿耦合满足特定条件，且量子诱导修正可推动早期宇宙的各向同性化（isotropization）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子改良带电黑洞（quantum-improved charged black holes）中，尺度依赖耦合会导致热力学及引力场方程出现潜在的不一致性。本文旨在系统检查这些不一致性，并澄清方程层面与作用量层面（action level）方法之间是否兼容。

Method: 以量子改良的Reissner-Nordström黑洞（Reissner-Nordström black holes）为具体模型，分别在热力学与场方程/作用量层面上进行分析，并结合比安基恒等式（Bianchi identity）检验爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）的兼容性，最后将分析推广到宇宙学解（cosmological solutions）。

Result: 热力学一致性允许牛顿耦合（Newton coupling）与电磁耦合（electromagnetic coupling）任意依赖于径向坐标；发现了尺度依赖电磁耦合下化学势（chemical potential）的微妙问题。方程与作用量层面的一致性要求牛顿耦合满足特定性质，且需要引入额外的量子能量-动量张量。量子诱导修正可驱动早期宇宙的各向同性化。

Conclusion: 量子改良的带电黑洞在热力学与场方程层面存在一致性条件，这些条件对耦合函数形式及量子修正项提出了具体要求；同时，这种修正机制在宇宙学层面具有潜在的应用价值。

Abstract: We investigate the consistency in the thermodynamics and the approaches at the equation and action levels for the quantum-improved charged black holes with scale-dependent couplings. For the quantum-improved Reissner-Nordström black holes, we find that the thermodynamic consistency allows both the Newton and electromagnetic couplings to have arbitrary dependence on the radial coordinate. We point out a subtlety in the chemical potential with the scale-dependent electromagnetic coupling in the study of thermodynamics. We also examine the compatibility of the Einstein equations at the equation and action levels with the Bianchi identity, identifying the need for an additional quantum energy-momentum tensor. We then find that the consistency between the approaches at the equation and action levels requires that the Newton coupling satisfy certain property. Finally, we extend the analysis to cosmological solutions, suggesting that quantum-induced modifications can drive the isotropization of the early universe.

Result: 宇宙学参数（cosmological parameters）的演化分析揭示了模型的行为特征。表观视界形式（apparent horizon formalism）下的热力学分析表明，熵演化（entropy evolution）在整个宇宙演化过程中保持物理自洽。

The modified gravitational action depends explicitly on the Ricci scalar \( \mathcal{R} \), the matter-coupling scalar \( Σ\), and the trace of the energy--momentum tensor \( \mathcal{T} \), which collectively generate significant corrections to the standard cosmological evolution. The particle creation mechanism is introduced through an open thermodynamic description of the Universe. In addition, the dark sector is modeled using the variable generalized Chaplygin gas formalism. To examine the observational consistency of the model, the free parameters are constrained using the Pantheon\(^+\) Type Ia Supernova compilation together with the combined observational Hubble and Pantheon\(^+\) datasets through a statistical \(χ^2\)-analysis. The cosmological behavior of the model is further explored through the evolution of the cosmological parameters. Furthermore, the thermodynamic properties of the model are investigated using the apparent horizon formalism. The obtained results demonstrate that the entropy evolution remains physically consistent throughout the cosmic evolution. Hence, the present \( \mathcal{F}(\mathcal{R},Σ,\mathcal{T}) \) gravity framework with particle creation provides a viable geometrical description of the late-time accelerated Universe and remains compatible with recent cosmological observations.

### [42] [Modifications of CMB Temperature and Polarization Quadrupole Signals in Thurston Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14572)
*Tanay Gupta,Sukanta Panda,Rajib Saha*

Method: 以瑟斯顿时空（Thurston spacetimes）作为背景模型，建立相应的转移方程（transfer equations）并针对每种时空几何求解；利用斯托克斯参数P、Q、U、V刻画温度与偏振振幅在不同时间戳下的演化，并尝试孤立识别各瑟斯顿几何。

Result: 展示了温度与偏振振幅在不同时间戳下随斯托克斯参数的演化模式，初步揭示了不同瑟斯顿几何产生的CMB信号特征，并分析了空间曲率（spatial curvature）在这些FLRW极限模型中的作用与底层几何的对称性。

Conclusion: 各向异性瑟斯顿几何能够在CMB中产生可区分的温度与偏振信号，空间曲率对FLRW极限模型有重要影响；基于斯托克斯参数的时间演化模式有助于识别不同的瑟斯顿几何类型。

Abstract: Recent cosmological tests have discovered a fresh new set of anomalies in the large-scale isotropy of the universe. Motivated thus by the numerous pieces of evidence for large-scale cosmic isotropy violation with the advent of the 'precision cosmology' era, we are led to explore the viability of anisotropic Thurston geometries, described in William Thurston's geometrization conjecture. In this work, we examine the coherent temperature and polarization signals generated in the CMB sky by such geometries. We begin with introducing Thurston spacetimes as our background model and the formalism we use to obtain the patterns. We then construct a set of transfer equations relative to a given background and solve them for each spacetime geometry. We finally discuss the role of spatial curvature in these FLRW limiting models along with their underlying geometry, and attempt to establish some general results on the symmetries of the patterns produced by their time evolution in terms of the Stokes parameters P, Q, U and V. We show the evolution of temperature and polarization amplitudes in terms of such Stokes parameters at different timestamps and attempt to isolate individual Thurston geometries.

### [43] [Parametrization of the primordial power spectrum in loop quantum cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14657)
*Almudena Guillén,Kai Langer,Guillermo A. Mena Marugán,Niklas Rodenbücher,Antonio Vicente-Becerril*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过混合（hybrid）和表观度量（dressed metric）两种圈量子宇宙学（loop quantum cosmology）方法，研究了暴胀前反弹相（pre-inflationary bounce phase）对宇宙学扰动角功率谱（angular power spectra）的影响，提出了一种新的原初功率谱参数化方案，并在约140个e-fold宇宙膨胀下，发现两种方法与Planck数据在高多极（high multipoles）处高度一致，且在低多极（low multipoles）处对ΛCDM模型有所改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准宇宙学模型未考虑量子引力效应，而圈量子宇宙学中的暴胀前反弹相可能在大尺度结构上留下可观测印记，但目前缺乏对原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）的精确参数化描述。

Method: 提出一种新的原初功率谱参数化方案，该方案除包含标准慢滚参数（slow-roll coefficients）和宇宙学参数外，额外依赖暴胀期前的反弹阶段e-fold数和特征抑制尺度（suppression scale）；采用NO-AHD真空态选择方案以避免振荡性原初功率谱；基于混合与表观度量两种方法计算角功率谱并与Planck数据比较。

Result: 反弹相e-fold数和由反弹能量密度（依赖于Immirzi参数和面积差（area gap））决定的抑制尺度共同决定了参数化形式；两种方法得到的张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）在观测尺度未远小于功率抑制区域时与标准ΛCDM一致；约140个e-fold下，两种方法与Planck数据在高多极吻合良好，在低多极处对ΛCDM拟合有所改善。

Conclusion: 该参数化方案为圈量子宇宙学暴胀前反弹相的观测检验提供了鲁棒且准确的工具；混合与表观度量两种方法均有望通过宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测数据对ΛCDM模型在低多极区域进行修正。

Abstract: We investigate the imprints on the angular power spectra of cosmological perturbations of a pre-inflationary bounce phase, as described by the hybrid and dressed metric approaches to loop quantum cosmology. For this purpose, we derive a new parametrization of the primordial power spectrum at the end of the inflationary regime. Apart from slow-roll coefficients and cosmological parameters that are present in the standard cosmological scenario without quantum modifications, this parametrization additionally depends only on pre-inflationary physics. More specifically, we find a dependence on the number of e-folds during the bounce epoch and on a characteristic suppression scale which, given the e-folds accumulated during cosmic evolution, is determined by the energy density at the bounce. Recall that this density depends on the Immirzi parameter and the area gap known from LQG. This leads to a robust and accurate parametrization of the primordial power spectrum. Since in pre-inflationary scenarios there is no preferred vacuum state, we adopt the NO-AHD proposal, which selects a vacuum that is optimally adapted to the background dynamics and yields a non-oscillatory primordial power spectrum. With this choice, we show that the tensor-to-scalar ratio in both quantization approaches coincides with its expression in the standard $Λ$CDM model when the observed scales are not much smaller than the power-suppressed region. Computing also the angular power spectrum, we find that, for a total cosmic expansion of about 140 e-folds, both the hybrid and the dressed metric approaches exhibit excellent agreement with Planck data at high multipoles, while apparently improving the fit with respect to $Λ$CDM for low multipole numbers.

### [44] [Static spherically symmetric Kundt vacuum solutions of higher-derivative gravities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14658)
*Breno L. Giacchini,Ivan Kolář,Vojtěch Pravda,Alena Pravdová*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了二次引力（quadratic gravity）和六阶导数引力（six-derivative gravity）中静态球对称Kundt真空解，分析了曲率奇点（curvature singularities）及其对测地观测者的可达性，并在此基础上构造了精确引力波解，发现高阶引力在某些耦合常数取值下允许全局光滑的引力波解，而爱因斯坦引力中的Nariai背景引力波则不可避免地包含奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高阶导数引力理论（higher-derivative gravity）中静态球对称Kundt真空解的完整分类，并研究其上的引力波解是否存在全局光滑（globally smooth）形式，以对比爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）中Nariai背景引力波必然含有奇点的已知结论。

Method: 在二次引力中，分别处理耦合常数满足${α\neq3β}$和${α=3β}$两种情况：前者直接识别所有解，后者采用 Frobenius 方法（Frobenius method）推导幂级数递推关系。在六阶导数引力中，选取特定模型展示闭式解（closed-form solutions）的多样性，并分析可能的 Frobenius 解指标族（indicial families）。

Result: 在二次引力中，完成了耦合常数不同取值下的解分类；在六阶导数引力中，展示了多种闭式解及Frobenius解指标族。对于所有解，均分析了曲率奇点及其对测地线观测者（geodesic observers）的可达性。在高阶引力中，对于适当的耦合常数值，引力波可以具有全局光滑解，而爱因斯坦引力中的Nariai背景引力波则必然包含奇点。

Conclusion: 高阶导数引力（higher-order gravities）能够在适当的耦合常数取值下提供全局光滑的引力波解，这与爱因斯坦引力中Nariai背景引力波必然包含奇点的情形形成对比，表明高阶引力在消除背景引力波奇点方面具有优势。

Abstract: We study static spherically symmetric Kundt solutions to the vacuum field equations of quadratic gravity with a cosmological constant, as well as specific models of six-derivative gravity. In quadratic gravity, we identify all solutions for coupling constants satisfying ${α\neq3β}$, while the case ${α=3β}$ is studied using the Frobenius method, where we derive the recurrence relations for the power series. In contrast, in six-derivative gravity, we focus on selected models to illustrate the variety of closed-form solutions; we also analyze possible indicial families of Frobenius solutions. For all solutions, we analyze curvature singularities and their accessibility to geodesic observers.
  We then construct exact gravitational-wave solutions propagating on some of these backgrounds in quadratic and six-derivative gravity. It is known that in Einstein gravity, gravitational waves on the Nariai background unavoidably contain singularities, which are interpreted as physical sources generating these gravitational waves. In contrast, in addition to singular solutions, for appropriate values of the coupling constants, higher-order gravities allow for globally smooth solutions representing gravitational waves.

### [45] [Black holes and neutron stars in massive Hellings-Nordtvedt theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14711)
*Zhe Luo,Liang Liang,Zhong-Xi Yu,Hong-Da Lyu,Shoulong Li,Hongwei Yu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了有质量Hellings-Nordtvedt矢量-张量引力理论中两种非最小耦合项（A²R和A^μA^νR_μν）对渐近真空结构的影响，发现只有单一耦合扇区（如A²R或A^μA^νR_μν）才能实现渐近平直真空，并进一步分析了A²R扇区的中子星解和太阳系约束，证明该扇区在弱场与强场下均具有自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期已知A^μA^νR_μν扇区在非零矢量真空（nonzero vector vacuum）下可产生类单极子（monopole-like）渐近真空结构，但该结构是否依赖于特殊的Ricci张量耦合（Ricci-tensor coupling）尚不明确。本文旨在检验这一结构是否具有普适性，并探索A²R扇区在强场致密天体中的可行性。

Method: 通过分析场方程在空间无穷远处的渐近行为，推导渐近真空条件（asymptotic vacuum condition），并系统考察两种耦合系数同时非零时的兼容性；进一步计算Noether质量（Noether mass），推导太阳系约束，并数值构造中子星（neutron-star）构型。

Result: 渐近真空条件排斥两种耦合系数同时非零的情形，仅允许两个单一耦合扇区。A^μA^νR_μν扇区复现已知的类单极子渐近结构；A²R扇区则允许一个渐近平直的Schwarzschild度规（Schwarzschild metric）伴随非平凡径向矢量场。在中子星中，A²R扇区在质量、半径和转动惯量上可显著偏离广义相对论（general relativity）及Ricci张量耦合扇区，尽管弱场偏差被约束在很小范围内。

Conclusion: A²R扇区是质量Hellings-Nordtvedt理论中一个自洽且可行的框架，可用于研究具有非零矢量真空的强场致密天体，同时与弱场实验检验保持良好的兼容性。

Abstract: Hellings-Nordtvedt theory is a vector-tensor theory in which a vector field $A_μ$ is nonminimally coupled to curvature through two independent interactions $A^2{\cal R}$ and $A^μA^ν{\cal R}_{μν}$. When supplemented by a potential whose zero-energy minimum occurs at nonzero $A^2$, the restricted $A^μA^ν{\cal R}_{μν}$ sector is known to admit black-hole and neutron-star solutions with a monopole-like asymptotic vacuum structure. We examine whether this structure is a generic consequence of the nonzero vector vacuum or instead relies on the special Ricci-tensor coupling. By analyzing the field equations near spatial infinity, we show that the asymptotic vacuum condition is incompatible with generic nonzero values of both couplings and instead selects two allowed single-coupling sectors. The $A^μA^ν{\cal R}_{μν}$ sector reproduces the known monopole-like asymptotics, whereas the $A^2{\cal R}$ sector admits an asymptotically flat Schwarzschild metric with a nontrivial radial vector field. We further compute the Noether mass in the $A^2{\cal R}$ sector, derive the corresponding Solar-System constraints, and construct neutron-star configurations. Although the weak-field deviation is constrained to be small, neutron stars can still show appreciable departures from both general relativity and the Ricci-tensor-coupling sector in their masses, radii, and moments of inertia. Our results identify that the $A^2{\cal R}$ sector of massive Hellings-Nordtvedt theory as a viable and useful framework for studying strong-field compact objects with a nonzero vector vacuum while remaining compatible with weak-field tests.

</details>


### [46] [Wide parameter-space O3 search for continuous gravitational waves from unknown neutron stars in binary systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14728)
*P. B. Covas,M. A. Papa,R. Prix*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文报告了对来自未知双星系统的连续引力波（continuous gravitational waves）的首次大范围参数空间搜索，覆盖50–1000 Hz频率和低于3天的轨道周期，未探测到信号但给出了迄今最严格的振幅上限约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续引力波信号来自非对称旋转中子星，但长期未被探测到；双星吸积（binary accretion）是产生所需非对称性的自然机制，且已知自旋高于25 Hz的脉冲星约一半属于双星系统，因此搜索来自未知双星系统的连续引力波至关重要，但计算上最具挑战性。

Method: 该搜索首次覆盖引力波频率从50到1000 Hz（高于之前的520 Hz上限），并首次使用先进探测器探索低于3天的轨道周期，从而填补了此前未探测的大范围参数空间区域。

Result: 未探测到任何信号；在95%置信水平下，排除距离100 pc以内、自旋速度高于约495 Hz的中子星具有高于5.2×10⁻⁸的椭率（ellipticity）；同样距离内，排除自旋速度高于约740 Hz的中子星的r模振幅（r-mode amplitude）高于1.5×10⁻⁶。

Conclusion: 该研究给出了迄今对这类信号振幅最严格的约束，显著缩小了连续引力波的理论允许参数空间。

Abstract: Continuous gravitational waves, i.e., persistent and nearly-monochromatic signals emitted by asymmetric spinning neutron stars, remain elusive. Searches for these signals from unknown binary systems are the most computationally challenging, but they are essential, given that binary accretion provides a natural mechanism for creating the required asymmetry, and around half of the known pulsars rotating above 25 Hz are part of a binary system. Here we report on a search of a large uncharted parameter-space region: for the first time we cover gravitational-wave frequencies above 520 Hz (from 50 to 1000 Hz), and, for the first time with advanced detectors, orbital periods lower than 3 days are explored. No signal is detected, and we set the most stringent constraints to date on the amplitude of signals of this kind. Our results exclude with $95\%$ confidence neutron stars within 100 pc and rotating faster than $\sim$ 495 Hz from having ellipticities above $5.2 \times 10^{-8}$. Within the same distance our results also exclude r-mode amplitudes above $1.5 \times 10^{-6}$ for stars rotating faster than $\sim$ 740 Hz.

</details>


### [47] [Regularized vacuum stress tensor of a scalar field as the inflaton or dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14729)
*Xuan Ye*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究最大对称时空中标量场的正则化真空应力张量（regularized vacuum stress tensor），通过分析弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equation）解的存在性，评估驱动暴胀（inflation）或当前宇宙加速膨胀（cosmic acceleration）的可行性。研究发现，质量约为10倍普朗克质量（$M_{\text{pl}}$）的共形耦合标量场（conformally coupled scalar field）可同时作为暴胀子（inflaton）和暗能量（dark energy）的候选者，暗示两者可能具有相同的量子起源；而最小耦合标量场（minimally coupled scalar field）则无论质量如何均无法扮演上述角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索标量场的量子真空效应是否能够驱动早期宇宙暴胀和当前宇宙加速膨胀，并检验暴胀与暗能量是否可能共享同一量子起源。

Method: 计算最大对称时空中标量场的正则化真空应力张量，并通过分析弗里德曼方程解的存在性来评估不同耦合类型（共形耦合与最小耦合）及不同质量的标量场能否驱动宇宙加速膨胀。

Result: 质量约为10倍普朗克质量的共形耦合标量场可以同时作为暴胀子和暗能量的候选者；而最小耦合标量场无论质量大小，均不能作为暴胀子或暗能量。

Conclusion: 暴胀与暗能量可能具有共同的量子起源，即来自共形耦合标量场的真空量子涨落；但该机制对耦合形式有严格限制，最小耦合标量场不适用。

Abstract: We study the regularized vacuum stress tensor of scalar fields in maximally symmetric spacetime and assess the feasibility of driving primordial inflation or current cosmic acceleration by analyzing the existence of solutions to the Friedmann equation. We find that a conformally coupled scalar field with mass of order $10$ $M_{\text{pl}}$ can be a candidate for both the inflaton and dark energy, suggesting that these two components may have the same quantum origin. In contrast, a minimally coupled scalar field cannot serve as either the inflaton or dark energy regardless of its mass.

*Panagiotis Dorlis,Nick E. Mavromatos,Sarben Sarkar,Sotirios-Neilos Vlachos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出，旋转黑洞周围的超辐射轴子类粒子云可产生含10⁶–10⁷个关联量子的多模压缩引力子态，这些态的极化关联与量子噪声特征可被未来引力波干涉仪探测到，从而直接验证引力辐射的量子性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力（quantum gravity）难以直接探测，因为其可观效应被普朗克能标（Planck scale）的幂次压制；单引力子（graviton）的直接探测被普遍认为不可能。作者希望找到一种天体物理机制来克服这一压制。

Method: 提出旋转黑洞周围的超辐射（superradiant）轴子类粒子（axion-like-particle）云可作为天体物理机制，产生包含10⁶–10⁷个关联量子的多模压缩态（multimode squeezed states）引力子。

Result: 这些多模压缩引力子态拥有独特的极化关联（polarization correlations）与量子噪声（quantum-noise）特征，有望在未来引力波干涉仪（gravitational-wave interferometer）中被探测到。

Conclusion: 若上述特征被观测到，将构成引力辐射具有量子本质的直接证据；若未被探测到，则可对轴子云寿命施加约束。该方案亦可检验作为有效场论（effective field theory）的广义相对论（General Relativity）。

Abstract: Quantum Gravity remains elusive, largely because its observable effects are suppressed by powers of the Planck scale. Direct detection of single gravitons is widely believed to be impossible. Here we propose a concrete astrophysical mechanism that may overcome this suppression. We show that superradiant axion-like-particle clouds surrounding rotating black holes can generate multimode squeezed states of gravitons containing up to $10^6$ - $10^7$ correlated quanta. Such states exhibit distinctive polarization correlations and quantum-noise signatures that could be detectable in future gravitational-wave interferometers. Observation of these signatures would constitute direct evidence for the quantum nature of gravitational radiation. Conversely, their absence can place constraints on axion-cloud lifetimes. Our approach also provides a test of General Relativity as an effective field theory.

### [49] [The sufficiently trapped surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14798)
*Eleni-Alexandra Kontou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了“充分捕获面（sufficiently trapped surface）”的概念，以推广传统“捕获面（trapped surface）”在量子场论或半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）等弱能量条件下的应用，并恢复了奇点定理和面积定理的核心结论，同时继续支持弱宇宙审查猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统捕获面（trapped surface）在满足零能量条件（null convergence condition）时能导出零测地线不完备性（null geodesic incompleteness）并支持弱宇宙审查猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）；但在半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）等违反零能量条件的情形下，捕获面失去了这些保障。因此需要一种更广义的概念来适应更弱的能量条件。

Method: 本文引入“充分捕获面（sufficiently trapped surface）”这一推广概念，使其能够在量子场（quantum fields）相关的更弱能量条件下依然成立，并重新推导奇点定理（singularity theorem）和面积定理（area theorem）中的关键作用。

Result: 充分捕获面（sufficiently trapped surface）在违反零能量条件（null convergence condition）时，仍能恢复奇点定理和面积定理中的关键作用，并继续支持弱宇宙审查猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）。

Conclusion: 广义的捕获面概念为半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）等弱能量条件下的引力理论提供了统一的几何框架，保留了对奇点形成和黑洞面积增长的预言能力，并维持了对弱宇宙审查猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）的支持。

Abstract: Roger Penrose introduced the concept of the trapped surface: a spacelike hypersurface where the two null normals have negative expansion. The trapped surface along with the null convergence condition leads to null geodesic incompleteness. If an event horizon forms, the trapped surface is also always behind it, providing evidence for the weak cosmic censorship conjecture. When the null convergence condition is violated, as in the case of semiclassical gravity, trapped surfaces lose these guarantees. A generalized notion, the sufficiently trapped surface, accommodates weaker energy conditions consistent with quantum fields. This concept restores key roles in singularity and area theorems and continues to support the weak cosmic censorship conjecture.

### [50] [Gravitational Wave Propagation through Viscous Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14956)

TL;DR: 本文研究了引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）在粘性介质中传播时的能量转移机制，发现在弯曲时空背景（如史瓦西时空）下，阻尼效应和流体加热显著增强，可能导致引力波大幅衰减乃至产生伽马射线暴（gamma-ray bursts），并在核心坍缩超新星、双中子星并合及双黑洞并合吸积等天体物理场景中具有潜在重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知引力波在粘性物质中传播时会转移能量，但效应通常太弱而缺乏天体物理意义。作者前期工作发现，当物质与源的距离小于引力波波长时，相互作用可能变得重要。本文旨在将这一分析推广到更真实的背景时空（史瓦西时空和静态球对称背景），以评估引力波阻尼及相关加热效应在实际天体物理环境中的可观测后果。

Method: 作者采用闵可夫斯基背景下的线性化微扰（linearized perturbations）方法，将其推广到史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）和静态球对称（static spherically symmetric）背景中，分析引力波在粘性流体中的传播与耗散行为。

Result: 在更真实的弯曲时空背景下，引力波阻尼及粘性流体的加热效应显著增强，可能导致引力波大幅衰减，甚至引发伽马射线暴。

Conclusion: 上述增强效应可能在多种天体物理场景中发挥作用，包括核心坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae）、双中子星并合（binary neutron star mergers）以及双黑洞并合过程中的吸积（accretion onto binary black hole mergers）。

Abstract: It has been known that gravitational waves (GWs) transfer energy to viscous matter through which they propagate, but the effect is too weak to be astrophysically significant. Using linearized perturbations about a Minkowski background, we previously showed that the interaction can become important when the distance between matter and source is smaller than the GW wavelength. Here, we review extensions to more realistic backgrounds, namely Schwarzschild spacetime and a static spherically symmetric setting. We find that GW damping and the associated heating of the viscous fluid are enhanced, and can lead to substantial attenuation or even gamma-ray bursts. We investigate astrophysical scenarios where these effects may be relevant, including core-collapse supernovae, binary neutron star mergers, and accretion onto binary black hole mergers.

### [51] [Conservative and dissipative sectors in a nonlinear scalar model for the gravitational self-force problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14958)
*Francisco M. Blanco,Eanna E. Flanagan,Abraham I. Harte*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文以非线性标量场（nonlinear scalar field）为玩具模型，研究引力自力（gravitational self-force）中保守分量（conservative component）与耗散分量（dissipative component）的分解。一阶分解唯一确定，但高阶分解存在多种可能性。通过要求保守部分满足哈密顿性（Hamiltonian），本文提出了多种保守二阶自力（conservative second-order self-force）的定义，并讨论了相关性质与哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相互作用（self-interaction）对物体运动的影响可通过将自力分解为保守和耗散部分来理解。作为引力自力的简化玩具模型，本文旨在探讨在高阶情形下这种分解的多种可能性及其判据差异。

Method: 采用非线性标量场耦合模型，假定存在具有特定性质的三点函数（three-point function）作为 Detweiler-Whiting 两点函数（Detweiler-Whiting two-point function）的推广。通过要求保守部分具有哈密顿结构，识别多种可能的保守二阶自力定义。

Result: 一阶标量自力的保守-耗散分解标准唯一；但高阶情形下不同判据不再等价，导致多种保守二阶自力的定义。结果适用于两体问题（two-body problem），但由于红外发散（infrared divergence），仅限于非束缚散射轨道（unbound scattering trajectories）。

Conclusion: 对于引力自力的保守-耗散分解，高阶情形下不存在唯一分解方式；通过施加哈密顿性要求可获得多种候选定义，相关哈密顿量已导出。这些结果对理解两体问题中高阶自力分解具有参考意义。

Abstract: When considering how self-interaction affects an object's motion, it can be convenient to decompose the self-force into conservative and dissipative pieces. As a toy model for understanding such decompositions of the gravitational self-force, we consider objects that do not affect the spacetime, but are instead coupled to a nonlinear scalar field. There is then a standard splitting of the first-order scalar self-force into conservative and dissipative components. Multiple criteria can be used to obtain this splitting, all of which imply the same result. However, the implications of these criteria generically differ at higher orders. Demanding that any reasonable conservative sector be Hamiltonian, we identify multiple possible definitions of the conservative second-order self-force. Motivations for these possibilities and their properties are discussed and relevant Hamiltonians are obtained. We assume the existence of a three-point function with certain properties that is a generalization of the Detweiler-Whiting two-point function. These results apply to the two-body problem but are restricted to unbound scattering trajectories, due to infrared divergences that arise for bound orbits.

### [52] [Exploring the CMB in Anisotropic Universes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14970)
*Robbert W. Scholtens,Marcello Seri,Holger Waalkens,Rien van de Weygaert*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文放弃宇宙学原理中的各向同性假设，仅保留空间均匀性，在Bianchi模型框架下构建各向异性宇宙学模型，推导弗里德曼方程的扰动方程，并通过Bianchi V型示例模拟了宇宙微波背景（CMB）辐射及其功率谱，旨在描述各向异性宇宙模型的信号特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来超新星和宇宙整体流（cosmic bulk flow）等观测对宇宙学原理（cosmological principle）提出了挑战，学界对其适用范围产生疑虑，因此需要更全面地理解不满足宇宙学原理的宇宙模型的性质与信号特征。

Method: 放弃宇宙各向同性（isotropy）要求，仅保留空间均匀性（spatial homogeneity）；引入Bianchi模型（Bianchi models）作为空间均匀宇宙的特例，通过指定适当的Killing矢量场（Killing vector fields）构造度规；采用与FLRW模型类似的方法，在牛顿规范（Newtonian gauge）下推导Bianchi模型中的弗里德曼方程扰动，并将其合并为一个特征偏微分方程。

Result: 得到了一个统一的特征偏微分方程，并基于该方程对Bianchi V型（toy Bianchi V example）宇宙模型进行了CMB模拟，生成了其功率谱（power spectrum）。

Conclusion: 本文系统整合了前期工作，为描述各向异性宇宙模型的信号特征提供了统一框架，并给出了进一步研究方向的讨论与建议。

Abstract: In recent years, there have been increasing challenges to the cosmological principle, based on new observations of e.g. supernovae and the cosmic bulk flow. As a result, the cosmological community is speaking their concern for the cosmological principle, and from which scales onwards it should apply. In this context, there is a desire to understand more fully the properties and signatures of cosmologies not obeying the cosmological principle. In this article, we let go of the demand of cosmic isotropy, and instead assume only spatial homogeneity in our cosmological models. We follow the results of our previous works [see citations in the list of references], and here bring these together into one unified picture, with the goal of describing the signature(s) of anisotropy in anisotropic cosmological models. We first introduce the Bianchi models -- a particular instance of spatially homogeneous cosmologies -- and show that a metric can be constructed for them when an appropriate collection of desired Killing vector fields is supplied. Then, we give the perturbations of the Friedmann equations in such Bianchi models, in the Newtonian gauge, derived using much the same methodology as applicable to the FLRW models. We show these can be combined into one characteristic partial differential equation. Finally, we use this equation in order to simulate the CMB of a toy Bianchi V example and produce its power spectrum. We close with a discussion, and suggestions for further research.

</details>


### [53] [Unified dark sector and Hubble-tension alleviation in scalar-vector-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14977)
*Kimet Jusufi,Amir A. Khodahami,Ahmad Sheykhi,Jackson Levi Said,Emmanuel N. Saridakis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种标量-矢量-张量理论，通过共形标量耦合修改物质观测者感受到的膨胀率，从而在低红移区域提升有效哈勃常数（Hubble constant），缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）。矢量场通过密度依赖的质量机制表现为无压强暗物质成分，标量场则充当动态暗能量（dark energy），并通过变色龙屏蔽机制（chameleon screening）满足局域引力约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缓解哈勃张力是当前宇宙学的一个核心难题。现有方案多依赖早期宇宙修改，而本文旨在构造一种纯粹晚期宇宙机制，在不影响早期宇宙物理的前提下缓解该张力，同时统一描述暗能量（dark energy）与暗物质（dark matter）行为。

Method: 构建一个标量-矢量-张量理论，其中物质最小耦合于 Jordan 框架（Jordan frame）度规，大质量矢量场与重子流耦合，共形标量场通过修改物质观测者的膨胀率影响有效哈勃常数（effective Hubble constant）。标量场的演化仅在低红移区变得显著，矢量场通过密度依赖的质量（density-dependent vector mass）表现为无压强成分。

Result: 该模型在晚期宇宙中提升了有效哈勃常数，从而缓解哈勃张力；标量势自然充当动态暗能量（dynamical dark energy），矢量贡献在宇宙学尺度上等效于无压强物质（pressureless component）。变色龙屏蔽机制（chameleon screening）使得理论在太阳系尺度仍与引力实验一致。

Conclusion: 该框架在一个统一的理论中同时实现了晚期标量动力学、有效暗能量演化与哈勃张力缓解，且满足局域引力约束，为解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀与哈勃张力提供了一种自洽的唯象方案。

Abstract: We investigate a scalar-vector-tensor theory in which matter is minimally coupled to a Jordan-frame metric, while a massive vector sector interacts with the baryonic current. We show that the conformal scalar coupling modifies the physical expansion rate measured by matter observers, leading to a late-time enhancement of the effective Hubble constant. By constructing a phenomenological scalar evolution that becomes relevant only at low redshifts, the model provides a purely late-time mechanism for alleviating the Hubble tension without significantly affecting early-universe cosmology. The scalar potential naturally acts as a dynamical dark-energy sector, while the vector contribution behaves effectively as a pressureless component at cosmological scales through a density-dependent vector mass. Hence, the framework connects late-time scalar dynamics, effective dark-energy evolution, and Hubble-tension alleviation within a unified setup. Finally, local gravitational constraints can be suppressed through a chameleon-type screening mechanism, allowing the theory to remain compatible with Solar-System tests while retaining nontrivial cosmological effects.

### [54] [An Exact Single-Rotating Near-Horizon Geometry in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15005)
*U. Can Çelik,Kamal Hajian,Jutta Kunz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet）引力框架下构建了五维单旋转近视界解。高斯-博内项在旋转参数低于某个由耦合常数决定的阈值时可消除局域曲率奇异性，使曲率不变量在全时空有限。这是该框架下首个具有有限曲率不变量的单旋转五维解析解。文章分析了参数空间中的正则、奇异和边缘区域，并研究了热力学性质，发现高阶导数修正虽正则化了局域曲率行为，但也给标准 Killing 视界的热力学描述带来了独特挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高阶曲率修正（如 Gauss-Bonnet 项）能否消除旋转黑洞近视界几何中的局域曲率奇异性，并构造一个在该框架下具有有限曲率不变量的解析解。

Method: 在五维 Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet 引力中构造单旋转近视界解，通过对旋转参数施加阈值条件来确保曲率不变量有限，并对参数空间进行分类分析。

Result: 成功构造了首个具有有限曲率不变量的单旋转五维近视界解析解；发现当旋转参数低于 Gauss-Bonnet 耦合确定的阈值时，局域曲率奇异性被消除；参数空间可分为正则、奇异和边缘三种区域。

Conclusion: Gauss-Bonnet 高阶导数项能够正则化局域曲率行为，但同时也给基于 Killing 视界的标准热力学描述带来了新的困难与挑战。

Abstract: We construct a five-dimensional singly rotating near-horizon solution in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. We show that the Gauss-Bonnet term removes the local curvature singularity, yielding finite curvature invariants throughout the spacetime, provided the rotation parameter remains below a certain value set by the Gauss-Bonnet coupling. To our knowledge, this is the first analytic example of a singly rotating five-dimensional solution in this framework with finite curvature invariants over a nontrivial region of parameter space. We analyze the geometry across this space, identifying regular, singular, and marginal regimes. Finally, we study the thermodynamic properties, finding that while higher-derivative corrections regularize the local curvature behavior, they also introduce unique challenges to the standard thermodynamic description of Killing horizons.

</details>

### [56] [Collider-Bench: Benchmarking AI Agents with Particle Physics Analysis Reproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13950)
*Darius A. Faroughy,Sofia Palacios Schweitzer,Ian Pang,Siddharth Mishra-Sharma,David Shih*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Collider-Bench 是一个用于评估大语言模型智能体（LLM agent）能否仅凭公开论文和科学软件复现大型强子对撞机（LHC）实验分析的新型基准测试。实验表明，尚无通用编程智能体能够稳定超越物理学家介入的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试难以捕捉真实科研工作的复杂性与细微之处，而大型强子对撞机（LHC）实验分析因公开工具链仅近似内部软件、论文省略实现细节而难以复现，亟需一个能评估LLM智能体在长周期工具使用（long-horizon tool-use）任务中填补这些空白能力的基准。

Method: 每个任务要求智能体将已发表的分析转化为可执行的模拟与筛选流水线（simulation-and-selection pipeline），并提交指定信号区（signal region）的碰撞事件产额预测。预测结果使用标准直方图指标（histogram metrics）给出连续保真度分数，并报告每项任务的算力成本。同时利用LLM裁判（LLM judge）评估完整代码库与会话轨迹，以捕捉捏造（fabrication）、幻觉（hallucination）和重复（duplication）等定性失败模式。

Result: 在涵盖不同能力层级的通用编程智能体（general purpose coding agents）上评估后，平均而言，没有任何智能体能可靠地击败物理学家介入（physician-in-the-loop）的解决方案。

Conclusion: Collider-Bench 能有效评估LLM智能体在复杂科研复现任务中的表现，当前最先进的通用编程智能体尚无法稳定超越人类专家介入的基准，表明该方向仍存在显著提升空间。

Abstract: Autonomous language-model agents are increasingly evaluated on long-horizon tool-use tasks, but existing benchmarks rarely capture the complexity and nuance of real scientific work. To address this gap, we introduce Collider-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating whether LLM agents can reproduce experimental analyses from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) using only public papers and open scientific software. Such analyses are often difficult to reproduce because the public toolchain only approximates the software used internally by the experimental collaborations, while the published papers inevitably omit implementation details needed for a faithful reconstruction. Agents must therefore rely on physical reasoning, domain knowledge, and trial-and-error to fill these gaps. Each task requires the agent to turn a published analysis into an executable simulation-and-selection pipeline and submit predicted collision event yields in specified signal regions. These predictions are evaluated with standard histogram metrics that provide continuous fidelity scores without a hand-written rubric. We also report the computational cost incurred by each agent per task. Finally, we evaluate the codebase and full session trace using an LLM judge to catch qualitative failure modes such as fabrications, hallucinations and duplications. We release an initial set of tasks drawn from LHC searches, together with a containerized sandbox and event simulation tools. We evaluate across a capability ladder of general purpose coding agents. Our results show that on average no agent reliably beats the physicist-in-the-loop solution.

</details>


### [57] [Criticality and Saturation in Orthogonal Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06563)
*Max Guillen,Jan E. Gerken*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文推导了正交初始化（orthogonal initialization）下神经网络有限宽度修正（finite-width corrections）中张量的逐层递归关系，扩展了适用于独立同分布（i.i.d.）初始化的费曼图（Feynman diagrams）方法，从理论上解释了正交初始化网络在深度增大时有限宽度张量保持稳定的现象，并通过数值实验验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来已知正交初始化（orthogonal initialization）相比独立同分布（i.i.d.）高斯初始化能改善训练性能，但学界对这一现象缺乏理论解释。本文旨在填补这一空白，从有限宽度修正的角度为正交初始化网络的稳定性提供严格的理论推导。

Method: 推导了正交初始化下网络统计量有限宽度展开中张量的显式逐层递归关系（layer-wise recursion relations）；将i.i.d.情形下已有的费曼图（Feynman diagrams）方法扩展至所有$1/\mathrm{width}$阶数；通过数值求解递归关系与解析大深度展开，与蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）估计进行对比验证。

Result: 推导的递归关系成功复现了Day等人实验观察到的有限宽度张量在深度增大时的稳定性，且针对具有零不动点（vanishing fixed point）的激活函数成立。数值解与解析大深度展开结果均与蒙特卡洛模拟高度一致。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上解释了正交初始化可稳定有限宽度非线性网络的深层原因，弥合了相关领域长期存在的理论空白，并提供了实验验证支持。

Abstract: It has been known for a long time that initializing weight matrices to be orthogonal instead of having i.i.d. Gaussian components can improve training performance. This phenomenon can be analyzed using finite-width corrections, where the infinite-width statistics are supplemented by a power series in $1/\mathrm{width}$. In particular, recent empirical results by Day et al. show that the tensors appearing in this treatment stabilize for large depth, as opposed to the tensors of i.i.d.-initialized networks. In this article, we derive explicit layer-wise recursion relations for the tensors appearing in the finite-width expansion of the network statistics in the case of orthogonal initializations. We also provide an extension of recently-introduced Feynman diagrams for the corresponding recursions in the i.i.d.-case which are valid to all orders in $1/\mathrm{width}$. Finally, we show explicitly that the recursions we derive reproduce the stability of the finite-width tensors which was observed for activation functions with vanishing fixed point. This work therefore provides a theoretical explanation for the stability of nonlinear networks of finite width initialized with orthogonal weights, closing a long-standing gap in the literature. We validate our theoretical results experimentally by showing that numerical solutions of our recursion relations and their analytical large-depth expansions agree excellently with Monte-Carlo estimates from network ensembles.

</details>


### [58] [Spontaneous symmetry breaking and Goldstone modes for deep information propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14685)
*Nabil Iqbal,T. Anderson Keller,Yue Song,Takeru Miyato,Max Welling*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了深度神经网络中连续对称性自发破缺所产生的类戈德斯通（Goldstone-like）自由度，证明其能够在无需残差连接或归一化等架构稳定器的情况下，实现跨层和跨时间步的相干信号传播，从而提升前馈网络的可训练性和表示多样性，以及循环网络在长序列建模中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索深度神经网络中连续对称性（continuous symmetry）自发破缺所引发的类戈德斯通（Goldstone-like）自由度，是否能够作为一种天然的机制，替代残差连接（residual connections）或归一化（normalization）等人工稳定器，实现深层网络中的稳定信息传播。

Method: 构建内部层具有等变性（equivariant）的深度神经网络，从解析和实证两个层面分析连续对称性自发破缺所产生的类戈德斯通自由度的动力学行为，并在前馈网络（feedforward networks）和循环网络（recurrent networks）中验证其对信号传播的影响。

Result: 在前馈网络中，类戈德斯通自由度提升了可训练性（trainability）和跨层的表示多样性（representational diversity）。在循环网络（RNNs, GRUs）中，该机制通过在循环迭代中传播信息，有效改善了长序列建模任务上的性能。

Conclusion: 连续对称性自发破缺导致的类戈德斯通自由度为深度网络提供了一种内在的、不依赖架构稳定器的信息传播机制，对理解深度学习的表征学习（representation learning）本质和设计更高效的网络架构具有启示意义。

Abstract: In physical systems, whenever a continuous symmetry is spontaneously broken, the system possesses excitations called Goldstone modes, which allow coherent information propagation over long distances and times. In this work, we study deep neural networks whose internal layers are equivariant under a continuous symmetry and may therefore support analogous Goldstone-like degrees of freedom. We demonstrate, both analytically and empirically, that these degrees of freedom enable coherent signal propagation across depth and recurrent iterations, providing a mechanism for stable information flow without relying on architectural stabilizers such as residual connections or normalization. In feedforward networks, this results in improved trainability and representational diversity across layers. In recurrent settings, we demonstrate the same mechanism is valuable for long-term memory by propagating information over recurrent iterations, thereby improving performance of RNNs and GRUs on long-sequence modeling tasks.

### [59] [A tree-free approach to 3D Yang-Mills Langevin dynamic. Analytic estimates and the existence of a model for a regularity structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14616)
*Alexey Sevostyanov*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功构造了与三维欧几里得杨-米尔斯泛函的随机朗之万方程对应的正则性结构及其模型；建立了几乎必然成立的全局随机估计与全局逐点加权贝索夫型估计；证明了当磨光去除后，光滑模型序列在特定拓扑下收敛。

Conclusion: 所得到的正则性结构与模型及其伴随的随机估计，为后续构造三维欧几里得杨-米尔斯测度提供了关键的解析基础，并展示了多指标方法在涉及向量值白噪声的方程组系统中的适用性。

Abstract: Using the multi-index approach to regularity structures due to F. Otto et al., we construct a regularity structure and a model for it associated to the stochastic Langevin equation for the 3D Euclidean Yang-Mills functional. For the model we also obtain global stochastic and global pointwise weighted Besov type estimates which hold almost surely. The model is defined as a limit of a sequence of smooth models introduced with the help of a mollified noise. When the mollification is removed the sequence converges in a certain topology defined with the help of the stochastic estimates. To obtain these results we develop the multi-index approach for systems of equations with vector-valued white noises. This project is motivated by the problem for constructing 3D Euclidean Yang-Mills measure and by the earlier results of the author on the related problem of canonical quantization of the Yang-Mills field on the Minkowski space.

### [61] [Lower bound on the mixing time of $p$-spin glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14681)
*Anouar Kouraich,Simone Warzel*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于 p-自旋玻璃（p-spin glass）模型，当逆温度（inverse temperature）大于 $c \cdot \ln(p)/p$（$c$ 为常数，$p$ 足够大）时，Glauber 动力学（Glauber dynamics）的混合时间（mixing time）以指数级缓慢增长。该结果通过高斯分解（Gaussian decomposition）分析能量景观（energy landscape）并建立瓶颈界（bottleneck bound）获得。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高斯分解（Gaussian decomposition）技术对 p-自旋玻璃的能量景观进行解析，进而利用瓶颈界（bottleneck bound）方法证明存在能量势垒，阻碍马尔可夫链（Markov chain）在状态空间中的快速转移。

Result: 证明了当逆温度 $\beta$ 大于某个与 $p$ 相关的阈值（即 $\beta > c \cdot \ln(p)/p$，$c$ 为常数且 $p$ 足够大）时，Glauber 动力学的混合时间随系统规模呈指数级增长。

Conclusion: 该结果首次在宽泛的参数区间内严格建立了 p-自旋玻璃模型在低温下的动力学缓慢混合现象，为理解自旋玻璃的动力学相变（dynamic phase transition）提供了理论支持。

Abstract: We show that Glauber dynamics for $ p$-spin glass mixes exponentially slowly at inverse temperatures larger than a constant times $ \ln (p)/p $ for large enough $ p $. This is done by analyzing the energy landscape using Gaussian decompositions and establishing a bottleneck bound.

### [62] [Finite-size scaling of hetero-associative retrieval in continuous-signal-driven Ising spin systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14059)
*Andrea Ladiana*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多层伊辛（Ising）框架，通过几何保持的连续-伊辛编码器（PCA白化+SimHash随机超平面投影）与Kanter-Sompolinsky伪逆记忆耦合的结合，将真实世界的高维连续物理信号映射到离散伊辛自旋的联想记忆（associative memory）系统中，实现跨模态回忆。该框架在睡眠脑电图的跨通道信号重建任务上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界物理信号是连续且高维的，但统计力学（statistical mechanics）中联想记忆的标准工具基于离散伊辛自旋（Ising spins），两者之间存在建模鸿沟。本文旨在弥合这一差距，构建一个能处理连续信号、同时保留联想记忆热力学与动力学优点的统一框架。

Method: 方法包含三部分：(1) 几何保持的编码器：PCA白化（PCA whitening）结合SimHash随机超平面投影（random-hyperplane projection），将连续信号映射为伊辛自旋；(2) Kanter-Sompolinsky伪逆记忆耦合（pseudo-inverse memory couplings），嵌入三层异联想系统的局部场方程；(3) 动力学设计：并行（Little）更新触发跨模态信号雪崩，顺序（Glauber）更新解决对称叠加态。

Result: 伪逆修正使得等权重混合态在热力学上不稳定，热涨落打破跨模态对称性并选出单一全局胜者。操作存储容量满足Amit-Gutfreund-Sompolinsky有限尺寸修正α_c(N)=α_c(∞)-c N^{-1/2}，外推得到渐近操作极限α_c(∞)≈0.50。在PhysioNet Sleep-EDF数据集上，单通道额叶脑电图（EEG）线索可重建顶叶EEG和眼电图（EOG）轴上的宏观睡眠状态。

Conclusion: 所提出的多层伊辛框架成功实现了从连续物理信号到离散自旋联想记忆的跨模态映射，在存在淬灭生物无序（quenched biological disorder）的条件下仍能完成跨模态回忆。该工作为统计力学方法在真实连续信号处理中的应用提供了理论桥梁与实践验证。

Abstract: Real-world physical signals are continuous and high-dimensional, yet the statistical-mechanics machinery of associative memory operates on discrete Ising spins. We bridge this divide through a multilayer Ising framework that couples a geometry-preserving continuous-to-Ising encoder (PCA whitening composed with SimHash random-hyperplane projection) to Kanter-Sompolinsky pseudo-inverse memory couplings, embedded directly into the local-field equations of a tri-layer hetero-associative system. The pseudo-inverse correction renders the equal-weight mixture state thermodynamically unstable, so that thermal fluctuations break the cross-modal symmetry and select a single global winner. We further establish a dynamical duality: parallel (Little) updates are structurally required to ignite the cross-modal signal avalanche from a single cued layer, whereas sequential (Glauber) sweeps resolve symmetric superpositions. The operational storage capacity obeys the Amit-Gutfreund-Sompolinsky finite-size correction $α_c(N)=α_c(\infty)-c\,N^{-1/2}$, extrapolating to an asymptotic operational limit $α_c(\infty)\approx 0.50$ under macroscopic-basin retrieval. Applied to multi-channel sleep polysomnography (PhysioNet Sleep-EDF), the architecture reconstructs the macroscopic sleep state on parietal EEG and EOG axes from a single noisy frontal-EEG cue, demonstrating cross-modal recall in the presence of quenched biological disorder.

</details>


### [63] [Quantum Criticality in Monolayer Amorphous Carbon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14349)
*Rejaul SK,Hanning Zhang,Artem K Grebenko,Arsen Herasymchuk,Ranjith Shivajirao,Hongji Zhang,Abee Nelson,Zheng Jue Tong,Gagandeep Singh,Naoto Kimiuchi,Yuta Sato,Kazutomo Suenaga,Chee Tat Toh,Rudolf A Romer,Shaffique Adam,Oleg V. Yazyev,Barbaros Ozyilmaz,Bent Weber*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过原子级波函数测量，证实单层非晶碳（MAC）是一种纯拓扑无序驱动的严格二维安德森临界电子系统，发现在带中心附近存在受手征对称性保护的临界态，并验证了多分形标度关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶固体中长程有序的缺失破坏了布洛赫（Bloch）电子态描述，而严格二维非晶晶格中电子局域化行为（尤其是否存在拓扑无序驱动的安德森临界性）尚未被实验证实。

Method: 对单层非晶碳（monolayer amorphous carbon, MAC）进行原子级分辨率的多分形波函数测量，结合原子尺度的紧束缚（tight-binding）计算，分析波函数的多分形标度行为并检验手征对称性（chiral symmetry）的保护机制。

Result: MAC中拓扑无序有效局域化了低能电子态，但在带中心（E∼0）处保留了一个扩展的类临界态；实验验证了多分形标度关系η = -Δ₂，且原子级紧束缚计算与该标度行为定量吻合。

Conclusion: MAC成为首个被确认为纯拓扑无序驱动的严格二维安德森临界（Anderson criticality）电子系统，其带中心临界态可能由连续随机网络中的残余手征对称性通过Wess-Zumino-Witten（WZW）拓扑项保护。

Abstract: Amorphous solids represent the extreme limit of broken translational symmetry, in which the absence of long-range order removes well-defined crystal momenta and invalidates the Bloch description of electronic states. Monolayer amorphous carbon (MAC) has emerged as a unique realization of a strictly two-dimensional (2D) amorphous lattice defined by a structurally contiguous but topologically disordered $sp^2$-bonded random network devoid of any defined long-range crystal symmetry. From atomic-resolution measurements of multifractal wavefunctions, we show that disorder in MAC effectively localizes the low-energy part of the electronic spectrum but retains an extended critical-like state near the band centre ($E\sim 0$). We conjecture that this state is protected from topological disorder by remnant chiral symmetry surviving within the continuous random network, described by a Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) topological term. Near criticality, we verify the multifractal scaling relation $η= -Δ_2$, providing quantitative agreement between independently measured spatial correlation decay and multifractal scaling exponents. Our results are confirmed by atomistic tight-binding calculations that closely mirror the multifractal scaling near $E\sim 0$. Our results establish MAC as the first strictly 2D amorphous electronic system to exhibit Anderson criticality driven purely by topological disorder

</details>

### [64] [Fermi Surface Geometry from Charge Fluctuations in Three-Dimensional Metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13951)
*Pok Man Tam,Yarden Sheffer,Xiao-Chuan Wu,F. D. M. Haldane,Shinsei Ryu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现三维无相互作用多带金属中，费米子双部分电荷涨落的次主导对数项编码了费米面的形状与量子几何信息；该对数项与结构因子的动量空间系数相关，可表示为费米面曲率张量和量子度量张量的费米面积分；当实空间分割面为二次曲面时，对数系数满足一个仅依赖于费米面欧拉示性数与陈数的拓扑界限，揭示了多带金属中拓扑与量子拓扑之间的非平凡相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索三维无相互作用多带金属中费米面形状和量子几何如何体现在电荷涨落的次主导对数项中，并揭示拓扑与量子拓扑在多带系统中的关联。

Method: 通过对三维无相互作用多带金属的双部分电荷涨落进行解析分析，提取次主导对数项；将其与动量空间中结构因子的特定系数相关联；利用费米面曲率张量（Fermi surface curvature tensor）和量子度量张量（quantum metric tensor）的费米面积分来表达这些量；在实空间分割面为二次曲面（quadric）的情形下，推导对数系数的拓扑界限。

Result: 次主导对数项与结构因子的无量纲∣q∣³系数存在等价关系；两者均可写为费米面曲率张量和量子度量张量的费米面积分；当分割面为球面或椭球面时，对数系数受限于一个取决于费米面欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）和陈数（Chern number）的拓扑界限。

Conclusion: 多带金属电荷涨落的次主导对数项携带了费米面的几何与拓扑信息，其拓扑界限表明了拓扑与量子拓扑之间非平凡的相互影响，为理解多带系统中的量子几何效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: For three-dimensional non-interacting multi-band metals, we show that important information about the shape and the quantum geometry of Fermi surfaces is encoded in the subleading logarithmic term of bipartite charge fluctuations. This logarithmic term is related to the dimensionless $|\mathbf{q}|^3$-coefficient of the structure factor in momentum space, and both quantities can be expressed as Fermi surface integrals of the Fermi surface curvature tensor and the quantum metric tensor. When the real-space partition surface is a quadric (i.e., sphere or ellipsoid), the logarithmic coefficient satisfies a topological bound depending only on the Euler characteristic and the Chern number of the Fermi surface, illustrating a non-trivial interplay between topology and quantum topology in multi-band metals.

</details>


### [65] [Switchable Surface Linear Photogalvanic Effect in the Magnetic Weyl Semimetal Co3Sn2S2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14107)
*Niket Shah,Aymen Nomani,Kai Chen,Hridis Pal,Pavan Hosur*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文运用格林函数（Green's function）与图解形式（diagrammatic formalism）理论分析了磁性外尔半金属（magnetic Weyl semimetal）Co3Sn2S2 表面的线性光生伏打效应（LPGE），揭示了表面晶体对称性与磁化翻转对光电流的调控机制，以及内禀贡献和外禀贡献的对称性约束差异，并指出该系统可实现对称性控制的非线性输运与磁控光电器件应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究磁性外尔半金属 Co3Sn2S2 表面的线性光生伏打效应（LPGE），探索表面对称性破缺下光电流的产生机制及其受磁化控制的规律。

Method: 采用格林函数（Green's function）与图解形式（diagrammatic formalism）进行理论分析，分别考察内禀贡献（intrinsic contribution）和外禀贡献（extrinsic contribution）的对称性约束与温度、频率依赖标度行为。

Result: 表面单一幺正晶体对称性（unitary crystal symmetry）导致磁化翻转时特定偏振角下的光电流符号反转；反幺正镜面对称（antiunitary mirror symmetry）强制内禀贡献的若干非线性响应张量元为零，而外禀贡献不受此约束且幅值较大；光电流呈近似线性温度依赖及低频幂律标度 |jy| ∝ ω^{-2.2}，标度指数温度依赖性弱。

Conclusion: Co3Sn2S2 是实现对称性控制非线性输运与磁控光电器件应用的有前景平台。

Abstract: We investigate the linear photogalvanic effect (LPGE) on the surface of the magnetic Weyl semimetal Co3Sn2S2 using a Green's-function and diagrammatic formalism. While the LPGE vanishes in the centrosymmetric bulk, it is symmetry-allowed on the surface where inversion symmetry is broken. We show that unitary crystal symmetries on the surface produce characteristic sign reversals of the total photocurrent at certain polarization angles upon flipping the magnetization. We further find that the intrinsic contribution to the LPGE is strongly constrained by an antiunitary mirror symmetry, which forces several nonlinear response tensor elements to vanish. In contrast, the extrinsic contribution is not subject to these constraints and displays a large magnitude which, we argue, is due to the enhanced density of states associated with Fermi-arc surface states. The current exhibits an approximately linear temperature dependence and a low-frequency power-law scaling, |jy| proportional to omega^-2.2, with weak temperature dependence of the scaling exponent. Our results identify Co3Sn2S2 as a promising platform for experimentally accessing symmetry-controlled nonlinear transport in realistic systems and for applications in magnetically controlled optoelectronic devices.

### [66] [Operator ordering as an emergent geometric background in Dirac systems with spatially varying mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14148)
*C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了空间变化质量下狄拉克哈密顿量唯一确定的厄米排序（Hermitian ordering）对能谱的影响，发现该排序引入对数梯度项并导致谱量子化条件的普适形变，在紧凑几何中产生模式依赖的二阶谱移，且在质量反转阈值附近显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在狄拉克哈密顿量（Dirac Hamiltonian）具有空间变化质量（spatially varying mass）时，如何确定其与概率流守恒（probability-current conservation）相容的唯一厄米排序，以及该排序对离散能谱产生的可观测修正。

Method: 通过要求概率流守恒来唯一确定狄拉克算符的厄米排序方案；在紧凑几何（compact geometry）下进行解析计算，分析谱移（spectral shift）的具体形式及其与质量剖面（mass profile）空间变化的关系。

Result: 唯一一致的排序引入了额外的对数梯度项（logarithmic-gradient term），该贡献修正了有效动能算符并导致谱量子化条件（spectral quantization condition）发生普适形变（universal deformation）。在紧凑几何中，解析计算得到模式依赖的二阶谱移（mode-dependent second-order spectral shift），该谱移在质量反转阈值（mass-inversion threshold）附近显著增强。

Conclusion: 狄拉克算符在空间非均匀标量背景（spatially inhomogeneous scalar background）下的一致相对论性排序会导致离散谱的可观测修正，这对理解相关物理系统中的谱行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the spectral consequences of the uniquely determined Hermitian ordering of the Dirac Hamiltonian with spatially varying mass. In contrast to the nonrelativistic case, where continuous families of admissible prescriptions exist, the relativistic Dirac operator admits a single consistent ordering compatible with probability-current conservation. This requirement generates an additional logarithmic-gradient term proportional to the spatial variation of the mass profile. We show that this contribution modifies the effective kinetic operator and induces a universal deformation of the spectral quantization condition. In compact geometry, an explicit analytic computation reveals a mode-dependent second-order spectral shift that becomes strongly enhanced near the mass-inversion threshold. These results demonstrate that the consistent relativistic ordering of the Dirac operator leads to observable modifications of discrete spectra in spatially inhomogeneous scalar backgrounds.

</details>


### [67] [Spin Hall effect in electronic Lévy glasses: Enhanced spin current generation in the superdiffusive regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14214)
*Diego B. Fonseca,Luiz Felipe C. Pereira,Anderson L. R. Barbosa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究电子莱维玻璃（electronic Lévy glasses）中的自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect），发现超扩散输运（superdiffusive regime）相比扩散输运（diffusive regime）能实现更高的自旋霍尔角（30% vs 5%），表明该系统可有效调控自旋流并优化自旋霍尔效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自旋电子学（spintronics）中，自旋流的产生、操控和探测是发展下一代自旋电子技术的核心需求。本文旨在探索一种可调控的自旋输运平台，研究自旋霍尔效应在非均匀、无序体系中的表现。

Method: 采用朗道尔-布蒂克方法（Landauer-Büttiker approach）结合数值精确的紧束缚（tight-binding）模拟，计算自旋分辨透射系数（spin-resolved transmission coefficients），进而评估自旋霍尔电流（spin Hall current）和自旋霍尔角（spin Hall angle）随费米能（Fermi energy）、自旋-轨道耦合强度（spin-orbit coupling strength）和局域静电势（on-site electrostatic potential）的变化。

Result: 在超扩散输运（superdiffusive regime）中，较小的电荷流可转化为较大的自旋霍尔电流，自旋霍尔角可达30%；而在扩散输运（diffusive regime）中，相同电荷流仅产生适中的自旋霍尔电流，自旋霍尔角仅为5%。超扩散区还具有低费米能、低电阻率和低磁电阻率，以及较长的自旋扩散长度（spin diffusion length）。

Conclusion: 电子莱维玻璃（electronic Lévy glasses）为调控自旋输运和优化自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）提供了多功能平台，有望应用于自旋电子学器件。

Abstract: In spintronics, both electronic charge and spin are used to process and store information. Generation, manipulation, and detection of spin currents are essential for the development of next-generation spintronic technologies. Here, we investigate the spin Hall effect in electronic Lévy glasses composed of graphene ribbons with randomly distributed circular regions of high spin-orbit coupling. These systems exhibit two transport regimes that can be tuned by adjusting the Fermi energy. The superdiffusive regime is characterized by low Fermi energy, low resistivity, and low magnetoresistivity, resulting in a long spin diffusion length, in contrast to the diffusive regime. Employing the Landauer-Büttiker approach in conjunction with numerically exact tight-binding simulations, we compute spin-resolved transmission coefficients to assess the spin Hall current and the spin Hall angle as functions of Fermi energy, spin-orbit coupling strength, and on-site electrostatic potential. Our findings reveal that, in the superdiffusive regime, a low charge current can be converted into a large spin Hall current, whereas in the diffusive regime, the same charge current generates a modest spin Hall current. Moreover, we observe that the spin Hall angle can reach 30% in the superdiffusive regime, whereas in the diffusive regime it is only 5%. These results demonstrate that electronic Lévy glasses provide a versatile platform for controlling spin transport and optimizing the spin Hall effect for spintronic applications.

</details>


### [68] [Engineering Delocalization in Graphene Nanoribbons via Quasiperiodic Edges and Electronic Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14216)
*Diego B. Fonseca,Anderson L. R. Barbosa,Luiz Felipe C. Pereira*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有准周期斐波那契型边缘延伸的锯齿形石墨烯纳米带中的局域化效应，考虑电子-电子相互作用。采用包含最近邻和第三近邻跃迁的紧束缚模型，结合自洽平均场哈伯德近似和Landauer-Büttiker formalism计算电荷输运性质，发现准周期几何与电子相互作用的组合导致三种输运区间：非相互作用下的几何局域化、弱相互作用下的导电区间（伴随传输振荡，多重性随斐波那契代数增加）、强相互作用下的重新局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索准周期边缘几何与电子相互作用共同作用对锯齿形石墨烯纳米带（zigzag graphene nanoribbons）中电荷输运和局域化效应的影响，揭示其物理机制。

Method: 采用包含最近邻（nearest-neighbor）和第三近邻（third-nearest-neighbor）跃迁的紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），电子相互作用通过自洽平均场哈伯德近似（self-consistent mean-field Hubbard approximation）处理，电荷输运性质利用Landauer-Büttiker形式（Landauer-Büttiker formalism）计算。

Result: 系统呈现三种输运区间：非相互作用情况下的几何局域化（geometric localization）；弱相互作用下的导电区间，传输振荡（transmission oscillations）的多重性随斐波那契代数（Fibonacci generation order）增加，离域化源于几何与相互作用诱导关联的协同作用；强相互作用下排斥占主导，系统返回局域化态。

Conclusion: 准周期边缘工程（quasiperiodic edge engineering）结合电子相互作用控制，为调控石墨烯纳米带的输运性质提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: We investigate localization effects in zigzag graphene nanoribbons with quasiperiodic Fibonacci-type edge extensions, accounting for electron-electron interactions. We employ a tight-binding model that includes first- and third-nearest-neighbor hoppings, in which electronic interactions are treated within a self-consistent mean-field Hubbard approximation. Charge transport properties are calculated using the Landauer-Büttiker formalism. Our results reveal that the combination of quasiperiodic geometry and electronic interactions gives rise to nontrivial transport phenomena. Specifically, the system exhibits three transport regimes: in the non-interacting case, we observe geometric localization. For weak interactions, the system shows a conductive regime with transmission oscillations, whose multiplicity increases with the Fibonacci generation order. In this regime, delocalization emerges from the interplay between geometry and interaction-induced correlations. Finally, for strong interactions, repulsion dominates, and the system returns to a localized state. Our results demonstrate that quasiperiodic edge engineering, combined with electronic interaction control, offers a promising path to modulate transport in graphene nanoribbons.

</details>


### [69] [Open Quantum Theory of Shot Noise in Dissipative Chiral Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14263)
*Ming Gong,Masahito Ueda*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个用于耗散手性输运中散粒噪声动力学的开放量子理论，通过量子电路映射揭示了电流噪声由占据数分布和粒子数涨落两个竞争因素控制，并提出了从可测噪声累积量直接重建隐藏占据数分布的反演方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解耗散手性输运（dissipative chiral transport）中散粒噪声（shot noise）的动力学机制，特别是耗散如何影响噪声行为以及不同噪声贡献之间的竞争关系。

Method: 将所考虑系统映射到量子电路（quantum circuit），发展开放量子理论（open quantum theory）进行分析；通过选择性加热源来揭示占据数分布与粒子数涨落之间的噪声贡献竞争；提出基于噪声累积量反演重建占据数分布的实验方案。

Result: 电流噪声由平均占据数分布和粒子数涨落两个竞争因素决定；能量完全弛豫时散粒噪声被强烈抑制，部分占据能级导致的分割噪声（partition noise）被淬灭，仅保留受强U(1)对称性保护的残余噪声；选择性加热源触发了通道间关联噪声（inter-channel correlation noise）的符号反转，该特征被看似相同的单通道热噪声所掩盖。

Conclusion: 耗散抑制了散粒噪声并淬灭分割噪声；通道间关联噪声的符号反转是一个被热噪声掩盖的关键特征；所提出的反演方案有望直接从实验可测噪声累积量中重建隐藏的占据数分布。

Abstract: We develop an open quantum theory for shot-noise dynamics in dissipative chiral transport. By mapping a system under consideration onto a quantum circuit, we show that current noise is governed by two competing factors: the average occupancy distribution and particle-number fluctuations. With energy fully relaxed, shot noise is strongly suppressed, reflecting the stacking of electrons into lower energy states due to dissipation. This process quenches the partition noise from partially occupied levels, and finally isolates the residual noise protected by strong $U(1)$ symmetry. Moreover, selectively heating the source against the bath uncovers the underlying competition between the noise contributions from the occupancy distribution and those from the particle-number fluctuations. It triggers a sign reversal in inter-channel correlation noise, a signature masked by seemingly identical single-channel thermal noises. We propose an inversion scheme to experimentally reconstruct the hidden occupancy distribution directly from measurable noise cumulants.

</details>


### [70] [Periodic Behavior of Topology in Graphene with Nanohole Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14436)
*Yong-Cheng Jiang,Xing-Xiang Wang,Xiao Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种直接通过超结构晶格常数 \(m\sqrt{3} \times m\sqrt{3}\)（其中 \(m\) 为整数）来诊断具有三角形或蜂窝状纳米孔阵列的石墨烯的能带拓扑性质的方法。在考虑 \(C_{6v}\) 晶格对称性的前提下，研究显示非平庸拓扑性质随 \(m\) 呈周期性出现：三角形阵列周期为二，蜂窝状阵列周期为六。该行为通过Wannier中心的Wyckoff位置和布里渊区高对称点价带的宇称指标得到了验证，为基于石墨烯衍生物的拓扑电子态材料设计提供了便捷指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯中的纳米孔阵列（nanohole arrays）可以调控其电子性质，但如何直接从超结构参数诊断其能带拓扑性尚不明确。本研究旨在建立一种基于晶格常数的直接判定方法，以简化拓扑电子态的材料设计流程。

Method: 作者利用超结构晶格常数 \(m\sqrt{3} \times m\sqrt{3}\) 中的整数 \(m\) 作为诊断参数，结合纳米孔及其阵列所满足的 \(C_{6v}\) 晶格对称性（crystalline symmetry），分析了三角形和蜂窝状两种排列方式下的拓扑性质。计算验证了Wannier中心的Wyckoff位置（Wyckoff positions）以及布里渊区（Brillouin zone）高对称点处价带的宇称指标（parity index）。

Result: 非平庸拓扑性质随 \(m\) 呈周期性出现：对于三角形阵列，周期为二；对于蜂窝状阵列，周期为六。这些周期性行为由Wannier中心的Wyckoff位置和价带宇称指标共同验证。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于石墨烯衍生物的拓扑电子态材料设计提供了一种便捷的指导方法，使得仅通过超结构晶格常数即可预判能带拓扑性。

Abstract: We derive a way to diagnose band topology for graphene with triangular and/or honeycomb array of nanoholes directly from the lattice constant of superstructure $m\sqrt{3}\times m\sqrt{3}$ with integer $m$. Taking into account the $C_{6v}$ crystalline symmetry respected by nanoholes and their array, we demonstrate that nontrivial topology appears periodically with $m$ with period two (six) for triangular (honeycomb) array. These behaviors are verified by Wyckoff positions of Wannier centers and parity index of valence bands at high-symmetry points in Brillouin zone. The results provide a convenient guide for material design of topological electronic states based on graphene derivatives.

</details>


### [71] [Spin resolved spectral topology and re-entrant localization in a non Hermitian quasiperiodic SSH chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14639)
*Hemant K Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究具有Rashba自旋-轨道耦合和自旋相关跳迁的非厄米准周期Su-Schrieffer-Heeger晶格中的局域化与谱拓扑，揭示了随着非厄米参数增加，体系发生从扩展到局域再回到扩展的可重入相变，伴随实-复-实能谱转变，并发现自旋相关跳迁导致能谱分裂为四个独立的自旋分辨谱分支，各自携带不同的绕数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非厄米准周期体系中局域化（localization）与谱拓扑（spectral topology）之间的关联，特别是自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和自旋相关跳迁（spin-dependent hopping）对体系相变行为的影响。

Method: 通过分析逆参与率（inverse participation ratio, IPR）、复能量谱（complex energy spectrum）和谱绕数（spectral winding numbers）等物理量，系统研究非厄米准周期Su-Schrieffer-Heeger晶格的局域化和拓扑性质。

Result: 发现随着非厄米参数增大，体系经历从扩展到局域再回到扩展的可重入相变（re-entrant transition），该局域化转变伴随着复能量平面上从实到复再到实的谱转变。无自旋相关跳迁时，能谱形成两个近自旋简并的环，绕数w=2；引入自旋相关跳迁后，每个环分裂为两个独立的自旋分辨谱分支，形成四个具有不同绕数扇区的孤立谱轮廓。

Conclusion: 在非厄米准周期体系中，局域化、谱拓扑和自旋分辨谱分裂之间存在直接的对应关系。

Abstract: We investigate localization and spectral topology in a non Hermitian quasiperiodic Su Schrieffer Heeger lattice with Rashba spin orbit coupling and spin-dependent hopping. By analyzing the inverse participation ratio, complex energy spectrum, and spectral winding numbers, we demonstrate the emergence of a re-entrant transition from extended to localized and back to extended phases as the non-Hermitian parameter increases. The localization transition is accompanied by a simultaneous real-complex-real spectral transition in the complex-energy plane. In the absence of spin dependent hopping, the spectrum forms two nearly spin-degenerate loops characterized by winding numbers w = 2. Upon introducing finite spin-dependent hopping, each loop splits into two independent spin-resolved spectral branches, resulting in four disconnected spectral contours carrying distinct winding sectors. Our results reveal a direct correspondence between localization, spectral topology, and spin-resolved spectral splitting in non-Hermitian quasiperiodic systems.

</details>


### [72] [Compositional and Magnetic Characterisation of Oblique Co and Fe Nanowire Structures Fabricated Using Focused Electron Beam Induced Deposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14673)
*Aurys Silinga,Keir Edgar,Stephen McVitie,Kayla Fallon,András Kovács,Rafal E. Dunin-Borkowski,Trevor P. Almeida*

TL;DR: 本文通过实验测量了聚焦电子束诱导沉积（FEBID）制备的3D铁磁性纳米线中原子组分与磁感应强度的变化关系，发现倾斜生长角度的增大会导致金属含量降低，但可通过调节电子束参数（降低电压、提高电流）在0°–60°范围内实现近似均匀的金属组分。

Method: 制备了41根Co和Fe纳米线（nanowire, NW），生长角度（相对于光轴）从0°到90°变化。使用（扫描）透射电子显微镜（(S)TEM）中的电子能量损失谱（EELS）和离轴电子全息术（off-axis electron holography）分别映射NW的元素组分和磁感应强度。

Result: FEBID NW中金属含量随倾斜生长角度的增大而降低。通过使用最低可行的电子束电压（减小相互作用体积）和最高可行的电子束电流（提高金属含量），可在0°–60°的生长角度范围内制备出金属含量近似相等的铁磁性纳米线。

Conclusion: FEBID生长角度对纳米线组分有显著影响，但通过优化电子束参数可以补偿这种效应，在较宽角度范围内实现均匀组分，为制造组分可控的3D纳米磁性结构提供了可行策略。

Abstract: Focused electron beam induced deposition (FEBID) is an additive manufacturing technique uniquely suited for fabricating nanoscale 3D prototypes for a range of applications, including spintronic devices. However, the variation of growth dynamics associated with electron beam translation and sample interaction volumes results in structures with non-uniform composition when fabricating intricate 3D geometries. Herein, we measure changes in atomic composition and corresponding changes in magnetic induction in 3D ferromagnetic nanostructures with overhanging elements, e.g. bridges or arches. To investigate the effects of electron beam translation, we fabricated 41 Co and Fe nanowire (NW) structures with growth angle relative to the optic axis varying from 0° to 90°. The (scanning) transmission electron microscopy techniques of electron energy loss spectroscopy and off-axis electron holography were performed to map the NW elemental composition and magnetic induction as a function of NW growth angle. Comparison of the results reveals a reduction in metal content with increased oblique growth angle in FEBID NWs. The magnitude of metal content reduction can be tuned by controlling electron beam parameters, and ferromagnetic NWs with approximately equal metal content at growth angles from 0° to 60° were fabricated by using the lowest viable electron beam voltage and the highest viable beam current to reduce the interaction volume and increase the metal content, respectively.

### [73] [Anisotropic Surface Spin Waves as Signature of A-type Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14735)
*Zhoujian Sun,Yiyuan Chen,Tao Yu,Hai-Zhou Lu,X. C. Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现A型交错磁体（A-type altermagnets）中存在各向异性的表面自旋波（anisotropic surface spin waves），该现象源自交错磁体的本质对称性破缺，并表现出手性依赖的上下表面位置差异和手性分裂的恒定频率轮廓（chiral split constant frequency contours）两个特征，可通过杂散场和谐振吸收谱实验测量，为交错磁体的实验识别提供了新判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁体（altermagnets）兼具铁磁体和反铁磁体的优势，但实验识别仍具挑战，尤其是对占材料候选者大部分的A型交错磁体。本文旨在发现A型交错磁体特有的表面自旋波各向异性特征，以提供可实验检测的识别标志。

Method: 从交错磁体的本质出发，即自旋相反的子晶格（spin-opposite sublattices）无法通过平移或反演操作相关联，这种结构破坏了组合的空间反演-时间反演对称性（combined spatial-inversion and time-reversal symmetry），从而推导出各向异性表面自旋波的产生机制。

Result: 发现A型交错磁体中的各向异性表面自旋波具有两个特性：手性依赖的上表面与下表面位置差异（chirality-dependent top-bottom positions），以及手性分裂的恒定频率轮廓（chiral split constant frequency contours）。这些特性可分别通过杂散场（stray field）和谐振吸收谱（resonance absorption spectrum）进行实验测量。

Conclusion: 所发现的各向异性表面自旋波为检测交错磁体提供了特征信号（signature），有望启发现代自旋逻辑器件和信息存储器件的发展。

Abstract: Altermagnets have attracted intense interest because they have the advantages of both ferromagnets and antiferromagnets. However, their experimental identification remains challenging, in particular for the A-type altermagnets that account for a large group of material candidates. Here, we discover a kind of anisotropic surface spin waves in A-type altermagnets, which is absent in ferromagnets and conventional antiferromagnets. The anisotropic surface spin waves arise directly from the nature of altermagnets, i.e., the spin-opposite sublattices cannot be related by translation or inversion, which breaks the combined spatial-inversion and time-reversal symmetry, leading to the anisotropic surface spin waves with two properties, the chirality-dependent top-bottom positions and chiral split constant frequency contours. We further show that these two properties can be measured experimentally from the stray field and by resonance absorption spectrum, respectively. Our results provide a signature for detecting altermagnets and will inspire spin-based logic and information-storage devices.

### [74] [Optimizing strong light-matter coupling of plasmonic lattices and monolayer semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14767)

Conclusion: 该方法实现了均匀的大面积极化激元晶格，为偏振控制和拓扑极化激元学等应用提供了可行平台。

Transition metal dichalcogenide monolayers host excitons with large oscillator strength and binding energies constituting a robust matter constituent that forms polaritons from cryogenic to room temperature when embedded in optical microcavities. Plasmonic nanoparticles arranged in lattice geometries offer strong field-confinement and high quality factors. However, the high sensitivity of monolayer excitons to strain and dielectric disorder necessitates encapsulation in atomically flat hBN to ensure a high optical quality, rendering plasmonics more challenging. Here, we employ our recently developed fabrication method for embedding gold nanodisk arrays into van der Waals heterostructures and compare two samples with opposite layer order. We observe that strain and etching-induced surface contamination can reduce the exciton quality and thus the light-matter interaction strength significantly. Our fabrication approach reduces interfacial irregularities and enables homogeneous large-area polariton lattices for a wide range of applications, such as polarization-control or topological polaritonics.

### [76] [Current induced magneto-optical Kerr effect as a probe of Dirac carriers in Bi$_{1-x}$Sb$_x$ alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14975)
*Ryota Miyazaki,Shunzhen Wang,Guanxiong Qu,Yukihiro Marui,Yuta Kobayashi,Masashi Kawaguchi,Masamitsu Hayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了Bi$_{1-x}$Sb$_x$半金属合金中电流诱导的磁光克尔效应（MOKE），发现纯Bi中的MOKE信号比过渡金属高出近四个数量级，且信号与电阻率的1.7次方和迁移率的2.0次方成比例，表明狄拉克电子（Dirac electrons）是自旋电流（spin current）产生的主要贡献者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Bi$_{1-x}$Sb$_x$半金属合金中电流诱导磁光克尔效应（current-induced MOKE）的强度及其与电子结构的关联，并区分不同能带结构（狄拉克电子 vs. 抛物带自由电子）对自旋电流（spin current）产生的影响。

Method: 实验测量Bi$_{1-x}$Sb$_x$合金中MOKE信号随Sb浓度的变化，并分析该信号与电阻率（resistivity, ρ）和迁移率（mobility, μ_c）的标度关系；同时结合模型计算（model calculations）进行理论解释。

Result: 纯Bi（$x=0$）的MOKE信号最大，比过渡金属（transition metals）高出约四个数量级；信号随Sb浓度增加单调下降。MOKE信号与电阻率呈ρ^{1.7±0.6}标度，与迁移率呈μ_c^{2.0±0.2}标度。

Conclusion: 狄拉克电子是MOKE信号的主要来源，与抛物带自由电子的ρ^2和μ_c^{-2}标度行为不同。MOKE信号与电阻率的标度关系部分解释了金属、半金属和半导体之间信号的量级差异。电流诱导MOKE可作为表征不同电子结构材料中自旋电流性质的有效手段。

Abstract: We study the current-induced magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) in Bi$_{1-x}$Sb$_x$ semi-metalic alloys. The MOKE signal is found to be the largest in pure Bi ($x=0$), exceeding that of transition metals by nearly four orders of magnitude, and decreases monotonically with increasing Sb concentration. We find the MOKE signal scales with the resistivity ($ρ$) as $ρ^{1.7 \pm 0.6}$ and with the mobility ($μ_\mathrm{c}$) as $μ_\mathrm{c}^{2.0 \pm 0.2}$. Model calculations show that such exponent can be accounted for if the Dirac electrons are responsible for the generation of spin current. This is in contrast to the $ρ^{2}$ and $μ_\mathrm{c}^{-2}$ scaling of the MOKE signal induced by the free electrons in parabolic band. The scaling of the MOKE amplitude with the resistivity also partly accounts for the order of magnitude differences of the signal observed between metals, semimetals, and semiconductors. These results demonstrate that current induced MOKE serves as an effective means to characterize the nature of spin current in materials with diverse electronic structures.

### [77] [Impurity-induced geometric correlations and fractional quantization in quantum Hall systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15022)
*M. A. Hidalgo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于杂质诱导关联（impurity-induced correlations）的几何机制来解释分数量子霍尔态（fractional quantum Hall states），通过朗道能级内电离杂质的关联分布改变能级简并度（degeneracy），产生分数能量子能级（fractional energy sublevels），自然导出奇分母分数量子霍尔序列，并预测了分数量子霍尔态稳定性对杂质几何构型与层间距的强依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分数量子霍尔效应（fractional quantum Hall effect）理论主要依赖电子-电子相互作用和复合费米子（composite fermion）图像，尚缺乏对杂质几何效应在分数态形成中作用的系统性理解。本文旨在探索杂质诱导的几何关联是否构成分数量子霍尔系统的一个额外组织原理（organizing principle）。

Method: 提出一种基于朗道能级（Landau level）内电离杂质关联分布的几何机制。通过杂质诱导的关联分布部分改变朗道能级简并度，利用回旋轨道（cyclotron orbits）之间的相干耦合（coherent coupling）生成分数能量子能级。该机制利用内禀的引导中心量子化（guiding-center quantization）和关联回旋运动自然导出奇分母层级（odd-denominator hierarchy）。

Result: 该机制复现了实验上观察到的主要分数量子霍尔序列。预测分数量子霍尔态的稳定性对杂质几何构型（impurity geometry）和层分离（layer separation）具有强依赖关系。填充因子（filling factor）ν=1/2处不出现不可压缩霍尔平台（incompressible Hall plateau）的原因被归因于产生奇分母态所需的几何关联被抵消。

Conclusion: 杂质诱导的几何关联可能构成量子霍尔系统（quantum Hall systems）中一个额外的组织原理，对理解分数量子霍尔态的起源提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: We propose a geometric mechanism for fractional quantum Hall states based on impurity-induced correlations within a Landau level. A correlated distribution of ionized impurities partially modifies the Landau-level degeneracy through coherent coupling between cyclotron orbits, generating fractional energy sublevels. The odd-denominator hierarchy emerges naturally from the intrinsic guiding-center quantization and the correlated cyclotron motion. The resulting spectrum reproduces the principal experimentally observed fractional sequences and predicts a strong dependence of fractional-state stability on impurity geometry and layer separation. The absence of an incompressible Hall plateau at filling factor 1/2 follows from cancellation of the geometric correlations responsible for odd-denominator states. These results suggest that impurity-induced geometry may constitute an additional organizing principle in quantum Hall systems.

</details>


### [78] [Oscillatory photoresistance on the high field side of the cyclotron resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15111)
*M. A. Zudov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文在短程无序（short-range disorder）和高辐射功率极限下，研究了重叠朗道能级（overlapping Landau levels）中位移对光电阻（photoresistance）的贡献，提出了一类新型磁阻振荡——无线电波诱导电阻振荡（RIROs），其特征包括振幅不受功率影响、周期由辐射电场而非频率决定、以及可呈现1/B或1/B²周期性，并指出其实验上易于观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在远小于回旋频率（cyclotron frequency）的辐射频率下，探究重叠朗道能级中位移效应对光电阻的影响，揭示区别于已知微波诱导电阻振荡（microwave-induced resistance oscillations）的新振荡现象。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，在短程无序和高辐射功率的极限条件下，推导位移项对光电阻的贡献，并分析新磁阻振荡的振幅、周期和周期性特征。

Result: 发现了无线电波诱导电阻振荡（RIROs），其振幅与辐射功率无关；周期由辐射电场强度控制，而非辐射频率；行为可呈现1/B或1/B²周期性，交叉点与回旋共振吸收曲线的宽度相关联。

Conclusion: 该理论预测的RIROs在实验条件下应可直接观测到，为二维电子系统中的磁阻振荡研究提供了新的方向。

Abstract: We consider the displacement contribution to photoresistance in overlapping Landau levels at radiation frequencies much smaller than the cyclotron frequency. We show that in the limit of short-range disorder and high radiation power, this contribution leads to a new class of magneto-resistance oscillations. These oscillations, which we call radiowave-induced resistance oscillations (RIROs), are distinct from the well known microwave-induced resistance oscillations in the following aspects: (i) their amplitude is independent of power, (ii) their period is controlled by the radiation electric field, rather than by the radiation frequency, and (iii) they can be either $1/B$ or $1/B^2$-periodic, depending on $B$, with the crossover point linked to the width of the cyclotron resonance absorption curve. We also show that RIROs should be readily observed in experiments.

</details>

### [79] [Laboratory rivers extremize friction and are cosmological analogues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14670)
*Valerio Faraoni,Nikki Veilleux*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索浅水近似（shallow water approximation）下实验室河流横截面轮廓的微分方程与宇宙学方程之间的形式联系，并基于该类比重新审视河流横截面轮廓的变分原理。

Method: 首先证明实验室河流横截面轮廓的微分方程在形式上等同于描述反德西特宇宙演化的弗里德曼方程；进而利用该宇宙学类比推导出河流横截面的拉格朗日量，并通过对作用量（action）进行二阶变分（second variation）分析来判定极值性质。

Result: 河流横截面轮廓的微分方程在形式上与反德西特宇宙的弗里德曼方程等价；由此得到的拉格朗日量导出的作用量的极值对应河底摩擦力及能量耗散率的极值；二阶变分分析表明该极值为极大值（maximum）。

Conclusion: 实验室河流的横截面轮廓可通过宇宙学类比获得一个反直觉的拉格朗日量，其变分原理揭示河流在横截面上以最大化河底摩擦力和能量耗散率的方式达到稳态。

Abstract: In the shallow water approximation, the cross-sectional profiles of laboratory rivers satisfy a differential equation here shown to be formally the Friedmann equation of cosmology ruling the evolution of Anti-de Sitter universe. The ensuing cosmic analogy provides a counterintuitive Lagrangian for the transverse river profile. Extremizing the corresponding action corresponds to extremizing the friction force on the river bottom and the energy dissipation rate. Analysis of the second variation establishes that this extremum is a maximum.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
