Method: 研究涵盖净电荷涨落（net-electric charge fluctuations）分析、π-π费米子对分析（femtoscopy）以及质子和负电荷强子的间歇性（intermittency）分析。此外，还发展了解决间歇性分析中逐箱相关（bin-by-bin correlations）问题的新方法，并改进系统误差与不确定度处理。

Result: 在上述分析中，迄今未观察到QCD临界点的明确迹象（clear indication）。

Conclusion: 目前尚无临界点的明确实验证据，但新方法的开发有望更精确地处理间歇性分析中的系统误差与不确定度，为进一步搜索提供支持。

Abstract: The NA61/SHINE experiment at the CERN SPS is a multipurpose fixed-target spectrometer for charged and neutral hadron measurements. Its research program includes studies of strong interactions as well as reference measurements for neutrino and cosmic-ray physics. One major goal of its strong interaction program is to determine the existence and pinpoint the location of the QCD critical point, an object of both experimental and theoretical studies.
  This contribution will summarize the current status of NA61/SHINE critical point searches in nucleus-nucleus collisions, in the collision energy range $\sqrt{s_{NN}} = 5-17$~GeV. The review includes studies of fluctuations of net-electric charge, femtoscopy analysis of $π-π$ pairs, as well as intermittency of protons and negatively charged hadrons. No clear indication of the critical point has been observed so far. Finally, we report on the development of novel methods aimed at solving the long-standing problem of bin-by-bin correlations in experimental intermittency analysis, and for a more accurate handling of systematics and uncertainties.

### [81] [Rongzai agent: A Large Language Model-Based Autonomous Assistant for Rietveld Refinement of Neutron Diffraction Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13911)
*Qingmeng Li,Hao Wang,Dongbo Xiong,Jiajun Zhong,Wenhai Ji,Hao Hu,Yiyu Zhang,Bolun Zhang,Hong Wang,Yongfeng Zhu,Rong Du,Zhengde Zhang,Fazhi Qi,Junrong Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于大语言模型（LLM）、专家知识库和GSAS-II精修引擎的自主精修助手Dr.Sai-Rongzai，实现了中子衍射数据Rietveld精修的全自动化流程，在多个样品上的精修结果达到或接近人类专家水平，并在中国散裂中子源部署使用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文构建了Dr.Sai-Rongzai智能体，它基于大语言模型（large language model, LLM）、专家知识库（specialist knowledge base）和GSAS-II精修引擎，首次实现了知识驱动决策的智能精修。该智能体完成了从自然语言任务解析到自主决策、精修策略执行和报告生成的完全自动化工作流。

Result: 在五个代表性样品上的评估显示，Rongzai智能体在三个样品上取得了比人类专家更低的Rwp值（2.88% vs. 4.42%，5.06% vs. 5.40%，7.60% vs. 9.00%），在另外两个样品上的结果与专家非常接近。该智能体已部署于中国散裂中子源（China Spallation Neutron Source, CSNS）并开放外部用户注册。

Conclusion: 该工作充分利用了大语言模型的前沿优势，为解决自动化精修这一长期难题提供了新路径，向智能化和全自动化的晶体学分析迈出了关键一步，并有望加速中子材料表征领域的AI for Science发现。

Abstract: Neutron diffraction (ND) is an indispensable technique for determining atomic positions (especially light elements) and thus serves as a critical probe for revealing microscopic structures in materials science. However, traditional Rietveld refinement of ND data relies heavily on manual operation of specialized software, which is time-consuming, labor-intensive, and highly dependent on user expertise, severely hindering automated analysis. The automation of Rietveld refinement has long been a long-standing and challenging problem in crystallography. To address this challenge, this paper presents the Dr.Sai-Rongzai agent, an autonomous refinement assistant based on a large language model (LLM), a specialist knowledge base, and the GSAS-II refinement engine, achieving for the first time an intelligent refinement that integrates knowledge-driven decision-making. The agent accomplishes a fully automated workflow from natural language task parsing to autonomous decision-making, execution of refinement strategies, and report generation. Evaluation on five representative samples shows that the Rongzai agent achieves lower Rwp values than human specialists on three samples (2.88% vs. 4.42%, 5.06% vs. 5.40%, 7.60% vs. 9.00%), while on the other two samples its results are very close to those of the specialists. The agent is currently deployed at the China Spallation Neutron Source (CSNS) and is open for external user registration, providing an intelligent and user-friendly analytical tool for materials research. This work fully leverages the cutting-edge advantages of LLM, offers a new path to solve the long-standing problem of automated refinement, takes a key step toward intelligent and fully automated crystallographic analysis, and holds great potential to accelerate AI for Science discoveries in neutron-based materials characterization.

</details>


### [82] [A Neural-Network Framework to Learn History-Dependent Constitutive Laws and Identifiability of Internal Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14179)
*Mayank Raj,Lianghao Cao,Andrew Stuart,Kaushik Bhattacharya*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种因果且基于能量的公式（causal and energetic formulation），用于学习历史依赖型本构律（history-dependent constitutive law），确保其与热力学第二定律、材料稳定性及控制方程解的存在性理论一致；在多晶镁单元的泰勒平均响应（Taylor-averaged response）学习中实现了2%的相对预测误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工程中广泛存在的本构律（constitutive law）识别——无论是将实验数据拟合到数学模型，还是学习替代模型（surrogate model）以规避多尺度数值模拟中的FE²高昂计算成本——所得到的模型若不配备势能公式（potential formulation），则未必满足热力学第二定律、极端应变下的材料稳定性以及控制方程解的存在性数学理论，因此亟需一种在物理和数学上一致的学习框架。

Method: 采用因果且基于能量的公式来学习历史依赖型本构律；通过对内变量（internal variables）类别的刻画，揭示了本构律等价替代模型（equivalent surrogate models）的等价类，并证明了从数据中学习到的内变量在线性变换意义下是唯一的。

Result: 将该框架应用于多晶镁（polycrystalline magnesium）单胞的泰勒平均响应学习，预测的泰勒平均响应相对误差为2%。

Conclusion: 所提出的因果-能量框架能够学习出满足热力学一致性、材料稳定性及数学适定性（well-posedness）的历史依赖型本构律；内变量的唯一性（至多相差一个线性变换）为替代模型的等价类提供了理论保证，并在实际多晶材料案例中展现了高精度。

Abstract: The identification of constitutive laws is ubiquitous in engineering: in modeling of materials where experimental data are fitted to mathematical models or learning surrogate models to beat the FE\textsuperscript{2} computational cost of multiscale numerical simulations. However, these models of constitutive laws, unless equipped with a potential formulation, are not necessarily consistent with (a) the second law of thermodynamics; (b) stability of the material under extreme applied strain; and (c) the mathematical theory underpinning the existence of solutions of the governing equation. In this work, we present a causal and energetic formulation, consistent with aforementioned properties, of learning a history-dependent constitutive law. This characterization of the class of internal variables sheds light on the equivalence class of equivalent surrogate models for the constitutive law. We show that the internal variables that are learned from the data are unique up to a linear transform. The framework is deployed to learn the Taylor-averaged response of a polycrystalline magnesium unit cell. We achieve 2\% relative error in the prediction of the Taylor-averaged response.

### [83] [Carrier-density dependence of magnetotransport in correlated Dirac semimetal CaIrO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14180)
*Rinsuke Yamada,Jun Fujioka,Minoru Kawamura,Tatsuya Okawa,Yoshio Kaneko,Shiro Sakai,Motoaki Hirayama,Ryotaro Arita,Kiyohiro Adachi,Daisuke Hashizume,Yoshinori Tokura*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文报道了关联狄拉克半金属（correlated Dirac semimetal）CaIrO₃中磁输运性质对载流子浓度的依赖性研究。在低载流子浓度区域（约2.2×10¹⁶ cm⁻³，2 K）观测到超过1.0×10⁵ cm²/Vs的高迁移率和高达2000%（12 T）的横向磁电阻（magnetoresistance）。量子振荡和霍尔电导分析表明费米速度（Fermi velocity）与费米面横截面积（即载流子浓度）几乎无关，支持狄拉克节点（Dirac node）的k线性色散关系。磁阻率（magnetoresistivity）的磁场依赖性在中载流子浓度区域近似为B线性，在更低载流子浓度区域则标度为Bᵅ（α>2），其变化可能受到量子极限（quantum limit）下增强的长程库仑相互作用（long-range Coulomb interaction）的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索关联狄拉克半金属CaIrO₃中磁输运性质随载流子浓度的演化规律，特别关注狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermions）在量子极限下的行为及其与长程库仑相互作用的关联。

Method: 通过测量不同载流子浓度下CaIrO₃的磁输运性质（包括迁移率、横向磁电阻、磁阻率），并结合量子振荡（quantum oscillations）和霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）分析，提取费米速度等电子结构信息，研究其与载流子浓度的关系。

Result: 低载流子浓度区域（~2.2×10¹⁶ cm⁻³）在2 K下迁移率超过1.0×10⁵ cm²/Vs，横向磁电阻在12 T下达2000%；费米速度几乎不依赖于费米面横截面积（即载流子浓度），支持狄拉克节点的k线性色散；磁阻率在中载流子浓度区域（n_H ≥ 4×10¹⁶ cm⁻³）近似为B线性，在更低浓度区域标度为Bᵅ（α>2）。

Conclusion: CaIrO₃中狄拉克费米子的k线性色散关系得到实验支持，而磁阻率在低载流子浓度区域的超线性磁场依赖性可能源于量子极限下增强的长程库仑相互作用效应。

Abstract: We report the carrier density dependence of the magnetotransport property in the correlated Dirac semimetal CaIrO$_3$. In the dilute carrier density region ($n_{\rm H}$ $\sim 2.2 \times 10^{16} \,$$\rm{cm}^{-3}$) at $2 \, \mathrm{K}$, the mobility exceeds $1.0 \times 10^{5} \,$$\rm{cm}^{2}/\rm{Vs}$ at $2 \, \mathrm{K}$, and the transverse magnetoresistance (MR) reaches $2,000 \,$\% at $12 \, \mathrm{T}$. The analysis of quantum oscillations and Hall conductivity shows that the Fermi velocity is nearly independent of the cross-sectional area of the Fermi surface, or equivalently the carrier density, supporting a $k$-linear dispersion of the Dirac node. The field dependence of magnetoresistivity is nearly $B$-linear in the moderate carrier density region ($n_\mathrm{H} \geq 4 \times 10^{16}\,$cm$^{-3}$), but scales with $B^α$ ($α> 2$) in the lower carrier density region. The variation of magnetoresistivity is likely affected by the enhanced long-range Coulomb interaction in the quantum limit, where Dirac electrons are subject to the magnetic confinement.

### [84] [Machine-learning-identified two-dimensional van der Waals multiferroics for four-state nonvolatile memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14303)
*Zhibin Tan,Tao Wang,Hao Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过机器学习筛选结合第一性原理计算，在二维范德华ABC₂X₆家族中发现了一系列高置信度多铁材料，其中AuCrP₂S₆单层具有铁磁基态、可观的面外极化和适中的铁电翻转势垒，并利用非线性光学体光伏效应实现了四种逻辑状态的非破坏性读出，为下一代多态光电存储提供了可行方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文将机器学习筛选（machine-learning screening）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）相结合，系统探索了二维范德华ABC₂X₆家族，从中识别出一组高置信度多铁候选材料。

Result: AuCrP₂S₆单层被确定为代表性体系，具有铁磁基态（ferromagnetic ground state）、大小为7.46 pC/m的面外极化（out-of-plane polarization），以及约130 meV/f.u.的适中铁电翻转势垒（ferroelectric switching barrier）。基于体光伏效应（bulk photovoltaic effect, BPVE）的非线性光学响应可提供双通道探针：极化方向决定光电流符号，磁序通过稳健的交换劈裂选择自旋通道。

Conclusion: 该材料中固有的耦合机制实现了在单个原子层内对四种逻辑状态的非破坏性读出，为下一代多态光电存储（multistate optoelectronic memory）提供了实用的蓝图。

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals (vdW) multiferroics offer an attractive platform for four-state nonvolatile memory by combining switchable ferroelectric polarization and magnetization within a single material system. However, their development is hindered by the scarcity of synthesizable candidates and the lack of non-destructive readout schemes. Here, we combine machine-learning screening with first-principles calculations to explore the 2D vdW ABC$_2$X$_6$ family and identify a set of high-confidence multiferroic candidates. Among them, AuCrP$_2$S$_6$ monolayer emerges as a representative system with a ferromagnetic ground state, a sizable out-of-plane polarization of 7.46 pC/m, and a moderate ferroelectric switching barrier of $\sim$130 meV/f.u. Moreover, the nonlinear optical response mediated by the bulk photovoltaic effect (BPVE) in AuCrP$_2$S$_6$ provides a dual-channel probe of the ferroic orders, in which the polarization direction governs the photocurrent sign while the magnetic order selects the spin channel via robust exchange splitting. This intrinsic coupling enables the non-destructive readout of four logic states within a single atomic layer, thereby providing a practical blueprint for next-generation multistate optoelectronic memory.

### [85] [Unified definition of ferroelectricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14328)
*Wei Luo,Shihan Deng,Hongjun Xiang,Laurent Bellaiche*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于可切换极化差异（switchable polarization differences）的统一铁电体定义，克服了传统极性空间群判据的局限，并据此开展高通量筛选，发现了一种全新的量子铁电体类型——任意离子位移即可产生量子化极化，并识别出Ba3I6和Cs2PdC2等具备低切换势垒和优异绝缘性的实验可行材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子铁电体（quantum ferroelectrics）的最新理论与实验进展表明，铁电性也可出现在非极性空间群（non-polar space group）中，这凸显了传统极性空间群判据在识别铁电材料方面的局限性，亟需建立更普适的定义与筛选方法。

Method: 提出基于能量等价态之间可切换极化差异的统一铁电体定义；基于该定义，对实验已合成的材料实施高通量筛选（high-throughput screening）策略，系统识别常规铁电体与量子铁电体。

Result: 发现了一种新型量子铁电体，其量子化极化（quantized polarization）来源于任意离子位移，区别于此前分数或整数离子位移产生的量子化极化；识别出Ba3I6和Cs2PdC2等材料具有低切换势垒和鲁棒的绝缘行为。

Conclusion: 该研究统一了常规铁电体与量子铁电体的框架，拓展了可探索的材料空间，并为发现具有先进可切换功能性的下一代铁电体提供了实用路线图。

Abstract: Recent theoretical and experimental advances in quantum ferroelectrics suggest that ferroelectricity can also emerge in non-polar space group, highlighting the limitations of conventional polar space group criteria in identifying ferroelectric materials. Here, we introduce a unified definition based on switchable polarization differences between energetically equivalent states, which naturally encompasses conventional and quantum ferroelectrics. Guided by this principle, we implement a high-throughput screening strategy that systematically identifies both conventional and quantum ferroelectrics among experimentally synthesized materials. In particular, we identify a new type of quantum ferroelectric in which the quantized polarization arises from arbitrary ionic displacements, in contrast to previous quantum ferroelectrics (including both fractional and integer quantum ferroelectrics) where quantized polarization results from fractional or integer ionic displacements. Notably, we find that materials such as Ba3I6 and Cs2PdC2 exhibit low switching barriers and robust insulating behavior, highlighting their experimental viability. Our results reconcile conventional and quantum ferroelectrics, expand the accessible materials landscape, and provide a practical roadmap for discovering next-generation ferroelectrics with advanced switchable functionalities.

Method: 在蓝宝石衬底上生长N极性AlN，并采用5.2 nm厚的GaN沟道层，利用突变的AlN/GaN异质结（abrupt AlN/GaN heterostructure）以及专用的AlN过渡层（AlN transition layer）来优化界面质量和抑制漏电。

Conclusion: 通过优化AlN/GaN异质结构及引入专用过渡层，显著提升了N极性AlN基HEMT的开关比和栅极漏电特性；但沟道层的高薄层电阻仍对器件的高频性能和导通电阻构成主要限制因素。

Abstract: We report N-polar AlN-based high-electron mobility transistors (HEMTs) with a GaN channel thickness of 5.2 nm on N-polar AlN on sapphire. The threshold voltage is around -2.4 to -3.0 V with saturation currents over 240 mA/mm and on/off ratios as high as 10,000, much higher than previously reported N-polar AlN-based HEMTs. The high on/off ratio is attributed to the use of an abrupt AlN/GaN heterostructure with a dedicated AlN transition layer, together with improved gate leakage. The high frequency properties as well as the on-resistance of ~20 Ohm mm are all limited by the 2000 Ohm/square sheet resistance of the channel layer.

### [87] [Ward identities and orbital magnetization in current density functional theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14336)
*Giovanni Vignale,Junren Shi,Di Xiao,Qian Niu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文在电流密度泛函理论（CDFT）框架下重新推导了周期晶体的轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）公式，通过长波极限下能量密度对周期磁场的线性响应计算，揭示了一个连接电流顶点（current vertex）与Kohn-Sham自能（self-energy）导数的Ward恒等式（Ward identity），并确认了文献[1]的结果：原则上可从CDFT的Kohn-Sham方程自洽本征函数与本征值精确计算相互作用固体的轨道磁化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证并完善电流密度泛函理论（CDFT）中周期晶体轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）公式的推导，解决现有推导中可能存在的理论不清晰或缺失的恒等关系。

Method: 采用长波极限（long-wavelength limit）下能量密度对周期磁场（periodic magnetic field）的线性响应（linear response）计算方法，通过分析Kohn-Sham自洽方程的结构，导出了连接电流顶点与自能导数的Ward恒等式（Ward identity）。

Result: 成功推导出一个新的Ward恒等式，该恒等式将电流顶点（current vertex）与Kohn-Sham自能对动量的导数联系起来，从而在形式上严格确认了文献[1]中轨道磁化公式的正确性。

Conclusion: 原则上，相互作用固体的轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）完全可以由CDFT中Kohn-Sham方程的自洽本征函数（self-consistent eigenfunctions）和本征值（eigenvalues）精确计算，这为实际的第一性原理计算提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: We revisit the derivation of the orbital magnetization formula for periodic crystals in current density functional theory (CDFT)[1]. Our new derivation computes the linear response of the energy density to a periodic magnetic field in the long-wavelength limit. We unveil a Ward identity which connects the current vertex to the derivative of the Kohn-Sham self-energy. The result of Ref.[1] is confirmed: the orbital magnetization of the interacting solid can be computed exactly (in principle) from the self-consistent eigenfunctions and eigenvalues of the Kohn-Sham equation of CDFT.

</details>

By transducing fabrication-induced stochastic microstates into handedness-dependent optical responses through chiroptical mapping, our platform enables native ternary digitization rather than conventional binary encoding, allowing physically harvested ternary random sequences to be used for key generation. The harvested outputs exhibit near-balanced symbol populations, negligible spatial and inter-sample correlations, Shannon entropy approaching the ternary ideal, and resistance to statistical and machine-learning-based prediction. ### [91] [Shaping Maximally Localized Wannier Functions via Discrete Adiabatic Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14414)
*Yuji Hamai,Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种非变分（non-variational）的确定性算法，用于构造最大局域瓦尼尔函数（MLWF），该方法将规范平滑与投影位置算符的本征值问题统一在一个框架中。通过对一维和二维体系的基准测试，该算法在展宽和轨道形状上与传统最小化方案一致，并揭示了石墨烯中O(L)量级网格依赖展宽标度的几何起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的最大局域瓦尼尔函数（MLWFs）构造依赖于在高维规范景观（gauge landscape）上迭代极小化展宽泛函（spread functional），该变分方法计算成本高且收敛路径复杂。本研究旨在开发一种非变分、确定性的构造算法，以提升瓦尼尔函数构造的效率和可解释性。

Method: 方法核心是一个非变分构造算法，将规范平滑（gauge smoothing）与投影位置算符（projected position operator）的本征值问题统一为单一确定性框架。通过引入输运对齐规范（transport-aligned gauge），使布洛赫重叠（Bloch overlaps）呈现近似线性相位依赖，从而利用确定性不动点迭代（fixed-point iterations）和自洽更新（self-consistent updates）提取瓦尼尔中心（Wannier centers），而非进行展宽泛函最小化。

Result: 在一维和二维体系的基准计算中，该方法得到的展宽和轨道形状与传统最小化方案吻合良好。此外，该方法清晰分离开来石墨烯中观察到的O(L)量级网格依赖展宽标度（L为边界缝分辨率），证明该标度是投影位置算符非对易（non-commuting）导致的固有几何表现，迫使有限规范缺陷（gauge defects）沿一维边界缝累积。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，离散绝热输运（discrete adiabatic transport）在能带简并（band degeneracies）处的出现是投影位置算符本征向量求解过程的自然组成部分，因此瓦尼尔函数的构造可以从变分优化范式转向确定性的解析框架，并更深刻地揭示体系几何与规范结构的内在联系。

Abstract: Maximally localized Wannier functions (MLWFs) are conventionally constructed by iteratively minimizing a spread functional over a high-dimensional gauge landscape. In this work, we present a non-variational constructive algorithm that unifies gauge smoothing and the eigenvalue problem of the projected position operator into a single deterministic framework. We demonstrate that discrete adiabatic transport across band degeneracies emerges naturally as an integral part of the solution procedure for the position eigenvectors. In this transport-aligned gauge, the Bloch overlaps exhibit an approximately linear phase dependence, allowing the Wannier centers to be extracted via deterministic fixed-point iterations and self-consistent updates rather than spread-functional minimization. Benchmark calculations for one- and two-dimensional systems yield spreads and orbital shapes in good agreement with standard minimization schemes. Furthermore, this analytical approach transparently isolates the physical origin of the $\mathcal{O}(L)$ mesh-dependent spread scaling ($L$ being the boundary seam resolution) observed in graphene, demonstrating that it is an intrinsic geometric manifestation of non-commuting projected position operators forcing finite gauge defects to accumulate along a one-dimensional boundary seam.

### [92] [High-Pressure Crystal Structure Database](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14471)
*Zhenyu Wang,Qingchang Wang,Junwen Duan,Heng Ge,Xiaoshan Luo,Pengyue Gao,Wei Zhang,Jian Lv,Yanchao Wang,Yanming Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍了高压晶体结构数据库（HPCSD），这是一个整合实验与理论高压结构的可追溯、压力可解析的数据库。初始版本包含77,346个结构条目，涵盖89种元素，所有结构均经过统一的密度泛函理论（DFT）框架重优化。分析表明高压诱导的多晶型现象普遍存在并呈现族依赖性趋势，结构多样性受元素电子适应性影响，最大结构复杂性出现在中等压力区间。HPCSD为加速实验物相鉴定、促进跨研究热力学比较以及支持机器学习势函数和生成模型开发提供了标准化基础设施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压研究是发现新结构和涌现性质的有效途径，但关键的高压结构信息高度碎片化地分散在各类文献和计算数据库中，形成了数据驱动材料设计的主要瓶颈。为弥合这一鸿沟，亟需一个标准化、可追溯且压力可解析的高压结构数据库。

Method: HPCSD通过两条互补数据流构建：元素高压相数据，以及基于CALYPSO晶体结构预测方法生成的稳定相与亚稳相的可搜索构型空间。为保证严格可比性，所有收录的结构均在统一的密度泛函理论（DFT）框架下进行重优化，并针对元素相在其稳定场范围内系统地生成连续焓曲线。

Result: 初始版本包含77,346个经一致评估的结构条目，覆盖89种元素。分析发现压力诱导的多晶型现象（pressure-induced polymorphism）普遍存在并呈现显著的族依赖性（family-dependent）趋势。结构多样性受元素的电子适应性（electronic adaptability）强烈影响，最大结构复杂性出现在中等压力而非最高压力区间。

Conclusion: HPCSD通过提供标准化、可复用且经过严格评估的高压结构数据，建立了稳健的基础设施，可加速实验物相鉴定、促进跨研究热力学比较，并支持高压系统的机器学习原子间势函数（machine-learning interatomic potentials）和生成模型（generative models）的开发。

Abstract: High-pressure research is a productive route to new structures and emergent properties. However, crucial high-pressure structural information remains highly fragmented across individual publications and heterogeneous computational repositories. This fragmentation creates a major bottleneck for data-driven materials design. To bridge this gap, we introduce the High-Pressure Crystal Structure Database (HPCSD), a traceable, pressure-resolved repository that integrates experimental and theoretical high-pressure structures. HPCSD is constructed from two complementary data streams: elemental high-pressure phases and a searchable configuration space of stable and metastable phases generated via CALYPSO crystal structure prediction. To ensure rigorous comparability, all retained structures underwent re-optimization under a unified density functional theory (DFT) framework , with continuous enthalpy curves systematically generated specifically for the elemental phases across their stability fields. The initial release encompasses 77,346 consistently evaluated structural entries spanning 89 elements. An analysis reveals that pressure-induced polymorphism is ubiquitous and exhibits pronounced family-dependent trends. Structural diversity is strongly influenced by an element's electronic adaptability , with the greatest structural complexity emerging at intermediate rather than highest pressures. By providing standardized, reusable, and rigorously evaluated high-pressure structural data, HPCSD establishes a robust infrastructure to accelerate experimental phase identification, facilitate cross-study thermodynamic comparisons, and support the development of machine-learning interatomic potentials and generative models for high-pressure systems.

### [93] [Accurate computation of the electron-phonon interaction contribution to the total energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14472)
*Shilpa Paul,Mogadalai Pandurangan Gururajan,Amrita Bhattacharya,Tiramkudlu R. S. Prasanna*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文指出标准电子-声子耦合哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）基于二阶微扰理论，其部分Fan-Migdal占据项（partial-FM-occ）实际具有高阶项结构。作者在非绝热近似（non-adiabatic approximation）下推导了该贡献的新表达式，并将其首次应用于碳同素异形体（金刚石和六方蓝丝黛尔石）的总能量计算，获得了迄今最精确的从头算（ab initio）总能量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在非绝热近似下解析推导partial-FM-occ项的新表达式，表明其具有高阶项结构而非二阶项；将该表达式用于碳同素异形体（金刚石和六方蓝丝黛尔石）的从头算总能量计算，首次纳入EPI对总能量的贡献。

Result: 新的partial-FM-occ表达式包含了该贡献的完整物理内涵，应在理论和计算研究中优先使用。对于所有材料（包括红外活性材料和非红外活性材料），总能量的EPI贡献必须在非绝热近似下计算。首次将标准哈密顿量（含EPI总能量贡献）应用于碳同素异形体，获得了迄今最精确的从头算总能量。

Conclusion: 修正后的partial-FM-occ表达式优于标准形式；该方法为在有限温度下更精确地计算从头算自由能（free-energy）开辟了道路——通过纳入EPI贡献。

Abstract: The standard Hamiltonian of a coupled electron-phonon system is based on second-order perturbation theory. The EPI contribution in the standard Hamiltonian consists of two terms, the EPI contribution to the band-structure energy and the partial-Fan-Migdal (FM)-occupied contribution. Within the non-adiabatic approximation, we derive a new expression for the partial-FM-occ contribution and show that it has the structure of a higher-order term, and not a second-order term. Along similar lines, we derive new expressions for the computation of the partial-FM-occ term. The new expressions for the partial-FM-occ term must be preferred over the standard expressions, in theoretical and computational studies, because they incorporate the complete physics underlying this term. Unlike the EPI contribution to individual eigenstates, the EPI contribution to the total energy must be computed in the non-adiabatic approximation for all materials, Infra-red (IR) active and IR-inactive. We report the computation of the standard Hamiltonian, for the first time, for Carbon polymorphs (diamond and hexagonal lonsdaleite) by including the EPI contribution to the total energy. This is the most accurate ab initio total energy reported till date. The present work also opens the way to compute the ab initio free-energy more accurately at finite temperatures by including the EPI contribution.

### [94] [Probing the Chirality of Trigonal Selenium and Tellurium by Spin and Orbital Hall Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14506)
*Yuting Xiong,Yingjie Hu,Wei Ren,Heng Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，揭示了手性晶体（硒和碲）中自旋霍尔电导（spin Hall conductivity, SHC）和轨道霍尔电导（orbital Hall conductivity, OHC）的符号在手性对映体之间完全相反，其根源在于镜面对称操作导致的自旋/轨道贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的反对称变换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性晶体（chiral crystals）表现出对映体依赖的输运现象，能够产生纯自旋流或纯轨道流，但自旋霍尔电导（SHC）和轨道霍尔电导（OHC）对结构手性（handedness）的敏感性尚未被充分理解。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），对三角相硒和碲（trigonal selenium and tellurium）这一原型手性半导体（chiral semiconductors）的左、右手性对映体分别计算其SHC/OHC张量分量。

Result: 左、右手性对映体（空间群 $P3_221$ 与 $P3_121$）的SHC/OHC张量分量 $σ_{yx}^{S_y}$ 和 $σ_{yx}^{L_y}$ 呈现符号相反；两种对映体能带结构完全相同且均有四个非零SHC/OHC张量分量，但 $σ_{yx}^{S_y}$ 和 $σ_{yx}^{L_y}$ 因 $M_{xy}$ 镜面操作下自旋/轨道贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的反对称变换而发生符号反转。

Conclusion: 对于镜面对映（mirror-related enantiomorphic）结构，选定的SHC/OHC张量分量可表现出由对称性支配的符号反转；可测量SHC/OHC信号与结构手性之间存在直接关联，为通过输运实验判定手性材料的绝对构型提供了可能的途径。

Abstract: Chiral crystals exhibit enantiomer-dependent transport phenomena that generate pure spin or orbital currents, while the handedness sensitivity of spin and orbital Hall conductivities (SHC/OHC) remains insufficiently understood. Using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that trigonal selenium and tellurium -- prototypical chiral semiconductors -- exhibit opposite signs of the SHC/OHC tensor elements $σ_{yx}^{S_y}$ and $σ_{yx}^{L_y}$ between their left- and right-handed enantiomers. This behavior originates from the mirror operation relating the two structures, described by space groups $P3_221$ (left-handed) and $P3_121$ (right-handed). Although both enantiomers share identical band structures and four nonzero SHC/OHC tensor components, $σ_{yx}^{S_y}$ and $σ_{yx}^{L_y}$ reverse sign due to the antisymmetric transformation of the spin/orbital Berry curvature under the $M_{xy}$ mirror operation. More generally, for mirror-related enantiomorphic structures, selected SHC/OHC tensor components can exhibit symmetry-governed sign reversal. For trigonal Se and Te, the calculated signs of these components can be directly correlated with the left- and right-handed structures under the chosen coordinate convention. These results clarify the symmetry origin of handedness-dependent SHC/OHC and suggest a possible route for correlating measurable SHC/OHC signals with structural handedness in specific chiral materials.

</details>


### [95] [Methane hydrate nucleation frustration and dimensional reduction of structural order under nanoconfinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14533)
*Jose Torres-Arenas,Ángel M. Fernández-Fernández,Martín Pérez-Rodríguez,Manuel M. Piñeiro*

Method: 采用二氧化硅（silica）平面狭缝孔隙模型，孔隙宽度为1至5 nm，温度范围为250至295 K。利用三维径向分布函数（three-dimensional radial distribution functions）和二维投影相关函数（projected two-dimensional correlations）分别表征体相和平面内的结构有序性。

Result: 三维径向分布函数显示，在强约束（<2 nm）条件下，水合物状有序性（hydrate-like ordering）被显著抑制，表明成核受阻。二维投影相关函数则表现出明显的面内结构组织化，证实约束导致了分子有序维度的降低（reduction in dimensionality）。

Conclusion: 纳米约束通过降低有序维度来重新组织水-甲烷体系的分子排列，使得平面内结构增强而体相有序性受阻。这一发现揭示了约束诱导的成核抑制机制，并突显了维度降低在受限水合物成核中的关键作用。

Abstract: Methane hydrate nucleation under nanoconfinement remains poorly understood due to the complex interplay between geometric restriction and molecular ordering. Here, we investigate the structural organization of water-methane systems confined between silica planar slit pores with widths ranging from 1 to 5 nm and temperatures between 250 and 295 K. Three-dimensional radial distribution functions reveal a clear suppression of hydrate-like ordering at strong confinement (below 2 nm), indicating frustrated nucleation. In contrast, projected two-dimensional correlations exhibit pronounced in-plane structural organization, evidencing a confinement-induced reduction in the dimensionality of molecular order.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）结合从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）以及基于Langmuir模型的统计热力学建模（Langmuir-based statistical thermodynamic modeling）进行计算分析。

Conclusion: N-GDY被确认为一种化学可调的骨架结构，可用于分散轻金属，并为在多孔二维材料中实现高容量、可逆氢存储提供了机制设计策略。

Abstract: Hydrogen (H2) is a promising carbon-neutral energy carrier. However, its deployment is limited by the lack of lightweight, reversible storage media that operate under practical conditions. AIMD simulations at 400 K further confirm the structural robustness of the decorated frameworks and the absence of metal aggregation. The polarised metal centres activate reversible H2 adsorption through electrostatic and dispersion interactions, with average adsorption energies falling within the optimal window (-0.15 to -0.35 eV per H2). Sequential adsorption analysis reveals uptake of up to 25 H2 molecules per primitive cell, achieving intrinsic gravimetric capacities of 13.08, 10.82, 9.23, and 9.15 wt% for Li-, Na-, K-, and Ca-functionalized systems, respectively. Thermodynamic analysis indicates favorable adsorption-desorption behavior under near-ambient conditions, with Li- and Ca-functionalized systems exceeding the 6.5 wt% U.S. Department of Energy's ultimate system-level target when considering intrinsic material capacity. Conclusion: 自动研究智能体能够在运行过程中无需人工特征工程，生成竞争性的、任务特异的材料描述符。同时揭示了当前局限性：描述符冗余（descriptor redundancy）、对贪婪特征扩展（greedy feature expansion）的敏感性，以及需要显式复杂度控制、描述符剪枝和更复杂的搜索策略。

Abstract: Autoresearch offers a flexible paradigm for automating scientific tasks, in which an AI agent proposes, implements, evaluates, and refines candidate solutions against a quantitative objective. Here, we use composition-based materials-property prediction to test whether such agents can perform a task beyond model selection and hyperparameter optimization: the design of input descriptors. We introduce Automat, an autoresearch framework where a coding agent based on a large language model generates composition-only descriptors for chemical compounds and evaluates them using a random forest workflow. The agent is restricted to information derivable from chemical formulas and iteratively proposes, implements, and tests chemically motivated descriptor strategies. We apply Automat, with OpenAI Codex using GPT-5.5 as the coding agent, to the prediction of experimental band gaps in inorganic materials and Curie temperatures in ferromagnetic compounds. In both tasks, Automat improves over fractional-composition, Magpie, and combined fractional-composition/Magpie baselines, while producing descriptor families that are chemically interpretable. These results provide a demonstration that autoresearch agents can generate competitive, task-specific materials descriptors without manual feature engineering during the run. They also reveal current limitations, including descriptor redundancy, sensitivity to greedy feature expansion, and the need for explicit complexity control, descriptor pruning, and more sophisticated search strategies.

### [98] [Telecom-Wavelength-Compatible Quantum Information Transcription Using Nitrogen-Vacancy Centers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14697)

Result: 直接观测到1042 nm发射中的ODMR对比度，并发现该信号随磁场呈现光谱色散；自旋态信息通过自旋选择性系间穿越（spin-selective intersystem crossing）从三重态转录至红外单重态发射，其机制与可见荧光读出类似。

Conclusion: 红外ODMR可作为高保真度光学读出通路；将自旋态转录扩展至1300–1600 nm电信波段，实现了金刚石自旋量子比特与标准电信基础设施的直接、无频率转换接口，避开了主动频率转换的效率瓶颈。

Abstract: Nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond are a leading platform for solid-state quantum sensing and quantum information processing. While most optical studies rely on the visible fluorescence associated with the triplet transitions, the infrared singlet transition near $1042$ nm, which is typically considered dark within the singlet manifold of the NV optical cycle, provides an alternative optical channel. Here, we report wavelength-resolved optically detected magnetic resonance (ODMR) measurements of this infrared emission. We directly observe ODMR contrast in the $1042$ nm emission and analyze its dependence on the magnetic field. The field-dependent spectral dispersion of the ODMR signal demonstrates that the spin-state information encoded in the NV center is transcribed to the infrared singlet emission through the spin-selective intersystem crossing, in close analogy to the visible fluorescence readout. These results establish infrared ODMR as a high-fidelity optical readout pathway. Crucially, by extending spin-state transcription directly into the $1300-1600$ nm range, this work demonstrates a direct, conversion-free interface between diamond spin-qubits and standard telecommunication infrastructure, bypassing the efficiency bottlenecks of active frequency conversion and benefiting from the already well-developed technologies in this range of the electromagnetic spectrum.

### [100] [Melting Behavior and Phase Stability of CaO from Neural Network Potentials: a Molecular Dynamics Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14793)
*Francesca Menescardi,Stefano de Gironcoli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用基于PANNA 2.0和LATTE描述符开发的机器学习原子间势（MLIP），结合大规模分子动力学模拟，计算了氧化钙（CaO）在极端条件下的熔化温度、熔化焓、热膨胀及高压熔化曲线，发现过热比（η）随压力增加而增大，验证了MLIP在离子氧化物相稳定性研究中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化钙（CaO）在极端条件下的熔化行为因实验限制而研究不足，但其对地球物理和技术应用具有重要意义，因此亟需可靠的数值方法来表征其高温高压相变特性。

Method: 使用PANNA 2.0和LATTE描述符构建机器学习原子间势（Machine Learning Interatomic Potential, MLIP），训练数据集包含约12,000个构型，涵盖固相、液相、界面及含空洞结构，数据源于基于PBEsol交换关联泛函的从头算分子动力学模拟；采用空洞成核熔化法和两相共存法进行大规模分子动力学模拟。

Result: 常压下VNM法测得熔化温度Tm=3055±11 K，TPC法测得Tm=2847±15 K；熔化焓ΔHf≈73 kJ/mol；熔化时体积膨胀约29%；高压熔化曲线计算至20 GPa，过热比η从常压的17%上升至20 GPa时的24%。

Conclusion: 基于MLIP的模拟为离子氧化物（ionic oxides）的相稳定性研究提供了稳健高效的计算框架，否定了固定过热比假设，并为CaO在极端条件下的熔化行为提供了新的认识。

Abstract: We investigate the melting behavior of calcium oxide (CaO) under extreme conditions, a problem that remains poorly constrained due to experimental limitations despite its relevance for geophysical and technological applications. We develop a Machine Learning Interatomic Potential (MLIP) for CaO with PANNA 2.0 and the LATTE descriptor, training it on a dataset of $\sim$12,000 configurations including solid, liquid, interfacial, and void-containing structures, extracted from ab-initio molecular dynamics data employing PBEsol exchange-correlation functional. We perform large-scale molecular dynamics simulations to compute the melting temperature at ambient pressure using both the void-nucleated melting (VNM) and two-phase coexistence (TPC) methods, obtaining $T_m=3055\pm11$ K and $T_m=2847\pm15$ K, respectively.\\ We calculate an enthalpy of fusion of $ΔH_f\sim73$ kJ/mol, in agreement with thermodynamic assessments and ab initio calculations. We also reproduce the thermal expansion and obtain a volume increase of $\sim$29% at Tm, consistent with the corresponding decrease in density extracted from spatially resolved number density profiles. Finally, we calculate the high-pressure melting curve of CaO up to 20 GPa, providing one of the very few computational determinations of this quantity to date. The results confirm that the overheating ratio $η$ is not constant under pressure, increasing from 17% at ambient pressure to 24% at 20 GPa, confirming previous findings and ruling out the assumption of a fixed overheating ratio. Our results establish MLIP-based simulations as a robust and efficient framework for investigating phase stability in ionic oxides and provide new insight into the melting behavior of CaO under extreme conditions.

### [101] [Generative reconstruction of 2D and 3D polycrystalline microstructures using symmetrized hyperspherical harmonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14898)
*Ali R. Safi,Paul Seibert,Santiago Benito,Alexander Raßloff,Markus Kästner,Benjamin Klusemann*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于取向的微分微观结构表征与重建框架（MCRpy），利用单位四元数和对称化超球面谐波克服传统欧拉角的奇异性，结合两点空间相关、混合三点变差函数和均值正则化项，从二维取向数据高效重建三维多晶微观结构，并验证了其在铝合金上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立多晶材料的微观结构-性能关联需要代表性的二维和三维微观结构输入，但实际中往往仅能获取有限的二维数据。因此，如何基于少量二维参考数据生成反映目标统计系综的二维和三维微观结构，成为微观结构表征与重建的核心目标。

Method: 该框架使用单位四元数（unit quaternions）结合对称化超球面谐波（symmetrized hyperspherical harmonics）导出连续且对称不变的晶体取向表示，以克服传统基于欧拉角（Euler angles）方法的数值奇异性与不连续性。重建过程由两点空间相关函数（two-point spatial correlations）、一种新型混合三点变差函数（hybrid three-point variogram）和均值正则化项（mean variation regularizer）共同驱动，并采用基于二阶梯度优化的L-BFGS-B算法进行优化。

Result: 在热机械加工后的铝合金上，该框架成功从二维取向数据重建出三维微观结构，恢复了形态特征和晶体学分布。系统基准测试表明，L-BFGS-B算法能有效导航复杂损失景观，生成高保真微观结构且残差极小。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一个通用、开源的多晶代表性体积元（representative volume element）数字合成框架，有助于加速微观结构信息驱动的材料设计工作流开发。

Abstract: Establishing structure-property linkages in polycrystalline materials requires representative two- (2D) and three- (3D) dimensional microstructural inputs for full-field simulations. A core objective of microstructure characterization and reconstruction is the generative synthesis of 2D and 3D microstructures that reflect a target statistical ensemble using limited 2D data as a reference. This work introduces an orientation-based differentiable microstructure characterization and reconstruction framework, implemented in MCRpy, to perform reconstructions of voxelized images. Unit quaternions in combination with symmetrized hyperspherical harmonics are utilized to derive a continuous, symmetry-invariant representation of crystallographic orientations to overcome the numerical singularities and discontinuities associated with traditional Euler-based methods.
  The descriptor-based reconstructions are driven by a set combining two-point spatial correlations, a novel hybrid three-point variogram, and a mean variation regularizer to capture both global texture and local interfacial topology. The framework's efficiency is demonstrated by reconstructing 3D realizations from 2D orientation data of an aluminum alloy after thermo-mechanical processing, successfully recovering both morphological features and crystallographic distribution. Systematic benchmarking indicates that second-order gradient-based optimization, utilizing the L-BFGS-B algorithm, effectively navigates the complex loss landscape to generate high-fidelity realizations with minimal residuals. This methodology provides a versatile, open-source framework for the digital synthesis of polycrystalline representative volume elements to facilitate the rapid development of microstructure-informed materials design workflows.

</details>

It is shown that, due to the sensitivity of the Debye-Waller analysis to this parameter, neglecting its changes under electronic excitation may lead to significant deviations of the atomic temperature extracted from its true values.

### [103] [Generalized Suzuki-Chin Factorization in Bosonic Path Integral Molecular Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14687)
*Jacob Higer,Barak Hirshberg*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明广义铃木-钦因子分解（GSF）可应用于玻色子路径积分分子动力学（PIMD），以重加权因子形式实现，在不改变原始采样的情况下将平衡平均值的收敛速度提升约2-4倍，且计算成本较低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代可区分粒子的PIMD模拟常使用高阶因子分解方案（如GSF）来加速平衡平均值的收敛。本文旨在将GSF推广至全同玻色子（bosons）和费米子（fermions）系统，以提升其PIMD模拟的收敛效率。

Method: 将GSF分解实现为可观测量（observables）的重加权因子（re-weighting factor），而不影响由标准二阶原始因子分解（primitive factorization）生成的抽样过程；该方法无需修改近期发展的二次标度玻色子PIMD算法。

Result: 在谐振子势阱和谐正弦势中的玻色子系统，以及谐振子势阱中的费米子期望值计算中，GSF在广泛温度范围内将收敛速度提升了约2-4倍，且仅需较低的计算开销。

Conclusion: GSF高阶因子分解方案可以直接应用于全同粒子的PIMD模拟，有效提升收敛性能，为多体量子系统的高效计算提供一条实用路径。

Abstract: Modern implementations of path integral molecular dynamics (PIMD) simulations of distinguishable particles frequently make use of high order factorization schemes for the Boltzmann operator to expedite convergence of equilibrium averages. Among these methods is the generalized Suzuki-Chin factorization (GSF), which is accurate up to fourth order in the imaginary-time step. In this work, we show that the GSF decomposition of the Boltzmann operator is applicable to bosonic PIMD, and results in an improved convergence of estimators. In particular, we show that the recently developed quadratic scaling bosonic PIMD need not change when using the GSF. The GSF scheme is implemented as a re-weighting factor for observables, without affecting the sampling generated by the standard, second-order, primitive factorization. We study the effect of this factorization for bosons in a harmonic trap and a sinusoidal potential. We also assess the effectiveness of GSF in calculating fermionic expectation values for harmonically-trapped atoms. In all these cases, we find that the GSF speeds up convergence with the Trotter number by a factor of $\sim 2-4$ across a wide temperature range, at only a modest computational cost.

### [104] [Testing $(q)$-Deformed Dunkl-Fokker-Planck Equation Algebra with Supersymmetry (SUSY) and Foldy-Wouthuysen (FW) Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13938)
*Abdelmalek Bouzenada*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在反射变形量子框架下，构建了(1+1)维(q)变形Dunkl-Fokker-Planck方程的相对论表述，建立了变形阶梯算符与超对称代数结构，并通过广义Foldy-Wouthuysen变换实现了正负能级相对论退耦，系统分析了变形参数与反射算符对谱性质的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先，在反射变形量子框架下构建(1+1)维(q)变形Dunkl-Fokker-Planck方程的相对论表述，引入(q)变形Dunkl算符与反射对称性。其次，通过构造变形阶梯算符与超对称代数关系，建立(q)-Wigner-Dunkl超对称构型。最后，引入广义Foldy-Wouthuysen（FW）变换实现正负能级相对论退耦，并分析高阶FW约化下的Dunkl-Fokker-Planck动力学。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个统一的代数与相对论描述框架，用于研究(q)变形Dunkl结构，并为一般反射对称量子模型中的超对称与相对论性质研究建立了自洽的理论基础。

Abstract: In this study, a relativistic formulation of the $(q)$-deformed Dunkl-Fokker-Planck equation in $(1+1)$-dimensions is constructed within the reflection-deformed quantum framework. In this case, the formalism includes $(q)$-deformed Dunkl operators and reflection symmetry to build a generalized dynamical structure for a relativistic quantum systems framework. Moreover, the corresponding $(q)$-Wigner-Dunkl supersymmetric configuration is established via the construction of deformed ladder operators and supersymmetric algebraic relations, yielding a consistent spectral representation of the model within the algebraic framework. The analysis extends to the harmonic oscillator with centrifugal interaction, where exact algebraic solutions, similarity reduction techniques, and closed energy spectra are obtained analytically in detail. The role of the deformation parameter and reflection operator on spectral properties and wavefunction structure is examined systematically in detail. A generalized Foldy-Wouthuysen (FW) transformation is introduced within the deformed Dunkl framework to achieve relativistic decoupling of positive- and negative-energy sectors within the present theoretical formulation. In this case, this approach yields an effective reduced Hamiltonian, including higher-order relativistic and deformation-induced terms. Also, the associated Dunkl-Fokker-Planck dynamics generated through high-order FW reduction are examined in detail for reflection-deformed relativistic quantum systems. In this context, results obtained here yield a unified algebraic and relativistic description of $(q)$-deformed Dunkl structures and construct a consistent framework for investigating supersymmetric and relativistic properties in reflection-symmetric quantum models in general.

### [105] [q-Askey Deformations of Double-Scaled SYK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13956)
*Sergio E. Aguilar-Gutierrez,Trivko Kukolj,Josef Seitz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构造了双标度SYK模型（double-scaled SYK, DSSYK）的形变族，研究其体（bulk）解释。通过引入微观形变，在系综平均和双标度极限下由q-Askey方案中基本正交多项式的传递矩阵（transfer matrix）描述。在半经典有限温度极限下，弦数（对应Krylov复杂度）等价于连接末端世界膜（End-Of-The-World brane）与反德西特（anti-de Sitter）渐近边界的爱因斯坦-罗森桥（Einstein-Rosen bridge）长度。增大形变参数后模型表现出离散能级，标志着正弦-膨胀引力（sine dilaton gravity）中的新几何转变。通过SYK-Schur对偶，Krylov复杂度还可解释为N=2 SU(2)规范理论指标中SU(2)自旋的扩散。变形理论的算子代数可为II₁型或I_∞型因子；II₁型代数间纯态的纠缠熵通过Ryu-Takayanagi公式展现为极值面。本文讨论了这些结果与体宇宙（baby universe）涌现之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索DSSYK模型形变族的体解释（bulk interpretation），揭示其与弦理论、引力对偶以及算子代数分类的关系。

Method: 引入SYK模型的微观形变，利用系综平均和双标度极限，通过q-Askey方案中基本正交多项式的传递矩阵来描述；借助SYK-Schur对偶与N=2 SU(2)规范理论建立联系；分析算子代数结构。

Result: 弦数（Krylov复杂度）在半经典有限温度下对应于爱因斯坦-罗森桥长度；形变参数增大导致离散能级，表明正弦-膨胀引力中出现新几何转变；Krylov复杂度通过SYK-Schur对偶具有SU(2)自旋扩散的代表论解释；算子代数可为II₁型或I_∞型因子；II₁型代数间的纠缠熵满足Ryu-Takayanagi公式；结果与体宇宙涌现相关。

Conclusion: DSSYK模型的形变族展现出丰富的体对偶结构，包括几何转变、算子代数分类与纠缠熵的引力解释，并可能与体宇宙（baby universe）的涌现机制密切相关。

Abstract: We construct families of deformations of the double-scaled SYK (DSSYK) model and investigate their bulk interpretation. We introduce microscopic deformations of the SYK model which, after ensemble averaging and in the double-scaling limit, are described by a transfer matrix encoding the recurrence relations of basic orthogonal polynomials in the q-Askey scheme. For certain families of deformations in the semiclassical limit at finite temperature, the chord number (encoding Krylov complexity) corresponds to the length of an Einstein-Rosen bridge connecting an End-Of-The-World brane to an anti-de Sitter asymptotic boundary. By increasing one of the deformation parameters, the models eventually exhibit discrete energy levels, signaling a new geometric transition in sine dilaton gravity. Via the SYK-Schur duality, Krylov complexity also admits a representation-theoretic interpretation as the spread of the SU(2) spin in the index of an $\mathcal{N}=2$ SU(2) gauge theory. We study the operator algebras of the deformed theories. The algebras can be type II$_1$ or type I$_\infty$ factors, depending on the operators that are included. The entanglement entropy between the type II$_1$ algebras for a pure state manifests as an extremal surface through the Ryu-Takayanagi formula. We discuss connections between our results and the emergence of baby universes in the bulk.

### [106] [A Twist on Scattering from Defect Anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13961)
*Andrea Antinucci,Christian Copetti,Giovanni Galati,Giovanni Rizi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出缺陷世界体积（worldvolume）上局域化的't Hooft反常作为驱动范畴散射的机制的普遍框架；通过无质量手征费米子模型验证该机制，并构造新的大质量可积理论（integrable theories）显式求解散射问题，最后构建晶格自旋链（lattice spin chains）以展现类似物理。

Result: 缺陷反常会在对称线（symmetry lines）与界面的连接处俘获非平凡荷（non-trivial charges），从而打开新的透射通道；在已有文献中的无质量手征费米子模型中，扭算符的出现可归结为缺陷反常的后果；新构造的大质量可积理论中类似现象被显式求解。

Conclusion: 缺陷反常是范畴散射的普遍驱动机制，该机制在无质量与大质量场论以及晶格模型中均适用，并提供了新的可积散射解。

Abstract: In the presence of extended defects, familiar incoming particles can scatter into exotic outgoing states created by twist operators. We show that one possible mechanism driving these "categorical scattering" processes is the presence of localized 't Hooft anomalies on the defect's worldvolume. Defect anomalies trap non-trivial charges at junctions between the symmetry lines and the interface, opening new transmission channels that would naively appear to violate selection rules. After outlining the general mechanism, we investigate several concrete examples with defects, interfaces, and boundaries. For models of massless chiral fermions already studied in the literature, we show that the emergence of twist operators can be understood as a consequence of defect anomalies. We then introduce new massive integrable theories in which a similar phenomenon occurs, and we explicitly solve the associated scattering problem, obtaining new integrable solutions. Finally, we construct lattice spin chains with defects where similar physics is expected to arise.

### [107] [A Tale of Two Hartle-Hawking Wave Functions: Fully Gravitational vs Partially Frozen](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13970)
*Galit Anikeeva,Raphaël Dulac,Zixia Wei,Mengyang Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了反德西特时空中的哈特尔-霍金波函数，提出了两种构造方式——完全引力波函数与部分冻结波函数。通过分析AdS₃爱因斯坦引力和AdS₂ Jackiw-Teitelboim引力的显式解，以及D维AdS爱因斯坦引力中双曲球配分函数的单圈修正，发现完全引力构造会引入非平凡单圈相位，而部分冻结构造保持实数正定。进一步对德西特时空（dS）的部分冻结球配分函数进行分析后，结果表明相位问题由引力路径积分是完全动力学的还是部分冻结的所控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在反德西特（AdS）时空中重新审视哈特尔-霍金（Hartle-Hawking）波函数，因为AdS时空具有开放的自然空间切片并需要额外的时空边界，这导致了两种不同的构造方式：完全引力波函数（边界构型被积分掉）和部分冻结波函数（边界构型固定，如AdS/CFT对应中的情况）。两种构造在处理引力路径积分时存在根本性差异，进而可能影响波函数的相位性质。

Method: 首先在AdS₃爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）和AdS₂ Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力中对完全引力构造进行显式分析。随后计算D维AdS爱因斯坦引力中双曲球（hyperbolic ball）配分函数的一圈修正（one-loop correction），该修正被认为是波函数模（wave-function norm）的主要贡献。进一步对比研究了德西特（dS）时空中部分冻结的球配分函数，其中赤道上的度规被固定。

Result: 完全引力构造的双曲球配分函数发展出非平凡的一圈相位 $(\mp i)^{D+1}$，与dS引力中的球配分函数类似。部分冻结的AdS双曲球配分函数则保持实数正定。部分冻结的dS球配分函数的一圈相位发生非平凡抵消。相位问题的产生与否由引力路径积分是完全动力学的还是部分冻结的所控制。

Conclusion: 相位问题（phase problem）的出现取决于引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）是否完全动力学化（fully dynamical）或部分冻结（partially frozen）。完全引力构造会引入非平凡相位，而部分冻结构造则保持相位实正定，揭示了这两种构造在量子引力波函数性质上的根本差异。

Abstract: We revisit the Hartle-Hawking wave function in AdS spacetime, where natural spatial slices are open and require an additional spacetime boundary. This leads to two constructions: a fully gravitational wave function, in which the boundary configuration is integrated over, and a partially frozen one, in which it is fixed, as in AdS/CFT. To illustrate the fully gravitational construction, we explicitly analyze it in AdS$_3$ Einstein gravity and AdS$_2$ Jackiw-Teitelboim gravity. We then evaluate the one-loop correction to the hyperbolic-ball partition function in $D$-dimensional AdS Einstein gravity, expected to give the leading contribution to the wave-function norm. We demonstrate that the fully gravitational hyperbolic ball partition function, where the boundary fluctuates, develops a nontrivial one-loop phase of $(\mp i)^{D+1}$, analogous to that of the sphere partition function in dS gravity. By contrast, the partially frozen partition function, where the boundary is fixed, remains real and positive. Motivated by this AdS comparison, we conversely investigate a partially frozen dS sphere partition function where the metric on an equator is fixed, finding that its one-loop phase cancels nontrivially. Our results suggest that the phase problem is controlled by whether the gravitational path integral is fully dynamical or partially frozen.

</details>


### [108] [Topological solitons of two-field scalar theories in rotationally symmetric backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14160)
*I. Andrade,M. A. Liao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究具有非平凡拓扑真空流形的标量场理论，在任意维旋转对称背景中发展了Bogomol'nyi框架，通过引入显式径向依赖势能克服高维标度不稳定性，得到了局域拓扑孤子解，并揭示了目标空间轨道在不同背景间的共享性以及向一维BPS理论的映射机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在任意维旋转对称背景下，标量场理论中具有拓扑非平凡真空流形（topologically nontrivial vacuum manifold）的局域拓扑解通常因高维中的标度不稳定性（scaling instability）而无法稳定存在。本文旨在通过引入显式径向依赖势能来克服这一限制，并建立统一的Bogomol'nyi分析框架。

Method: 考虑具有正则动能项（canonical kinetic terms）和广义动能项（generalized kinetic terms）的拉格朗日量（Lagrangian），发展针对对称约化理论的Bogomol'nyi框架。导出的一阶方程给出可积轨道方程，并通过由函数ξ(r)编码的变换将一阶方程映射为一维BPS理论（BPS theory）。

Result: 得到了局域拓扑解（localized topological solutions），并证明其稳定性由势能中的显式径向依赖实现。发现目标空间轨道（target space orbits）——而非解本身——在不同背景的类似系统间共享。一阶方程可通过ξ(r)映射到一维BPS理论，缺陷的 internal structure、大小和存在性取决于该映射的性质与范围。在Minkowski、Schwarzschild、de Sitter、Schwarzschild de Sitter以及共形平坦背景（conformally flat backgrounds）中给出了精确解（exact solutions）。

Conclusion: 该框架系统地评估了几何对孤子（solitons）的约束（confinement）、存在性和结构的影响。显式径向依赖势能是维持高维拓扑解稳定性的关键机制，而不同背景间的轨道共享性揭示了几何与场构型之间的深层关联。

Abstract: This work concerns scalar field theories with topologically nontrivial vacuum manifold in rotationally symmetric backgrounds of arbitrary dimension. Lagrangians with canonical and generalized kinetic terms are considered, and a Bogomol'nyi framework is developed for the symmetric restriction of the theory. Localized topological solutions are found. Their stability, which would normally be prevented in higher dimensions due to scaling instability, is made possible by the presence of an explicit radial dependence on the potential. The first-order equations give rise to an integrable orbit equation which can be used to solve the problem completely. It is shown that target space orbits - but not the solutions themselves - are shared between analogous systems defined in different backgrounds. Moreover, the first-order equations can be mapped into a one-dimensional BPS theory through a transformation encoded by a function $ξ(r)$. The internal structure, size and existence of defects follows from the properties and range of this mapping. We use these tools to evaluate the effect of geometry on confinement, existence, and structure of solitons. Exact solutions are provided in Minkowski, Schwarzschild, de Sitter, Schwarzschild de Sitter and conformally flat backgrounds.

</details>


### [109] [Constitutive Origin of Hamiltonian Degeneracy in Nonlinear Electrodynamics with Spontaneous Lorentz Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14172)
*C. A. Escobar,Román Linares*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在Plebański非线性电动力学中，自发洛伦兹对称破缺下磁真空的驻点条件等价于二阶约束泊松括号矩阵行列式为零的结构性根源：该等价性源于本构关系（constitutive relations）的生成机制，驻点对应互补能量（complementary energy）的极值，且线性化本构映射在该点失去秩（loss of rank）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的研究发现，在Plebański非线性电动力学中，磁背景（magnetic backgrounds）的驻点条件与二阶约束（second-class constraints）的泊松括号矩阵行列式为零相重合，但这一重合的结构性起源尚不明确。本文旨在阐明这一等价关系的深层理论根源。

Method: 作者从理论的本构起源（constitutive origin）出发，分析了结构势（structural potential）V(P,Q)如何生成电磁本构关系（electromagnetic constitutive relations），并考察了固定Dvec下磁真空的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）与互补能量（complementary energy）之间的对应关系。通过将一阶本构关系（first-order constitutive relation）纳入Dirac约束结构（Dirac constraint structure），揭示了磁本构雅可比矩阵（magnetic constitutive Jacobian）作为二阶约束泊松括号矩阵的局部子块出现。

Result: 证明了每一个非平凡磁驻点都位于线性化映射δHvec↦δBvec（固定Dvec下）失去秩（loss of rank）的曲面（surface）上。基于这一互补能量结构，作者给出了真空约化线性化理论，讨论了真空约化理论中径向模（radial mode）的移除，并澄清了在单不变量模型（single-invariant models）中电分支和混合驻点分支被阻遏的原因。

Conclusion: 本构关系的生成机制是解释驻点条件与约束矩阵奇异性之间等价关系的根本原因，该互补能量结构为理解Plebański非线性电动力学中自发洛伦兹对称破缺（spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking）的真空选择提供了统一框架。

Abstract: In Plebański nonlinear electrodynamics with spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking, nontrivial magnetic backgrounds are selected by stationary points of an effective Hamiltonian. Previous branchwise Hamiltonian analyses showed that this same stationarity requirement coincides with the vanishing of the determinant of the Poisson-bracket matrix among the second-class constraints, but the structural origin of this coincidence was not manifest. We show that it follows from the constitutive origin of the theory. The structural potential \(V(P,Q)\) generates the electromagnetic constitutive relations, while the effective Hamiltonian for magnetic vacua is the complementary energy associated with the magnetic response at fixed \(\Dvec\). Moreover, because the first-order constitutive relation enters the Dirac constraint structure, the magnetic constitutive Jacobian appears as a local block of the Poisson-bracket matrix among the second-class constraints. This complementary-energy structure implies that every nontrivial magnetic stationary point lies on a surface where the linearized map \(δ\Hvec\mapstoδ\Bvec\), at fixed \(\Dvec\), loses rank. We use this interpretation to formulate the reduced linearized theory at the vacuum, discuss the removal of the radial mode in the vacuum-restricted theory, and clarify why electric and mixed stationary branches are obstructed in single-invariant models.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文将全息林德布拉德（holographic Lindblad）方案推广至非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）情境，并将其应用于耦合标量场的JT引力。在半经典与高温区间的数值模拟中，展示了黑洞的动力学形成过程。

Conclusion: 非马尔可夫全息林德布拉德框架可以描述黑洞动力学形成过程，进一步支持了全息对偶中体视界形成与边界热化之间的对应关系。

Abstract: Black-hole formation is expected, via holography, to correspond to thermalization in the boundary theory. In this paper, we extend the holographic Lindblad prescription to a non-Markovian setting and apply it to JT gravity coupled to a scalar field. ### [111] [Scattering off Chamblin-Reall Branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14580)
*Dongsheng Ge,Christopher P. Herzog*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究三维时空中胶子-引力子（dilaton-graviton）波在薄膜（thin brane）上的线性化散射。全息对偶（holographic dual）对应于强耦合理论中界面散射。结果表明：对于d>1，存在反射、透射和倏逝（evanescent）分量；d=2时界面行为类似粗糙半透窗，产生漫散射和表面模吸收；d=4时散射过程对红外边界条件敏感，需正则化奇异零温几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过三维时空薄膜上的胶子-引力子波散射，研究全息对偶框架下强耦合理论中的界面散射问题，特别是不同于纯AdS₃情形的新物理效应。

Method: 采用线性化散射方法，分析三维时空中薄膜对胶子-引力子波的散射，并利用全息对偶（holographic duality）将问题映射为高维AdS₊₂引力约化后的一族强耦合理论中的界面散射。对d=2和d=4两种情形分别求解。

Result: 对于d>1，物理体模（physical bulk mode）允许入射辐射被重新分布为反射、透射和倏逝分量。d=2时界面表现为粗糙半透窗，产生漫散射并吸收进入表面模；该散射过程在全息对偶视角下暗示耗散性流向红外（infrared）。d=4时散射对红外边界条件敏感，零温奇异几何需正则化，但方程结构表明正则化后可能呈现与d=2类似的定性行为。

Abstract: We study the linearized scattering of dilaton-graviton waves from a thin brane in three-dimensional spacetime. Holographically, the setup models scattering from an interface in a family of strongly coupled theories related to dimensional reductions of higher-dimensional $AdS_{d+2}$ gravity. Unlike the pure $AdS_3$ case, for $d>1$ the physical bulk mode allows incident radiation to be redistributed into reflected, transmitted, and evanescent components. For the $d=2$ background, we obtain a controlled solution in which the interface acts like a rough translucent window, producing diffuse angular scattering and absorption into surface modes. From the dual perspective, the scattering process is suggestive of dissipative flow toward the infrared. For $d=4$, the same analysis reveals a sensitivity to the infrared boundary condition, suggesting that the singular zero-temperature geometry must be regulated in order to have a well-defined scattering process. The structure of the equations nevertheless suggests that a regulated $d=4$ problem may exhibit the same qualitative redistribution of incident flux.

### [112] [$α'$ corrections to self-dual gravitational instantons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14668)
*José Luis V. Cerdeira,Cristóbal Corral,Tomás Ortín*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究四维Cano–Ruipérez作用量中自对偶引力瞬子（self-dual gravitational instanton）的α'修正，发现自对偶曲率空间的度规不受修正，但原本平凡的膨胀子（dilaton）和轴子（axion）场由于与Gauss–Bonnet和Pontrjagin密度的耦合而获得修正。文章给出了Gibbons–Hawking多瞬子解的修正通用形式，以及Euclidean Taub–NUT和Eguchi–Hanson空间的具体修正；构造了适定的Dirichlet变分原理所需的边界项，并证明Eguchi–Hanson瞬子的总作用量在一阶α'下不受修正。此外，文章还构造了在未修正的自对偶引力瞬子背景上具有非平凡膨胀子与轴子的弦论D-瞬子（D-instanton）类欧几里得解，并给出了其α'修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦论有效作用量中的α'修正对于理解引力瞬子（gravitational instanton）的非微扰效应至关重要。本文旨在研究Cano–Ruipérez作用量框架下自对偶引力瞬子如何受到α'修正，特别是膨胀子与轴子的行为，并建立适定的边界项以正确计算作用量。

Method: 从Bergshoeff–de Roo杂化弦有效作用量在T⁶上的紧致化出发，经截断和场重定义得到四维Cano–Ruipérez作用量；通过分析自对偶曲率空间中膨胀子和轴子与Gauss–Bonnet及Pontrjagin密度的耦合，求解其修正形式；构造包含这两个拓扑项贡献的边界项，并针对渐近局部欧几里得（asymptotically-locally-Euclidean）解进行归一化。

Result: 自对偶曲率空间的度规在α'下不受修正；膨胀子和轴子获得修正，并给出了Gibbons–Hawking多瞬子解的通用形式以及Euclidean Taub–NUT和Eguchi–Hanson空间的具体表达式。构建的边界项使得Dirichlet变分原理适定；Eguchi–Hanson瞬子的总欧几里得作用量在一阶α'下无修正。此外，在未修正的自对偶引力瞬子背景上构造了具有非平凡膨胀子和轴子的D-瞬子类解，并给出了其α'修正。

Conclusion: 在Cano–Ruipérez理论中，自对偶引力瞬子的度规保持经典形式不变，但膨胀子和轴子通过拓扑耦合获得α'修正；适当定义的边界项保证了变分问题的良定性，且一阶α'修正不影响总作用量。这些结果有助于理解弦论框架下引力瞬子的非微扰性质。

Abstract: We study the $α'$ corrections to self-dual gravitational instantons in the context of the four-dimensional Cano--Ruipérez action, which can be obtained by the compactification of the Bergshoeff--de Roo heterotic string effective action on $\mathbb{T}^{6}$ followed by a truncation and a field redefinition. We show that the metric of spaces of self-dual curvature does not receive any corrections, but their (initially trivial) dilaton and axion fields do, owing to their couplings to Gauss--Bonnet and Pontrjagin densities. We find the generic form of the corrections of the dilaton and axion fields for the Gibbons--Hawking multi-instanton solutions and their explicit form for the particular cases of the Euclidean Taub--NUT and Eguchi--Hanson spaces. We construct the boundary terms required to define a well-posed Dirichlet variational principle in the Euclidean Cano--Ruipérez theory, including the contributions associated with the Gauss--Bonnet and Pontrjagin terms. The boundary terms are normalized for asymptotically-locally-Euclidean solutions, and we evaluate with them the Euclidean action of the $α'$-corrected Eguchi--Hanson instanton showing that the total action receives no corrections to first order in $α'$. We also show that, at zeroth order in $α'$, one can construct Euclidean solutions similar to the string theory D-instanton with non-trivial dilaton and axion on the background of a self-dual purely gravitational instanton which remains unmodified. We also compute the $α'$ corrections to these solutions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析，将非紧致轴子宇宙学的三个一致性条件作为判据，检验膨胀子（dilaton）作为近似尺度不变性自发破缺的赝南布-戈德斯通玻色子是否能够同时满足这些条件。

Abstract: A consistent non-compact axion cosmology requires a non-periodic field, an effective field theory valid sufficiently above the inflationary scale, and a small non-QCD contribution to the potential that tilts the axionic vacuum landscape in order to trigger a timely domain-wall collapse. All conditions can be met by the dilaton -- the pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson of spontaneously broken approximate scale invariance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

The theory arises by gauging an $\mathrm{SO}(2)\cong\mathrm{U}(1)$ subgroup of the flavour symmetry of $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ SQCD with $n+1$ flavours.

We demonstrate that, for these configurations, the thermodynamic Smarr formula is structurally identical to the single-copy Gauss's law. Extending this to asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetimes, we prove that the thermodynamic pressure-volume term ($PV$) naturally emerges from a gauge-theoretic background subtraction. This relationship establishes a novel connection between the classical double copy and black hole thermodynamics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AMPS防火墙论证基于早期辐射、晚期出射霍金模与内部伙伴模近似独立这一假设，但在微分同胚不变量子引力（diffeomorphism-invariant quantum gravity）中，引力着装（gravitational dressing）与渐近约束阻碍了物理可观测量（physical observables）的张量积分解，因此需要重新审视该假设的有效性。

Method: 采用算子代数框架直接表述子系统独立性；运用模理论（modular theory）、沿零方向的半侧模包含（half-sided modular inclusion）以及未来零无穷远处着装辐射代数的扇区-wise 极大性（sector-wise maximality）进行论证。

Result: 在固定渐近荷扇区（fixed asymptotic charge sector）内，内部霍金伙伴模式对应的代数不能构成独立的交换子代数（commuting subalgebra），而必须被包含为辐射代数自身的一个（非交换的）子代数（non-commuting subalgebra）。因此，AMPS论证中的子系统独立性假设失效，纠缠单配性（entanglement monogamy）步骤不再适用。

Conclusion: 在渐近平坦量子引力中，unitary 黑洞蒸发与半经典视界光滑性可以共存，无需借助纠缠岛（entanglement islands）、复制虫洞（replica wormholes）或对半经典视界物理的修改。

Abstract: The AMPS firewall argument relies on treating early radiation, late outgoing Hawking modes, and interior partner modes as approximately independent quantum subsystems. In diffeomorphism-invariant quantum gravity, however, gravitational dressing and asymptotic constraints obstruct such a tensor-product factorization of physical observables. In this essay, we sharpen this obstruction by formulating subsystem independence directly in operator-algebraic terms. Using modular theory, half-sided modular inclusions along null directions, and the sector-wise maximality of the dressed radiation algebra at future null infinity, we show that -- within a fixed asymptotic charge sector -- the algebra associated with the interior Hawking partner cannot form an independent commuting subalgebra, but must be contained as a (non-commuting) subalgebra of the radiation algebra itself. The subsystem-independence assumption underlying the AMPS paradox therefore fails, and the entanglement-monogamy step never becomes applicable. As a result, unitary black hole evaporation and semiclassical horizon smoothness are compatible in asymptotically flat quantum gravity, without invoking entanglement islands, replica wormholes, or modifications of semiclassical horizon physics.

</details>


### [118] [From AdS Propagators to Celestial Propagators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15025)
*Pongwit Srisangyingcharoen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究AdS标量传播子在 celestial 基（celestial basis）中的表示，将标准体-边界传播子（bulk-to-boundary propagator）通过 Schwinger 参数化转换为边界-边界传播子（boundary-to-boundary propagator），并利用共形本征波函数（conformal primary wavefunctions）将其变换到 celestial 基。无质量情形下，celestial 传播子简化为天球上有效的二维边界-边界对象；有质量情形下，则展现出包含修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel functions）的非平凡核结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 AdS 标量传播子在 celestial 基中的表示形式，旨在建立 AdS 体传播子与 celestial 传播子之间的结构对应关系，从而深化对 AdS/CFT 对偶中全息映射的理解。

Method: 从欧几里得 AdS 空间中的标准体-边界传播子出发，采用 Schwinger 参数化（Schwinger parametrization）表达传播子，并构造相应的边界-边界传播子；随后利用无质量和有质量标量场的共形本征波函数（conformal primary wavefunctions）将所得传播子变换到 celestial 基。

Result: 无质量情形下，celestial 传播子简化为天球上依赖于 AdS/CFT 共形维度 Δ（conformal dimension）的二维边界-边界对象；有质量情形下，celestial 传播子展现出包含修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel functions）的非平凡核结构，该结构与 AdS 体-边界传播子在动量空间中的径向结构高度相似。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，AdS 传播子与 celestial 传播子之间存在结构上的翻译对应关系，为全息对偶中的 celestial 基表述提供了新的见解。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate how AdS scalar propagators are represented in the celestial basis. Starting from the standard bulk-to-boundary propagator in Euclidean AdS space, we express the propagator in a Schwinger parametrization and construct the corresponding boundary-to-boundary propagator. We then transform the resulting propagators to the celestial basis using conformal primary wavefunctions for both massless and massive scalar fields. For the massless case, the celestial propagator reduces to an effectively two-dimensional boundary-to-boundary object on the celestial sphere dependent on the AdS/CFT conformal dimension $Δ$. For the massive case, the celestial propagator exhibits a nontrivial kernel involving modified Bessel functions, closely resembling the momentum-space radial structure of AdS bulk-to-boundary propagators. The results suggest a structural translation from AdS propagators and celestial propagators.

</details>


### [119] [Wormholes and Averaging over N](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15180)
*Jonah Kudler-Flam,Edward Witten*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出“梅林平均”（Mellin averaging）方法，通过对整数参数 N 进行解析延拓（analytic continuation）并定义渐近平均，来理解引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）中虫洞（wormholes）所表现的系综平均（ensemble average）行为，并以谱形因子（spectral form factor）和随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）为例进行验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力路径积分在可观测量的计算中产生 G_N 的渐近展开，但对于预期剧烈涨落的可观测量，这一事实令人困惑。虫洞看似计算了这些可观测量的系综平均，但在典型的 AdS/CFT 对偶构造中，除了个别例子中的单个整数 N，并无参数可供平均。

Method: 引入“梅林平均”程序，定义函数在 N 上的渐近平均（asymptotic average）；论证若对偶理论允许在 N 上解析延拓且相关可观测量在超多项式小尺度上涨落，则梅林平均足以再现虫洞物理中的表观随机性（apparent randomness）。以双锥（double cone）主导引力路径积分区域的谱形因子为检验案例，与将 N 视为连续变量的随机矩阵理论进行比较；并构建了 N 上解析延拓的量子比特模型（qubit model）和确定性函数模型。

Result: 梅林平均能够从确定性函数中提取出与虫洞计算一致的随机统计行为；在谱形因子的测试案例中，该方法与随机矩阵理论的预测相匹配；所构造的量子比特模型和确定性高斯模拟函数展示了 N 上解析延拓的可操作性。

Conclusion: 梅林平均提供了一种在 AdS/CFT 对偶框架中无需引入额外参数即可解释虫洞系综平均现象的新机制，前提是边界理论允许 N 的解析延拓且可观测量在 N 上具有超多项式小尺度的涨落。

Abstract: The gravitational path integral produces an asymptotic expansion in $G_N$, a fact which is puzzling in the case of observables that are expected to fluctuate wildly. Wormholes appear to compute ensemble averages of functions of such observables, though in typical constructions of AdS/CFT, there are no parameters to average over except, in some examples, a single integer $N$. We introduce a procedure that we call ``Mellin averaging'' to define a sort of asymptotic average of a function of $N$. We argue that Mellin averaging over $N$ may suffice to reproduce the apparent randomness seen in wormhole physics, provided that the dual theory admits an analytic continuation in $N$ and the relevant observables fluctuate on superpolynomially small scales in $N$. As a test case, we consider the spectral form factor in the regime where the double cone is believed to dominate the gravitational path integral and compare to a random matrix theory in which $N$ behaves as a continuous variable. We also describe some toy models of analytic continuation in $N$: a qubit model that can be analytically continued in $N$, and an explicit construction of a deterministic function of $N$ that simulates a sequence of independent draws from a Gaussian ensemble.

</details>

Method: 本研究采用理论分析与实际考量相结合的方法，从科学案例（scientific case）和实际部署（practical considerations）两个维度，系统评估在南极部署长基线原子干涉仪（long-baseline atom interferometer）的可行性。

Result: 南极的低地震噪声、现有基础设施及对引力波源全球定位能力的提升，使其成为部署原子干涉仪的优越候选地。该探测器有望扩展全球引力波探测网络（global network of gravitational wave detectors），并支持基础物理的精确测试（precision tests of fundamental physics）。

Conclusion: 南极部署长基线原子干涉仪在科学上和工程上均具有可行性，能够填补分赫兹频段的引力波探测空白，同时增强全球探测网络的空间分辨率，并为检验基础物理提供新平台。

Abstract: Atom interferometers represent a promising approach for gravitational wave detection in the decihertz frequency band, complementary to existing light-based detectors. The South Pole offers unique advantages for such experiments: exceptionally low seismic noise, established infrastructure for large scientific projects, and a location that strengthens gravitational wave source localization through global triangulation. Here we discuss the scientific case and practical considerations for deploying a long-baseline atom interferometer at the South Pole, which has the potential to expand the global network of gravitational wave detectors while enabling precision tests of fundamental physics.

### [122] [Diquark Correlators and Phase Structure in the Quark-Meson-Diquark Model beyond Mean Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13934)
*Mire Ugo,Schaefer Bernd-Jochen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 介子涨落的引入显著改变了模型的相结构；在足够强的双夸克耦合下，系统动力学由双夸克凝聚（diquark condensation）主导。

Conclusion: 双夸克极点质量（diquark pole mass）和银焰性质的分析揭示了介子涨落和双夸克耦合强度对相结构的关键影响，表明超出平均场近似的涨落效应不可忽略。

Abstract: A comprehensive study of the phase structure of the two-flavor quark-meson-diquark model is presented within the nonperturbative functional renormalization group framework. The influence of mesonic fluctuations beyond the mean-field approximation is investigated, and two-point functions of the diquark fields are computed at finite real-time frequencies. Renormalization group consistency of the effective potential is ensured in order to avoid cutoff artifacts. Substantial modifications of the phase structure are found once mesonic fluctuations are included, and for sufficiently strong diquark couplings the dynamics become dominated by diquark condensation. These effects are elucidated through an analysis of the diquark pole mass and the Silver-Blaze property.

### [123] [Approximate mass spectra of the heavy mesons under a Coulomb plus logarithmic spin-dependent potential function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14094)
*E. Omugbe,E. P Inyang,K. Adegoke,E. M. Khokha*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于微扰论（perturbation theory）近似解析求解库仑加对数势（Coulomb plus logarithmic potential），用于计算底偶素（bottomonium）和粲偶素（charmonium）介子低阶量子态的质量谱，通过与实验数据拟合确定势参数，所得结果与实验值吻合良好，绝对百分比平均偏差（APAD）分别为0.24%和1.65%，优于或可比于已有理论计算结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子色动力学（Quantum chromodynamics, QCD）中强相互作用的两个核心特征——短程渐进自由（asymptotic freedom）和长程夸克禁闭（quark confinement）——需要选择合适的唯象势模型来描述重夸克偶素（quarkonia）系统。本文旨在通过库仑加对数势结合微扰论，提供一种解析近似处理方法，以准确计算底偶素和粲偶素的质量谱。

Method: 采用微扰论对库仑加对数势（Coulomb plus logarithmic potential）进行近似解析处理，推导出一阶修正的能级方程；通过拟合粒子数据组（Particle Data Group）的实验数据来标定自由势参数；并采用矩阵Numerov方法（matrix Numerov method）获得精确数值解，以验证解析近似的可靠性。

Result: 底偶素质量的计算结果与实验值高度吻合，绝对百分比平均偏差（absolute percentage average deviation, APAD）为0.24%，优于若干已有理论结果；矢量（vector）和赝标量（pseudoscalar）粲偶素质量的APAD为1.65%，与现有竞争性理论计算相比表现出改进或相当的精度。与矩阵Numerov方法所得精确数值解的比较也验证了该近似的可靠性。

Conclusion: 所提出的唯象势模型及微扰近似方法在描述夸克偶素（quarkonia）系统方面是有效的，小的百分比误差证实了其可靠性；该方法有望被可靠地推广应用于更高激发态的研究。

Abstract: In this paper, we presented an approximate analytical treatment of the Coulomb plus logarithmic potential using perturbation theory to investigate the mass spectra of bottomonium and charmonium mesons for the low-order quantum states. The derived energy equation, to first-order corrections, was employed to model the free potential parameters through fitting to experimental data of the Particle Data Group. The proposed potential successfully reproduces asymptotic freedom at short distances through one-gluon exchange interactions and quark confinement at large distances, which are the essential features of the strong interactions in Quantum chromodynamics theory. The calculated bottomonium masses exhibited excellent agreement with experimental values, yielding an absolute percentage average deviation (APAD) of 0.24%, which improves upon several previously reported theoretical results. Similarly, the vector and pseudoscalar charmonium masses were obtained with an APAD of 1.65%, demonstrating improved and comparable accuracy relative to existing competing theoretical calculations. Although our results were limited to first-order corrections to the energy spectra within the perturbation theory, the reliability of the approximation was validated by comparison with exact numerical solutions obtained using the matrix Numerov method. The small percentage errors obtained confirm the effectiveness of the phenomenological potential and perturbation approximation in describing quarkonia systems. The results suggest that the approach can be reliably extended to higher excited states.

### [124] [Complete one-loop self-energies of the linear sigma model coupled to quarks at finite temperature and in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14372)
*Adolfo Flores-Aguilar,Luis A. Hernández,J. Carlos Márquez,R. Zamora*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文系统计算了有限温度与均匀磁场下线性σ模型（linear sigma model）与夸克耦合时所有场的一圈自能（one-loop self-energies），采用Matsubara形式论（Matsubara formalism）处理温度效应、Schwinger固有时表示（Schwinger proper-time representation）处理带电传播子，并借助Ritus形式论（Ritus formalism）处理非对易的Schwinger相位（Schwinger phases），最终建立了热磁（thermomagnetic）一圈修正的完整计算框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有有效模型（effective models of QCD）在有限温度和磁场下的圈图计算中，中性场与带电场的处理方式不一致，且带电粒子在磁场中的Schwinger相位问题尚未被系统解决，亟需一个适用于任意温度和磁场强度的统一计算框架。

Method: 利用Matsubara形式论引入有限温度效应，采用Schwinger固有时表示构建磁场中的带电传播子（charged propagators），并通过Ritus形式论在坐标空间中系统评估涉及不同电荷粒子的圈图中无法抵消的Schwinger相位，再将结果一致地表达于动量空间（momentum space）。

Result: 得到了所有场（中性场与带电场）的一圈自能解析表达式，清晰呈现了热涨落（thermal fluctuations）与磁场效应之间的非平凡耦合，实现了真空贡献（vacuum contributions）与物质贡献（matter contributions）的明确分离，并给出了紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences）的规范识别结构。

Conclusion: 所建立的框架能够统一且系统地计算QCD有效模型中所有动力学自由度（dynamic degrees of freedom）的热磁一圈修正，为后续研究有限温度和磁场下的量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）相变及手征对称性恢复（chiral symmetry restoration）等现象提供了可靠的理论工具。

Abstract: We present a complete calculation of the one-loop self-energies for all fields in the linear sigma model coupled to quarks at finite temperature and in the presence of a uniform magnetic field. The analysis consistently incorporates thermal and magnetic effects for both neutral and charged degrees of freedom, providing a unified framework valid for arbitrary values of the temperature and the field strength. The computation is performed using the Matsubara formalism to account for finite temperature effects and the Schwinger proper-time representation for charged propagators in a magnetic background. Special attention is given to loop contributions involving particles with different electric charges, for which the associated Schwinger phases do not cancel. We show that these terms can be systematically evaluated in coordinate space using the Ritus formalism, which provides the appropriate framework for treating external charged states in the presence of a magnetic background, and consistently expressed in momentum space. The resulting expressions exhibit a nontrivial interplay between thermal fluctuations and magnetic effects and allow for a clear separation between vacuum and matter contributions, providing a well-defined structure for the identification of ultraviolet divergences. Our results establish a consistent and systematic framework for the computation of thermomagnetic one-loop corrections in effective models of QCD, capturing the full interplay between thermal and magnetic effects for all dynamical degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [125] [Scattering and depletion in a flying focus from conformal transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14751)
*Tim Adamo,Anton Ilderton,Adam Noble*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 通过复共形变换（complex conformal transformation）将平面波转化为飞行聚焦（flying focus）场，进而将强场量子电动力学（strong-field QED）中的光子发射振幅直接简化为对平面波振幅的简单高斯平均，从而“免费”引入聚焦效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强场量子电动力学（strong-field QED）中，理论计算通常依赖平面波近似，但实际实验中的激光场具有聚焦结构。该研究旨在建立一种方法，能在不增加计算复杂度的前提下，将聚焦效应纳入强场QED散射振幅的计算中。

Method: 利用复共形变换（complex conformal transformation）将平面波变换为飞行聚焦（flying focus）场；相应地，无质量波动方程（massless wave equation）的解由Volkov解（Volkov solutions）经共形变换得到。光子发射振幅的计算转化为对原平面波振幅中某些动量变量进行简单高斯平均（Gaussian average）。

Result: 在完全耗尽（totally depleting）的飞行聚焦光束中，光子发射振幅可直接从对应的平面波振幅通过动量变量的高斯平均得到。在反自对偶极限（anti-self-dual limit）下，部分耗尽（partial depletion）情形的一阶结果也已给出。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种将聚焦效应引入强场QED计算的“免费”途径，并讨论了向部分耗尽散射振幅的扩展及其在反自对偶极限下的初步结果。

Abstract: We show that flying focus fields can be obtained from complex conformal transformation of plane waves, and that solutions of the massless wave equation in the so-obtained fields are, correspondingly, conformal transformations of the Volkov solutions. This leads to the result that photon emission amplitudes in a totally depleting flying focus beam may be computed directly from the corresponding plane wave amplitudes by taking a simple Gaussian average over certain momentum variables. In effect, this gives a way of introducing focussing effects into strong-field QED calculations `for free'. The extension of these results to scattering amplitudes including only partial depletion is discussed and some first results presented in the anti-self-dual limit.

</details>


<div id='hep-ex'></div>
