### [126] [Constraints on anomalous Higgs boson couplings to vector bosons and fermions using the $γγ$ final state in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14245)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于CMS实验138 fb⁻¹的质子对撞数据，通过分析双光子衰变道的希格斯玻色子候选事件，研究其与矢量玻色子和费米子的异常耦合，结果表明所有测量与标准模型预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model, SM）对希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）的耦合性质有精确预言，任何偏离标准模型的异常耦合（anomalous couplings）都预示着可能存在超出标准模型的新物理。本研究旨在利用大型强子对撞机（LHC）CMS实验的高统计量数据，对希格斯玻色子与矢量玻色子（vector bosons）及费米子（fermions）的耦合结构进行精确检验。

Method: 使用CMS实验在质心能量$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV下采集的质子-质子对撞数据，总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为138 fb⁻¹。选取希格斯玻色子衰变至双光子（diphoton）的候选事件，根据胶子融合（gluon fusion）、电弱矢量玻色子融合（electroweak vector boson fusion）和伴随矢量玻色子产生（associated production）三种产生机制进行事件分类，采用矩阵元技术（matrix element techniques）和多变量判别器（multivariate discriminants）进行区分。在此基础上研究希格斯玻色子与胶子（通过重粒子圈）耦合的$CP$性质，以及其与两个电弱玻色子相互作用的张量结构（tensor structure）。

Result: 将测量结果以各产生过程中异常希格斯玻色子耦合对总产生截面的分数贡献（fractional contributions）形式进行诠释。所有观测结果与标准模型预期一致。

Conclusion: 在现有统计精度下，未发现希格斯玻色子耦合偏离标准模型预言的证据，标准模型对希格斯玻色子耦合性质的描述仍然成立。

Abstract: Possible anomalous couplings of the Higgs boson to vector bosons and fermions are studied using Higgs boson candidates decaying to a pair of photons. The study is based on proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV collected by the CMS experiment, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Events with Higgs boson candidates produced via gluon fusion, electroweak vector boson fusion and in association with a vector boson, are categorized using matrix element techniques and multivariate discriminants. The $CP$ properties of the Higgs boson couplings to gluons through loops of heavy particles, as well as the tensor structure of its interactions with two electroweak bosons, are investigated. The results are interpreted in terms of the fractional contributions of anomalous Higgs boson couplings to the total production cross section of each process and are found to be consistent with the standard model expectations.

</details>


### [127] [Search for new physics in triple boson production in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV using the effective field theory approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15023)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了在三重规范玻色子（VVV，V = W或Z玻色子）产生过程中寻找新物理的搜索。在Lorentz boosted区域（所有三个玻色子的横动量p_T > 200 GeV）进行事件选择，利用V-tagged jets重建技术对信号进行识别，最终未观测到超出标准模型（SM）预期的显著超额，并在SM有效场论（SMEFT）框架下对一组质量维度-6和-8算符的Wilson系数设置了置信水平为95%的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三重规范玻色子产生过程是探测标准模型（Standard Model, SM）精确预测之外新物理的敏感探针，尤其是在Lorentz boosted区域，标准模型本底事件极少，有利于提高对新物理信号的灵敏度。

Method: 采用针对Lorentz boosted区域的事件选择方案，要求三个玻色子的横动量（transverse momentum, $p_\mathrm{T}$）均高于200 GeV。利用大半径喷注（large-radius jet）的亚结构（substructure）识别由强子衰变W/Z玻色子产生的V-tagged jets。根据带电轻子和V-tagged jets的数量及运动学特征对事件进行分类，并在标量横动量之和（scalar $p_\mathrm{T}$ sum）等运动学变元的分箱中获取事件产额。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型预期的显著信号超额。在SM有效场论（SM effective field theory, SMEFT）框架下，对质量维度-6和-8算符的Wilson系数设置了95%置信水平（CL）的上限。其中两个最严格的限制为：$-$0.13 $\lt$ $c_\mathrm{W}/Λ^2$ $\lt$ 0.12 TeV$^{-2}$ 和 $-$0.24 $\lt$ $c_\mathrm{Hq3}/Λ^2$ $\lt$ 0.21 TeV$^{-2}$（$c_\mathrm{W}$和$c_\mathrm{Hq3}$为Warsaw基下的维度-6 Wilson系数，$Λ$为新物理的质量标度）。

Conclusion: 三重规范玻色子产生过程在Lorentz boosted区域的数据与标准模型预期一致，未发现新物理证据。基于SMEFT的约束为未来高能对撞机上的新物理搜索提供了重要的参数限制基准。

Abstract: A search for new physics in the production of three massive gauge bosons (VVV, where V is a W or Z boson) is presented. The event selection is most effective in the Lorentz-boosted regime in which all three bosons have a transverse momentum ($p_\mathrm{T}$) above 200 GeV. Standard model (SM) processes contribute few events in this regime. When a boosted W or Z boson decays hadronically, the decay products tend to form a large-radius jet with substructure that reflects the presence of two quarks from the decay; such jets are called V-tagged jets. Special techniques to reconstruct and select V-tagged jets are applied. Events are categorized according to the number and kinematic features of charged leptons and V-tagged jets. Event yields are obtained in bins of a suitable kinematic variable such as the scalar $p_\mathrm{T}$ sum of the reconstructed objects in the event. No excess over SM expectations is observed. Bounds are placed on Wilson coefficients for a set of mass dimension-6 and -8 operators in the framework of SM effective field theory. The two most stringent bounds placed by this analysis are $-$0.13 $\lt$ $c_\mathrm{W}/Λ^2$ $\lt$ 0.12 TeV$^{-2}$ and $-$0.24 $\lt$ $c_\mathrm{Hq3}/Λ^2$ $\lt$ 0.21 TeV$^{-2}$ at 95% CL, where $c_\mathrm{W}$ and $c_\mathrm{Hq3}$ are dimension-6 Wilson coefficients in the Warsaw basis and $Λ$ is the mass scale of new physics.

</details>

### [128] [Time Crystals in Coupled Exciton-Polariton Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14250)
*Xuan Ye,Hong-Jin Xiong,Alexey Kavokin,Sanjib Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文证明，在耦合激子-极化激元凝聚体（exciton-polariton condensates）中，无需周期性外部驱动即可通过非相干增益和耗散通道涌现出时间晶体（time crystals）。通过平均场相图、数值分岔分析和Bogoliubov微扰理论，确定了时间晶体存在的参数条件及其量子鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在不依赖周期性外部驱动的情况下，利用半导体微腔中固有的非相干增益和耗散通道，在耦合激子-极化激元凝聚体中实现时间晶体的可能性。

Method: 给出了描述该过程的完整量子理论，该理论在平均场（mean-field）水平恢复已知的有效理论。通过解析方法确定平均场相图，结合数值分岔图分析时间晶体相与稳态相之间的转变，并运用Bogoliubov微扰理论（Bogoliubov perturbation theory）评估领头阶量子修正。

Result: 时间晶体相的出现要求Kerr非线性（Kerr nonlinearity）与非线性耗散之比超过√(5/4)。在该区域内，粒子数的周期性振荡形成与初始条件无关的吸引子（attractor）。数值分岔图与解析结果高度吻合。量子修正保持周期性且远小于平均场背景，证实时间晶体的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 耦合激子-极化激元凝聚体可以在无外部周期驱动条件下自发形成时间晶体，该相在宽参数范围内对量子涨落具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that time crystals can emerge in coupled exciton-polariton condensates without periodic external driving, enabled instead by incoherent gain and dissipation channels inherent to semiconductor microcavities. We present a full quantum description of these processes that recovers the established effective theory at the mean-field level. We analytically determine the mean-field phase diagram for the time-crystalline phase and find that its emergence requires the ratio of Kerr nonlinearity to nonlinear dissipation to exceed $\sqrt{5/4}$. Within this regime, the periodic oscillation of the particle numbers forms an attractor that is insensitive to the initial conditions. Numerical bifurcation diagrams reveal transitions between the time-crystalline phase and various steady phases, in excellent agreement with the analytical results. Using Bogoliubov perturbation theory, we evaluate the leading-order quantum corrections and find that, over a wide parameter range, these corrections remain periodic and much smaller than the mean-field background, thereby establishing the robustness of the time crystal.

### [129] [Revealing Hidden Correlations in a Fermi-Hubbard system via Interaction Ramps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14909)
*Botond Oreg,Carter Turnbaugh,Jens Hertkorn,Ningyuan Jia,Martin Zwierlein*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在冷原子实现的有吸引哈伯德模型（attractive Hubbard model）中，通过快速提升相互作用强度，观测到电荷密度波关联（charge-density-wave correlations）的增强信号，并利用自旋-电荷关联分析区分了未配对的费米液体（Fermi liquid）与预配对形成的赝能隙相（pseudogap phase）。该方法有望用于观测自旋不平衡系统中的奇异配对序及掺杂排斥哈伯德模型中的条纹序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在强关联体系中如何通过快速调控相互作用强度来增强并观测电荷密度波关联，特别是区分费米液体与预配对赝能隙相的微观机制。

Method: 在冷原子实现的有吸引哈伯德模型中，快速提升相互作用强度（interaction boost），将非局域对（nonlocal pairs）结合为双占据态（doublons），从而标记原来对的质心。通过分析升阶后的原子分辨自旋-电荷关联（atom-resolved spin-charge correlations），区分未配对的费米液体与预配对形成的赝能隙相。

Result: 观测到电荷密度波关联的增强能见度（enhanced visibility）。增强效应在配对呈现非局域性的强关联区域（strongly correlated regime）最为显著。

Conclusion: 该技术可能促进在自旋不平衡系统中观测奇异配对序（exotic pair order），以及在掺杂排斥哈伯德模型（doped repulsive Hubbard model）的对偶情况下观测条纹序（stripe order）。

Abstract: We observe an enhanced visibility of charge-density-wave correlations in a cold-atom realization of the attractive Hubbard model following a rapid boost of the interaction strength. The interaction boost associates nonlocal pairs into doublons which mark the center of mass of the original pairs. The enhancement is largest in the strongly correlated regime where pairing is nonlocal. We distinguish the unpaired Fermi liquid from the pseudogap phase of preformed pairs by analyzing atom-resolved spin-charge correlations after the ramp. The technique we establish here may facilitate the observation of exotic forms of pair order in spin-imbalanced systems, and of stripe order in the dual case of the doped repulsive Hubbard model.

</details>


### [130] [Larkin-Ovchinnikov-Fulde-Ferrell state of spin polarized atomic Fermi superfluid on a spherical surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14985)
*Yan He,Chih-Chun Chien*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 通过在薄球壳几何中实现 Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) 形式论，研究了自旋极化原子费米气体中的 LOFF 态，发现其仅存在于均匀解消失的相边界附近，且高自旋极化下多节点 LOFF 态更稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在紧致球壳几何中表征 Larkin-Ovchinnikov-Fulde-Ferrell (LOFF) 态的行为，并探索有限几何对自旋极化费米超流相图的影响。

Method: 采用 Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) 形式论，对薄球壳中具有配对相互作用的粒子数不平衡原子费米气体进行数值求解，构建相图并比较不同解（均匀解与 LOFF 解）的巨势（grand potential）。

Result: 均匀自旋极化费米超流解在序参量（order parameter）为零时消失；LOFF 态在相边界附近作为收敛解存在；高自旋极化下多节点（multiple nodes）LOFF 态在能量上更有利；但 LOFF 态仅在均匀解消失的相边界附近存活，显示出球面上的脆弱性。

Conclusion: LOFF 态在球形表面上仅在相边界附近稳定存在，且高自旋极化利于多节点 LOFF 态，表明紧致几何对非均匀超流相有显著限制作用。

Abstract: By implementing the Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) formalism of population-imbalanced atomic Fermi gases with pairing interactions in a thin spherical shell, we characterize the Larkin-Ovchinnikov-Fulde-Ferrell (LOFF) state in such a compact geometry. We first construct a phase diagram showing where uniform solutions of spin-polarized Fermi superfluid from the BdG equation cease to exist due to the vanishing order parameter. Near the boundary, various LOFF states with spatially modulating order parameters and density profiles can survive as convergent solutions to the BdG equation. When both uniform and LOFF solutions are present, we compare their grand potentials to determine the energetically favorable state and find that the LOFF states with multiple nodes in the order parameter become more stable at higher spin polarization. However, the LOFF state only survives close to the phase boundary where the uniform solutions vanish, indicating fragility of the LOFF state on a spherical surface. We also briefly discuss possible implications.

### [131] [Quantum Monte Carlo fermion spectroscopy of a non-compact CP$^1$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13945)
*Xu Zhang,Nick Bultinck*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过量子蒙特卡洛模拟研究了无hedgehog缺陷的电子-反铁磁自旋涨落耦合模型，发现该系统可实现非紧致CP¹理论中退禁闭U(1)规范场的物理，并揭示了电子能隙与平均场色散关系的相似性，同时完整保留了平移和自旋旋转对称性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用量子蒙特卡洛（Quantum Monte Carlo）方法，在双层正方晶格上模拟一个hedgehog缺陷被抑制的电子-玻色子模型，并将玻色子部分与非紧致CP¹理论（non-compact CP¹ theory）中的退禁闭U(1)规范场（deconfined U(1) gauge field）联系起来，再通过强耦合将玻色子与费米子自旋耦合。

Result: 在半填充绝缘体上，存在无能隙光子涨落（gapless photon fluctuations）的情况下，电子能隙（electron gap）的色散关系与电子在反铁磁自旋背景中的平均场色散（mean-field dispersion）高度相似；同时系统完整保留了平移对称性（translation symmetry）和自旋旋转对称性（spin rotation symmetry）。

Abstract: We study a model describing electrons coupled to anti-ferromagnetic spin fluctuations, and consider the situation where hedgehog defects in the order parameter field are suppressed. Without hedgehogs, the bosonic sector of the theory can be taken to realize the physics of the non-compact CP$^1$ theory with a deconfined U$(1)$ gauge field. After strongly coupling the boson to fermion spins, we simulate the single-particle spectral properties of a hedgehog-suppressed electron-boson model defined on a bilayer square lattice with Quantum Monte Carlo, and interpret the results in terms of an effective theory with fractionalized spinon and chargon excitations. As one of our main results we show that the electron gap on top of the half-filled insulator with gapless photon fluctuations closely resembles the mean-field dispersion of an electron in an anti-ferromagnetic spin background, even though the system fully preserves both the translation and spin rotation symmetry. Finally, we discuss potential implications of our results for the high-temperature superconductors.

### [132] [Corner Charge Fluctuations in Higher Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13971)
*Xiao-Chuan Wu,Pok Man Tam,Xuyang Liang,Zenan Liu,Dao-Xin Yao,Zheng Yan,Shinsei Ryu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统地将二维空间中电荷涨落（charge fluctuations）的角贡献（corner contribution）分析框架推广到高维，推导了三维三面角（trihedral corners）的普适角度依赖关系，并通过O(3)量子临界点（quantum critical point）的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟验证了预测。此外，识别出一种直接探测量子度量（quantum metric）的楔形角（wedge-corner）贡献，并给出了任意维数平行多面体（parallelotopes）多面体角（polyhedral corners）的角度函数，阐明了角贡献在不同物质相中的标度行为，揭示了金属相特有的奇偶维数效应（even-odd dimensional effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量子区域内电荷涨落是探测量子多体系统（quantum many-body systems）的有力手段。在二维中，角贡献（corner contribution）的形状依赖编码了量子临界点（quantum critical points）的普适数据，并揭示了各种量子相中量子几何（quantum geometry）的可观测量。本文旨在将此框架系统性地扩展到更高维度。

Method: 在三维中，推导了与一般平行六面体（parallelepiped）的三面角（trihedral corners）相关的普适角度依赖关系，并利用O(3)量子临界点（quantum critical point）的晶格模型蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行基准验证。进一步识别出楔形角（wedge-corner）贡献以直接探测量子度量（quantum metric），并通过晶格外尔半金属模型（lattice Weyl semimetal model）的数值结果加以支持。更一般地，推导了任意维数平行多面体（parallelotopes）多面体角（polyhedral corners）的角度函数，并阐明了角贡献在不同物质相中的标度行为。

Result: 在三维情况下，推导并验证了三面角的普适角度依赖关系；识别了楔形角贡献与量子度量的直接联系，并在外尔半金属模型中获得了数值支持。在任意维数下，得到了平行多面体多面体角的普适角度函数。绝缘体（insulators）和共形临界点（conformal critical points）在不同维数间表现出相似行为，而金属（metals）则展现出特征性的奇偶维数效应（even-odd dimensional effect）。

Conclusion: 本文成功地将电荷涨落的角贡献分析框架从二维推广至更高维，为研究量子多体系统在不同维数下的普适行为提供了新的理论工具。特别是，楔形角贡献为直接探测量子度量（quantum metric）提供了新的途径，而金属相的奇偶维数效应则揭示了不同维数下物质相的本质差异。

Abstract: Measuring charge fluctuations within a subregion provides a powerful probe of quantum many-body systems. In two spatial dimensions, the shape dependence of the dimensionless corner contribution encodes universal data of quantum critical points and reveals observables of quantum geometry in various quantum phases. Here, we systematically extend this framework to higher dimensions. In three dimensions, we derive the universal angle dependence associated with trihedral corners of a generic parallelepiped and benchmark the predictions against Monte Carlo simulations of lattice models at the O(3) quantum critical point. We further identify a wedge-corner contribution that directly probes the quantum metric, supported by numerical results for a lattice Weyl semimetal model. More generally, we obtain angle functions for polyhedral corners of arbitrary parallelotopes in general dimensions and clarify the scaling of the corner contribution across phases of matter. While insulators and conformal critical points exhibit similar behavior across dimensions, metals display a characteristic even-odd dimensional effect.

</details>


### [133] [Generalized Model Fractional Quantum Hall States on Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13978)
*Guangyue Ji,Jie Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过解析与数值相结合的方法，系统构造了Laughlin、Moore-Read以及一般Z_k Read-Rezayi系列的晶格模型态（lattice model states），这些态具备理想化的能量与纠缠特征，并在聚类行为上区别于连续统对应态，为理解拓扑有序相稳定性及晶格上共形希尔伯特空间的组织原理提供了新见解，同时对冷原子与合成平带平台有直接意义。

Method: 通过结合解析（analytical）与数值（numerical）方法，系统构造了Laughlin、Moore-Read以及一般Z_k Read-Rezayi系列的晶格模型态，并分析了其能量、纠缠特征及聚类（clustering）行为。

Result: 所构造的晶格特定态（lattice-specific states）具有理想化的能量与纠缠特征，并在聚类行为上与连续统对应态（continuum counterparts）存在显著区别。

Conclusion: 该理论推进了对拓扑有序相（topologically ordered phases）稳定性的理解，揭示了晶格上共形希尔伯特空间（conformal Hilbert space）的组织原理，并为在密度相互作用中工程化拓扑序及研究晶格特定激发提供了可行路径，对冷原子与合成平带平台具有直接应用潜力。

Abstract: Model wave functions are essential for studying fractional quantum Hall phases, yet lattice model states have so far been limited to bosonic systems with on-site interactions. In this work, by combining analytical and numerical methods, we systematically construct lattice model states for the Laughlin, Moore--Read, and general $\mathbb{Z}_k$ Read--Rezayi series. Our lattice-specific states are characterized by their idealized energy and entanglement features and are distinguished from their continuum counterparts by a modified clustering behavior. Our theory advances the understanding of the stability of topologically ordered phases and illustrates the organizing principles of the conformal Hilbert space on lattices. Practically, this work paves the way for further studying lattice-specific excitations and offers a constructive route for engineering topological orders within density interactions, with potential immediate implications for cold-atom and synthetic flat-band platforms.

In this work, we directly observed chiral magnons in the altermagnetic prototype MnTe using polarized inelastic neutron scattering. Furthermore, the magnon chirality was found to be reversibly switched by magnetic-field control, establishing a robust foundation for functional altermagnetic magnonics.

Abstract: The quest for efficient devices has fueled research in thermoelectric materials. In these materials, the goal is to maximize the Figure of Merit $ZT$. One of the components of this quantity is the Seebeck coefficient, which measures the voltage generated in response to a temperature gradient. Recent studies have revealed that strong electronic correlations can enhance the Seebeck coefficient, leading to anomalous behavior near half-filling. However, the impact of interactions beyond the on-site Hubbard remains mostly unexplored. We also show that the anomalous behavior is connected to a gap opening in the ground state. Moreover, electron-phonon coupling also lead to a Seebeck anomaly, even without on-site repulsion. We connect these changes of sign in the Seebeck coefficient with a restructuring of the Fermi surface and a change in its topology, an effect commonly seen in cuprates.

Method: 对最优掺杂 YBCO（YBa₂Cu₃O_y, y=6.94, T_c=92 K）采用宽带（0.16–4.1 eV, 约 100 fs）和近单周期（6 fs）瞬态反射光谱（transient reflectivity spectroscopy）进行观测。

Result: 在数飞秒内，增强的电子-电子 Umklapp 散射占主导，表明 eV 尺度上长程库仑相互作用的瞬态调制；随后，与自旋涨落修饰的载流子相关的中红外吸收散射率被快速抑制，该过程发生在约 90 fs 的时间尺度上，对应于光学能隙的倒数。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了铜氧化物中准粒子产生背后的关联多体动力学（correlated many-body dynamics），并为非常规配对机制提供了进一步线索。

Abstract: Understanding how quasiparticles are generated following a rapid quench of superconductivity in high-Tc cuprates is a key unresolved problem in nonequilibrium superconductivity. Here we resolve these processes in optimally doped YBCO [YBa2Cu3Oy(y=6.94, Tc=92 K)] using broadband (0.16 -4.1 eV, ca. 100 fs) and nearly single-cycle (6 fs) transient reflectivity spectroscopy. We show that within a few femtosecond, enhanced electron-electron Umklapp scattering dominates, signaling a transient modulation of long-range Coulomb interactions on the eV scale. This regime is followed by a rapid suppression of the scattering rate of the mid-infrared absorption associated with carriers dressed by spin fluctuations. We attribute this observation to an ultrafast decoupling of quasiparticles from the spin-fluctuation background, occurring on a 90 fs timescale set by the inverse optical gap. These findings reveal the correlated many-body dynamics underlying quasiparticle generation in cuprates and provide further clues for unconventional pairing mechanism.

### [137] [Strong electron correlations and ligand hybridization for altermagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14248)
*Byungkyun Kang,Anderson Janotti,Dai Q. Ho,Myoung-Hwan Kim,Chul Hong Park,Sangkook Choi,Mark R. Pederson,Eunja Kim*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用最先进的量子多体框架（quantum many-body frameworks），对三种代表性候选材料——MnF₂、MnTe 和 RuO₂——进行电子结构的解构与分析。

Conclusion: 强局域电子关联和通过配体选择促进轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）是实现强关联体系中交变磁（altermagnetism）的关键前提，为合理设计和发现新型交变磁材料提供了指导。

Abstract: Spin-band splitting is a hallmark of altermagnetism, intrinsically linked to magnetic ordering driven by electron correlations. However, recent inconsistencies in the detection of altermagnetism in strongly correlated altermagnet candidates have cast doubt on the robustness of this phenomenon and its dependence on many-body effects. Here, using state-of-the-art quantum many-body frameworks, we dissect the electronic origins of altermagnetism in three prototypical candidates: MnF$_2$, MnTe, and RuO$_2$. In MnF$_2$, we identify pronounced local electron correlations within Mn-3$d$ states and uncover a distinct Mott gap in the visible range, rooted in nonlocal screening effects. The strong correlations markedly localize the Mn-3$d$ electrons, leading to a narrowing of the spin-resolved bandwidth and, consequently, a suppression of spin-band splitting. By contrast, MnTe provides an ideal platform for altermagnetism, exhibiting substantial local Mn-3$d$ magnetic moments due to the strong correlations and pronounced spin-band splitting, enabled by robust Mn 3$d$--Te-5$p$ orbital hybridization. RuO$_2$ manifests as a Pauli paramagnet with vanishing local moments, even in its antiferromagnetic phase. Nonetheless, it exhibits significant spin-band splitting, indicative of itinerant altermagnetic behavior. Our results reveal that both strong local electron correlations and judicious ligand selection to promote orbital hybridization are key prerequisites to realizing altermagnetism in strongly correlated systems. These insights pave the way for the rational design and discovery of novel altermagnetic materials.

Our results agree with the experimental data.The calculation shows that the 4f electrons in all these phases are well localized, the Kondo peaks are suppressed and the hybridization between the 4f electrons and conduction electrons are quite weak. Our results also show the strong correlation effect is significant in Sm metal.

### [139] [Non-Invertible Symmetries on Tensor-Product Hilbert Spaces and Quantum Cellular Automata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15194)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先基于缺陷（defects）的物理假设，证明 QCA 精炼实现中 QCA 和对称性算符的指标由范畴数据决定（仅存在重新定义对称性算符的自由度）；随后针对任意弱整融合范畴对称性，在张量积希尔伯特空间上显式构造了 QCA 精炼晶格模型，并计算了其中 QCA 的指标。

Result: 证明了在给定物理假设下 QCA 与对称性算符指标完全由范畴数据确定；构建了适用于任意弱整融合范畴对称性的 QCA 精炼晶格模型；模型中的 QCA 指标与理论推导一致。

Abstract: We investigate realizations of (1+1)-dimensional fusion category symmetries on tensor-product Hilbert spaces, allowing for mixing with quantum cellular automata (QCAs). It was argued recently that any such realizable symmetry must be weakly integral. We develop a systematic analysis of QCA-refined realizations of fusion categories and prove two statements. First, we show that, under certain physical assumptions on defects, any QCA-refined realization has QCA and symmetry-operator indices determined by the categorical data, up to the freedom of redefining the symmetry operators. Second, we construct a lattice model that provides a QCA-refined realization for any weakly integral fusion category symmetry on a tensor product Hilbert space. We also compute indices of the QCAs in our lattice model and show agreement with the first result. ### [140] [On the Symmetries of Anisotropic Spin Interaction Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14969)
*Arist Zhenyuan Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出扭曲自旋空间群（twisted spin-space group, tSSG）理论，指出各向异性自旋相互作用并非简单地破缺自旋空间群（SSG）对称性，而是通过上同调不变量（cohomology invariants）将其扭曲，从而产生超出 $O(3)\times \operatorname{Isom}(\mathbb{R}^3)$ 子群的新对称类。基于该理论，在一个自旋-1模型中发现了定义在自旋布里渊克莱因瓶（Klein-bottle）而非传统环面（torus）上的拓扑四极激发，其玻色型BdG哈密顿量满足滑移反射缝合关系（glide reflection sewing relation），能带谱呈现莫比乌斯边界态（Möbius boundary states），并由 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 拓扑不变量分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论认为各向异性自旋相互作用仅破缺自旋空间群（spin-space group, SSG）对称性，但未考虑其可能通过上同调不变量（cohomology invariants）扭曲对称性结构，从而遗漏了超出 $O(3)\times \operatorname{Isom}(\mathbb{R}^3)$ 子群的新对称类。

Method: 首先重新定义自旋-only群（spin-only group）$S_0$ 为纯自旋旋转（proper spin rotations），进而提出扭曲自旋空间群（twisted SSG, tSSG）理论以完整刻画自旋空间对称性；并采用线性味道波理论（linear flavor wave theory, LFWT）研究具有tSSG对称性的自旋-1模型。

Result: 在自旋-1模型中，拓扑四极激发（topological quadrupolar excitations）定义在自旋布里渊克莱因瓶（spin Brillouin Klein-bottle）而非传统环面（torus）上。玻色型BdG哈密顿量满足滑移反射缝合关系（glide reflection sewing relation），能带谱呈现莫比乌斯边界态（Möbius boundary states），这些拓扑激发由 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 拓扑不变量分类，源于克莱因瓶的不可定向性（nonorientability）。

Conclusion: 各向异性自旋相互作用可通过上同调不变量扭曲自旋空间群对称性，形成tSSG这一更广泛的对称性框架；该理论预言了非传统拓扑激发态，为探索基于自旋空间群之外的新型对称性拓扑物态提供了新途径。

Abstract: We show that anisotropic spin interactions do not merely break spin-space group (SSG) symmetries, but instead twist them through cohomology invariants, yielding symmetry classes beyond subgroups of $O(3)\times \operatorname{Isom}(\mathbb{R}^3) $. This requires redefining the spin-only group $S_0$ in terms of proper spin rotations. Based on this unitary $S_0$, we formulate a twisted SSG (tSSG) theory that captures the complete set of spin-space symmetries. We then study a spin-1 model with tSSG symmetry using linear flavor wave theory and find topological quadrupolar excitations defined on a spin Brillouin Klein-bottle rather than the conventional torus. Specifically, the bosonic BdG Hamiltonian satisfies a glide reflection sewing relation, the ribbon spectrum exhibits Möbius boundary states. These topological excitations are classified by $ \mathbb{Z}_2 $, enforced by the nonorientability of the Klein-bottle.

</details>


### [141] [Quantum criticality in the two-dimensional Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15059)
*Mathias Pelz,Gabriel Kotliar,Jan von Delft,Andreas Gleis*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用动力学簇近似（dynamical cluster approximation）结合数值重整化群（numerical renormalization group）作为簇求解器，在接近零温下研究了正方格子Hubbard模型的正常态掺杂驱动相图。在铜氧化物超导体相关参数区域（U=7t, t'=-0.3t）中，发现了一个临界掺杂浓度p*，标志着赝能隙金属（pseudogap metal）与正常费米液体（normal Fermi liquid）之间连续的量子相变。该相变通过从两侧连续塌缩的费米液体尺度被识别，并在p*处产生一个可延伸至任意低能标的非费米液体（non-Fermi-liquid）区域。穿越p*时，反节点区（antinodal region）的低能相干谱权重消失并被窄金属性赝能隙取代，而节点区（nodal region）平滑演化并保持相对相干，从而在赝能隙金属中产生费米弧（Fermi arcs）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Hubbard模型中赝能隙相（pseudogap phase）与费米液体相之间的量子相变本质，尤其是该相变是否为连续相变及其与掺杂浓度的关系。该研究在铜氧化物超导体的参数区域内进行，旨在揭示赝能隙态与正常费米液体之间的相变机制。

Method: 采用动力学簇近似（dynamical cluster approximation, DCA）结合数值重整化群（numerical renormalization group, NRG）作为簇求解器，该方法可直接获取接近零温下实频率（real-frequency）动力学信息。计算在铜氧化物相关参数区域（U=7t, t'=-0.3t）的正方格子Hubbard模型上进行，通过提取电荷、自旋和d波配对磁化率中的费米液体尺度来识别相变。

Result: 发现临界掺杂浓度p*标志着赝能隙金属与正常费米液体之间的连续量子相变。费米液体尺度从两侧连续塌缩，在p*处产生一个延伸至任意低能标的非费米液体区域。穿越p*时，反节点区的低能相干谱权重消失并被窄金属性赝能隙取代，节点区则平滑演化，导致赝能隙金属中出现费米弧。

Conclusion: 正方格子Hubbard模型中赝能隙金属与正常费米液体之间存在一个由掺杂浓度驱动的连续量子相变，该相变在反节点区和节点区表现出截然不同的电子结构演化行为，并在临界掺杂处产生非费米液体行为。

Abstract: We study the normal-state, doping-driven phase diagram of the square-lattice Hubbard model using the dynamical cluster approximation combined with the numerical renormalization group as a cluster solver, which gives direct access to real-frequency dynamics at essentially zero temperature. In a parameter regime relevant for cuprates, $U=7t$ and $t'=-0.3t$, we find a critical doping $p^{\ast}$ that marks a continuous quantum phase transition between a pseudogap metal and a normal Fermi liquid. The transition is identified by a continuous collapse, from both sides, of the Fermi-liquid scale extracted from charge, spin, and $d_{x^2-y^2}$-wave pairing susceptibilities. This collapse produces a non-Fermi-liquid regime at intermediate energy scales, which appears to extend to arbitrarily low scales at $p^{\ast}$. As $p^{\ast}$ is crossed from the normal Fermi liquid at $p>p^{\ast}$ into the pseudogap metal at $p<p^{\ast}$, the coherent low-energy spectral weight in the antinodal region is lost and replaced by a narrow, metallic pseudogap, while the nodal region evolves smoothly and remains comparatively coherent. This gives rise to Fermi arcs in the pseudogap metal at $p<p^{\ast}$, since the zero-frequency spectral weight remains large in the nodal region but is strongly suppressed in the antinodal region.

</details>
